 jñāninaḥ ye atra vipanna dṛṣṭyā bhāveṣu ca āsakti mahā grahāṇām vaśena grastā hi praṇaṣṭa prajñā nāgārjuna ādīn  ca mahā mahimnaḥ kṣipanti tena ātma vināśa eva teṣām mahābhūta graha upaśāntyai prārabhyate poṣa karaḥ  abhyupāyaḥ kāruṇyam āśritya mayā adhūnā atra bhāva abhiniveśa eva tāvat  samasta saṅkleśa jāla mūlam atas tad parihṛtya niḥśreyasa pada abhilāṣiṇām sarva dharma niḥsvabhāva tā vyutpādana artham idam ārabhyate parama artha gambhīra udadhinayam anavagāhya atra kecid āhuḥ yukti āgamābhyām sarva dharma niḥsvabhāva tā sidhyati iti ced  na āgamaḥ tāvat śaktaḥ kena api tathā abhyupagama abhāvāt  vivakṣā adhīna tvāt  vacanānām tad vastu sambandha abhāvāt ca na prāmāṇyam syāt api sambandhaḥ tathā api arvāk darśibhiḥ avadhārayitum na śakyate prekṣakāḥ tad pravacanam ata mabhyupagamyamānebhyaḥ  api niḥsaṃśayam sarva bhāvānām niḥsvabhāvatā pratipādakam kim api vacanam upadarśayitum na śaknuvanti sūtreṣu keṣucid  aniḥsvabhāvāḥ sarva dharmāḥ anutpannāḥ ādiśāntāḥ prakṛti parinirvṛtā ityādīni vacanāni āgacchanti tāni api neyārthāni eva veditavyāni nānā abhisandhi dvāreṇa bhagavataḥ  deśanayā avatāraṇāt  trayāṇām svabhāvānām parikalpita paratantra pariniṣpannānām kramaśas  lakṣaṇata utpattitaḥ paramārthataḥ niḥsvabhāva tām sandhāya sarva dharmā niḥsvabhāvā uktāḥ tena niḥsvabhāva tvāt anutpannā tatas  ādiśāntāḥ tena prakṛti parinirvṛtāḥ tathā eva bhagavatā ārya sandhi nirmocana sūtra ādau sūtra artha abhiprāya yogaḥ  deśitaḥ dvaita abhāsi vijñāna mātreṇa sarva dharmāṇām utpatti ādayaḥ  vibhajyante na tu sva saṃvedana mātreṇa dvaita ābhāsaḥ  api mithyā tena sarva bhāvā api mṛṣā eva vyavasthāpyante parikalpitasya lakṣaṇa niḥsvabhāva tvāt sarva dharma anutpāda āt ayaḥ  deśitāḥ na tu paramārthataḥ atas  na āgama dvārā sarva dharma niḥsvabhāva tā sādhayitum śakyate na api yukti dvārā na khalu sarve bhāvāḥ pratyakṣata evam viviktāḥ śūnyāḥ anubhūyante vastu tvāt tasya viṣayāṇām abhāvāya tāvat  nīrūpa tayā na katham api svarūpa upadarśanena vijñāna janaka tvam yujyate janaka tve sati vastutva prasaṅgaḥ artha kriyā samarthya tvāt  vastu lakṣaṇasya yad  pratyakṣam tad api yadi sa svabhāvam tadā sarva dharma niḥsvabhāvatā pratijñāyā hāni prasaṅgaḥ yadi tad niḥsvabhāvam katham tena sarva dharmāṇām viviktatā anubhūyate atha kaiścid  artha antarā viviktatā iti pakṣaḥ  gṛhyate tadā itareṇa tāvat  pratyakṣeṇa śūnyatā grāhyā syāt  sarva dharmaḥ svabhāva vādiṣu ye kecana dharmāḥ pratyakṣeṇa upalabhyante te sarve dharmā viviktāḥ pratīyeran sarva dharmāṇām svabhāva vivikta tā tāvat na asti kim api vastu tasyāḥ  api sarva dharma antargata tvāt na ced antarbhāvaḥ sva pratijñā hāniḥ ayam tāvat  viṣayaḥ sarvajña ādīnām yoginām pratyakṣeṇa sugamya iti ucyamāne api na khalu vidvadbhyaḥ tṛptim āsādayati yukti abhāvāt tatra yadi tad  yogi jñānam api asat iti ced  tadā katham tasya prāmāṇyam yadi tad  sat  tadā pratijñāhāniḥ na api anumānena api asarve bhāvāḥ śūnyāḥ iti sādhayitum śakyate kasya api ādhārasya dharmiṇa eva abhāvāt hetu dṛṣṭānta ādīnām api anupapanna tvāt svabhāva āśraya rahitaiḥ sarva hetubhiḥ katham sarva dharma niḥsvabhāva tā sādhayitum śakyate paraiḥ siddha tvāt  para abhyupagata hetu ādibhiḥ sva pakṣaḥ prasidhyet iti ced  tadā api na yujyate sādhana dūṣaṇayā uḥ ubhaya prasiddha tvena abhimata tvāt  itham yadā para abhyupagata hetvādayaḥ  yadi na vāstavikāḥ mohena kalpita mātra sattākāḥ tadā katham taiḥ sva pakṣaḥ prasidhyet  yadi te bhāva rupeṇa sanmātrāḥ tadā na kevalam te para prasiddha mātrāḥ tava api tad prasiddha tvāt  bhāvānām siddhaya siddhayaḥ  na puruṣa vivakṣā adhīnāḥ para abhyupagata sādha nāt ayaḥ  yadi sat mātrā eva abhyupeyante tadā bhāvā api sa svabhāvāḥ katham na abhyupeyante sarva dharma śūnyatā kutra api kena api hetunā na sambaddhā atyanta parokṣa tvāt yadi sambandhaḥ siddhaḥ syāt  tadā sarve tattva darśinaḥ syuḥ iti prasaṅgaḥ pūrvata eva siddha tvāt  yukti anusaraṇam api nirarthakam syāt  api ca na tāvat  kārya svabhāva liṅgābhyām śakyate sādhayitum sarva dharma niḥsvabhāva tā teṣām khalu bhāva sādhana tvāt  tvad mate tu etau kārya svabhāvau na sambhavataḥ tathā hi sarveṣām dharmāṇām anutpanna tvena kasya api kena api saha kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya anabhyupeta tvāt kārya hetuḥ tāvat na sambhavati sarva dharmāṇām niḥsvabhāva tvena kasya api ātmanaḥ svabhāvasya asattvāt kutas tāvat  svabhāva hetuḥ anupalabdhiḥ api tām sādhayitum na śaktā svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ yā khalu asat vyavahāram sādhayati sā tad itara viviktasya vastunaḥ pratyakṣataḥ pratītau satyām api asat śāstra śravaṇa vimūḍha manasā kenacid  tad itara viveka vyavahāre apravṛttānām tad vyavahāra prasādhanāya prayujyata iti tava tu sādhya māna sarva dharma abhāva vyavahārasya pratyakṣataḥ jñāna artham kiñcid api na asti eva sva pakṣa hāni prasaṅgāt iti ukta pūrvam viruddha upalabdhi ādayaḥ  api tava mate abhāva sādhana artham na sambhavanti eva atyanta parokṣāt  sarva dharma vivekāt saha anavasthāna virodhena api na kiñcid api sidhyati yadi sidhyet  tadā tad viruddhāt ayaḥ  bhāva tvena eva sidhyeyuḥ iti anabhyupetā na syuḥ bhāvānām virodhaḥ  dvidhā vyavasthāpyate tad yathā saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇaḥ paraspara parihāra lakṣaṇaḥ ca ye tatra avikala kāraṇāni tebhyaḥ  niyatam yasmin  bhavati tayoḥ prathamaḥ  virodhaḥ  vyavasthāpyate śīta uṣṇa sparśavat yad  yasmin parihriyate yad na vicchidyate tayoḥ ubhayoḥ abhāvayoḥ dvitīyaḥ  virodhaḥ  vyavasthāpyate ekasmin dharmiṇi yugapad  sat asattvavat tathāvidhau dvau  api virodhau sarva dharma aniḥsvabhāva vādiṣu na eva sambhavataḥ gagana aravinda ādiṣu na santi avikala kāraṇāni api tathā na asti atad vyāvṛttyā paricchedaḥ  api bhāva paryantavāt  sattā vyavacchena yadi api paricchedaḥ  vyavasthāpyate tathā api kutracid  kācid  sattā vyavacchinnā sidhyet  kintu bhavantaḥ tāvat  kutra api kasya api vyavacchedam katham api na eva abhyupagacchanti yadi sarve dharmā niḥsvabhāvatā pratyāsannāḥ tadā yuṣmāsu kim api avikala kāraṇa sattvam na sidhyet  yadi sidhyet tadā tāni avikala kāraṇāni eva bhāvāḥ sidhyeyuḥ yadi sarva dharma niḥsvabhāva tā vyavacchedana kecana bhāvāḥ paricchidyante tadā ta eva asmāsu vastu santaḥ sidhyeyuḥ tad viruddha upalabdhi asambhavāt yadi asambhavaḥ tadā vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhi ādayaḥ  api na sambhaveyuḥ viruddha upalabdhi asiddheḥ tā api na sambhavanti viruddha upalabdhi prabhāvita tvāt tāsām vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ api vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva siddhau vyāpya niṣedhāya yadi prayujyate tadā sarva dharma svabhāva śūnya tvam tu tāvat na kasya api vyāpyam sidhyati iti yadi sidhyati iti ced  tad  vyāpyam eva hi vastu tayā siddham syāt  kāraṇa anupalabdhiḥ api kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhau kāryatva niṣedhāya yadi prayujyate tadā sarva dharma niḥsvabhāva tāyām tu kārya kāraṇa bhāva eva siddhaḥ  na bhavati yadi siddhaḥ tadā yad  kāraṇam yad ca api vā kāryam tad eva vastu syāt  sarva dharmeṣu kasya api ekasya niṣedhāt  eteṣām niḥsvabhāvatā siddhayartham na asti kim api ekam kāraṇam kena api īḥ cara ādi eka nimitta abhyupagama niṣedhe api na ime niḥsvabhāva tve sidhyanti sarveṣām sva nimitta utpanna tvāt eteṣām pratisvam nimittāni api niṣeddhum na śakyante teṣām prasiddha tvāt  api ca nairātmyam yadi sarva dharma gocara tāyām sādhyate tadā na dṛṣṭāntaḥ prasiddhayati pratibimbādayaḥ  ye api dṛṣṭāntāḥ teṣu api kecid  bāhya vastu svabhāvāḥ anye tāvat jñāna svabhāvā abhyupagamyante atas te vastu svabhāvā eva svīkṛtāḥ yadi prādeśikam nairātmyam sādhayitum iṣyeta tatra yadi tairthika parikalpitāḥ pradhāna ādayaḥ niṣidhyante tadā siddha sādhana mātram eva yadi loka prasiddhā rupādayaḥ tadā dṛṣṭānta eva tauvat na upalabhyate pratijñāyāḥ ca api pratyakṣa virodhaḥ yadi anumānasya pratibandha sādhana artham pratyakṣa pramāṇam abhayupagamyate tadā siddha eva tāvat  bhāvaḥ tad yathā kalpanā apoḍham abhra antam iti pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam abhrānta jñānena nirūpitaḥ  api bhāva svabhāvaḥ katham anumānena apahnotum śakyate yadi sa nirākriyate tadā pratyakṣasya eva bādha prasaṅgaḥ yadi sa badhyate tadā na anumānasya api sausthityam pratyakṣa sambandhāt anuprāpta anumānena api sa eva katham bādhayitum śakyate yadi pratyakṣa siddhaḥ  arthaḥ  na bādhyate tadā vastu vādinām eva sausthityam prāpyasya prāpta tvāt  api ca sarva dharma niḥsvabhāva tvam sādhayitu yadi kaścid  bhāva svabhāvaḥ  hetuḥ pradarśyate tadā viparīta sādhya sādhakaḥ  hetuḥ viroddhaḥ  bhavati yadi abhāva svabhāvaḥ tadā asat abhavayoḥ paraspara sambandhāa bhāvāt katham sādhayiṣyati yadi ubhaya svabhāvaḥ saḥ  api aniyata eva vipakṣe api sattvāt  yatas  hi tad  sādhayitum na anyat  kim api pramāṇam iti śabda mātrataḥ  api na tad  sidhyati sarvatas  sarva siddhi prasaṅgāt  śabdaḥ  api viruddhaḥ yatas  hi yadi niḥsvabhāvaḥ tadā katham sa siddhaḥ prasaṅga tvena siddhe api na iṣṭa artha siddhiḥ tathāvidha prasaṅgasya eva asiddhatvāt prasaṅgena tāvat  para pakṣaḥ  bādhayitum śakyate tathā api sva pakṣaḥ tu na sidhyati ubhaya siddha hetu antara apekṣa tvāt tasya svatas  na utpadyate bhāvaḥ yaḥ ca anutpannaḥ tasya asattvena kutra api hetu tvena anupapatteḥ utpannānām punar utpāde nairarthakyam vidyamāna tvāt  yadi aviśiṣṭaḥ tadā kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ  api na yujyate viśiṣṭasya eva hetu tvāt  paratas  api na utpadyate bhāvaḥ parasya eva asiddha tvāt api ca nitya bhūtāt api tāvat  parān na utpadyate nityasya krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā virodhāt anityāt api tāvat  vinaṣṭān na tasya avidyamāana tvāt avinaṣṭāt api na kārya kāraṇayoḥ tutva prasaṅgāt  sama kālikayoḥ tāvat  kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ  na yujyate niṣpannavasthāyām dvayoḥ vidyamāna svabhāva tvena paraspara upakārakatva abhāvāt aniṣpannavasthāyām tu dvayoḥ asattvāt  upakārakatva atyanta abhāvaḥ ubhayatas  api na utpadyate yathā ukta ubhaya doṣa prasaṅgāt  ekasmin dvitva virodhāt ca ahetutaḥ  api na utpadyate bhāvaḥ kādācid ka tvāt  na evam kathanam yujyate yad na svatas  na ubhayatas  na api vinaṣṭāt hetoḥ na apya hetutaḥ na abhīṣṭān nityāt hetoḥ kārya utpattiḥ bhavati iti tathā vādinaḥ tad sarvam yujyate kintu nitya tvena abhīṣṭāt tad itarādavinaṣṭāt hetoḥ kārya utpattau kaḥ tāvat  virodhaḥ kena hetunā tatas  kārya utpattiḥ niṣidhyate na asti tad bādhakam kim api pramāṇam para bhūtasya bhāva mātrasya api asiddhiḥ iti na yatas  hi yad anantaram kāryam utpadyate tad eva apara aḥ iti abhidhīyate kārya utpādāt  prāk  para iti na āmraḥ  asiddha tve api bhāvasya tu na eva hāniḥ kecid  para tvāt iti bādhakam pramāṇam vadanti tad api anaikāntikam eva parātva janaka tvayoḥ avirodhāt sa tau  avirodhana yaḥ  api niṣeddhum na śakyate atiprasaṅgāt  yadi evam asti tadā kasmiṃścid aparasmin drāri draya mūḍhatva ādi dharmāṇām dṛśya tvena paratva hetoḥ sarva jagat dāridraya ādi dharma upādānam syāt  avyavahitādavinaṣṭāt  parāt  kārya utpattau kārya kāraṇa sama kālikatva prasaṅgaḥ  bādhaka praṇam iti yadi kaścid evam manyate tad api ayuktam eva avyavahi kārya utpādena api kārya kāraṇa sama kālika tvam na prasajyate kṣaṇika tvena kārya sattve kāraṇasya asattvāt yadā kāryam utpadyate tadā eva kāraṇam nirudhyate tulā daṇḍa unnāma avanāmavat iti kutas  sama kālikatva prasaṅgaḥ kāraṇa avasthāyām api kāryasya vidyamāna tvāt  nairarthakyam eva yathā avyavahita vinaṣṭaḥ  bhāva uttarakṣaṇa bhāvinā bhāvena saha yugapad  vyavasthāpyaḥ  na bhavati evam eva kāryasya api tad sadṛśa tvāt aviruddha tā eva chāyā ātapavat  yathā ca pūrva apara avyavadhānena pravahamāna jala dhārāyām viṣaya eka tvam na bhavati tathā eva asya api tad sadṛśa tvāt  sama kālika tvam na bhaviṣyati vidyamānasya api kāryasya na eva utpādaḥ utpāda vaiyarthāt  na api avidyamānasya śaśaśṛṅgadīnām api utpatti prasaṅgāt  iti api kathanam na eva yujyate yadi vidyamāna kāryasya utpatti nirṣidhyate tadā tava pakṣe ubhaya siddhaḥ  hetuḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ ca na syātām yadi asti tadā niḥsvabhāvatva pratijñāyā hāniḥ sāṃkhya ādi parikalpita sat kārya vādaḥ  yadi api ayuktaḥ tathā api asatkārya utpāde kim nāma viruddha tvam kimartham ca tad niṣidhyate na eva ca syāt  śaśaśṛṅga ādi utpatti prasaṅgaḥ tad tathāvidha hetūnām abhāvāt anutpatteḥ na tu abhāvāt hetoḥ sarvatas  sarva utpatti prasaṅgaḥ  api na eva  kāraṇa pratiniyata sāmarthasya vyavasthita tvāt  pratiniyata kāraṇa sāmarthyam api aśyam abhyupeyam anyathā sāṃvṛtike api kārya kāraṇa bhāve katham na sarvatas  sarva utpattiḥ bhavati iti api ca yadi vinaṣṭa āvinaṣṭa ādayaḥ  vikalpāḥ pāramārthikīm utpattim bādhante tadā katham na sāṃvṛtikīm api bādhante vastu bala pravṛttasya hetoḥ viṣasya puruṣa icchā vaśena vibhāgaḥ  na yukta rūpaḥ yadi pati akṣa bādhitatva āśaṅkayā tasmin hetu tvam na pravartata iti ucyeta tarhi sa hetuḥ eva na asti bādha yogya tvāt  na hi ekena hetunā aneka kārya utpattiḥ yujyate na ca anekena api eka utpattiḥ yujyate anyathā hetu bhedena bhedaḥ  na syāt  ata eva na anekebhyaḥ  api aneka kārya utpattiḥ bhavati iti yadi ekam kāryam sarve hetovaḥ  abhinirvartayanti tadā bhinnānām hetūnām abhedaḥ syāt  anekebhyaḥ  ekaikasya utpatteḥ yadheka ekam na abhinirvartayanti tadā katham nāma anekebhyaḥ  aneka utpattiḥ api na hi ekena api ekasya utpattiḥ cakṣuḥ ādi indriyebhyaḥ tad vijñānasya utpatteḥ tad anantaram yadi sajātī ya kṣaṇa utpattiḥ na bhavet tadā sarveṣām andha badhiratva ādi prasaṅga iti api kathanam tāvat na eva yujyate evam yaḥ tāvat andha badhiratva ādi prasaṅgaḥ  abhihita sa na eva sambhavati anabhyupagata tvāt  sāmagryā utpatteḥ na hi kācid ekena ekasya utpattiḥ iti yena ekasmāt aneka utpattiḥ anekasmāt  vā ekasya utpattiḥ tatas  sa viruddhaḥ  hetu svabhāva atikrāntaḥ  janaka tvena anabhyupagataḥ  bhavati tathā api vidyamāna mātrāt aneka svabhāvāt pradīpa ādeḥ aneka svabhāvam kāryam utpadyamānam dṛśyate hetu bhedaḥ  bhedakaḥ  na bhaviṣyati iti na syāt  hetu viśeṣeṇa kārya viśeṣasya utpatteḥ hetu viśeṣeṇa kārya viśeṣa utpāda iti yad eva kathanam tad eva hetu bhedasya bhedakatva pratipādakam iti yaḥ pratītyasamutpannaḥ sa prakṛtyā śānta iti etad anaikāntika tvam pratītyasamutpannasya sa svabhāva tvena virodha abhāvāt pratītyasamupādasya sa svabhāva tve prasiddha tvāt  hetoḥ viruddha tvam api ajātānām khapuṣpa ādīnām sa svabhāva tvena ananubhūyamāna tvāt  yaḥ  hi paramārtha taḥ  asan sa saṃvṛtau  api svabhāvataḥ  anutpannaḥ  dṛśyate yathā vandhyā putraḥ tulye api niḥsvabhāva tve yathā rupādayaḥ avabhāsante tathā śaśa śṛṅga ādayaḥ katham na avabhāsante avabhāsa viśeṣasya asya na asti kim api kāraṇam asarve dharmā niḥsvabhāvāḥ eka aneka svabhāva rahita tvāt iti evam abhidadhānā ye prasaṅgam sādhayanti teṣām api tathā paraiḥ anaṅgīkārāt  hetuḥ asiddha eva eka aneka svabhāva rahita tvasya na kena api abhyupagata tvāt atas  svatas  siddhau  api hetuḥ ayam paratas  asiddhaḥ anyat ca sādhya sādhane paryudāsā ātmake prasajya ātmake vā yadi paryudāsā ātmake tadā eka aneka svabhāva rahitātvasya bhāva svabhāva tvena abhyupeta tvāt tad api anabhyupagatam na bhavet  yadi prasajya ātmake tadā na asti gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ tayoḥ niḥsvabhāva tvāt  anyaḥ  anya asambaddha tvāt  abhinna tvāt ca yad ca sarva abhilāpa viraha lakṣaṇam tad na kiñcid  gamyam gamakam vā yathā aśva śṛṅgam yathā ukta sādhya sādhane api sarva abhilāpa viraha lakṣaṇe yau hi anyaḥ  anya asambaddhau tayoḥ na asti gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ yathā vindhya hima ālayau sādhya sādhane ca api anyaḥ  anya asambaddhe yadi ubhe abhāva svabhāva tvena tādātmya lakṣaṇa āpanne eva iti manyase ced  tad api uktam tad ā ātmanaḥ  bhāve vyavasthita tvāt  yaḥ  yasmāt na bhinna svabhāvaḥ tayoḥ na asti gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ vṛkṣa drumavat  yathā ukta sādhya sādhane api na bhinna svabhāve na ayam kṛtakatva anitya tvābhyām anaikāntikaḥ  api vyāvṛttyā bhinna tvāt tayoḥ atra api vyāvṛttyā bheda iti manyate ced  tad api ayuktam yadi evam svād bhāva eva te syātām nīla pītavat  api ca yathā kena api eka aneka svabhāva viyuktatva hetunā bhāvānām niḥsvabhāva tā sādhyate tathā dharmiṇaḥ  api abhāvaḥ sādhyate tadā dharmi vyāvṛttatva siddheḥ hetuḥ viruddhaḥ syāt  tathā niḥsvabhāvatva siddhau na asti kim api pramāṇam api ca yadi vijñānam api anya dharmavat  paramārtha taḥ  niḥsvabhāvam syāt tadā tad anupādeyam syāt  vitatha tvāt anya dharmavat  yadi evam syāt tadā na syuḥ yoginaḥ  api na eva yogi jñānam api syāt na ca taiḥ tattva pratibodhaḥ syāt  na eva teṣām bhagavatām buddhānām apratiṣṭhita nirvāṇam syāt na ca sarva ākāram jñānam syāt  phalataḥ sarva vyavasthā vilopaḥ syāt iti saṃvṛtau yogi jñāna ādīnām abhyupagamāt  buddhā api viparyastā bhaveyuḥ iti prasaṅgaḥ api ca asti bhavatām sarva dharma niḥsvabhāvatva pratijñāyām yukti āgamābhyām virodhaḥ  api yathā rupādayaḥ tāvat  sa svabhāva tve eva niyatā deśa kāla avasthā bhedena sphuṭam avabhāsamāna tvāt  ata ādau tāvat  pratyakṣa virodhaḥ su spaṣṭaḥ agni ādayaḥ  ye bhāvāḥ parokṣarvena abhyupagatāḥ te api abhrāntena niyata dhūma ādi hetunā anumāna pramāṇena sat svabhāva ātmakā eva bhāvānām utpādaḥ  api khalu hetu pratyaya sāpekṣa eva siddhaḥ kādācid ka tvāt  ahetukasya tu kādācid ka tvam api na yujyate nirapekṣa tvāt  atas  pratijñāyām anumāna bādhā api yāni trāyastriṃśānām nagara ādīni atyanta parokṣāṇi tāni api samasta loka eka cakṣuḥ bhūtena tāyinā svakīyena anāvṛtena jñānacakṣuṣā pratyakṣīkṛtya anyebhyaḥ  api samprakāśitāni atas  viścasta āgamena sattāyāḥ siddheḥ āgama virodhaḥ  api asatām ākāśa puṣpa ādīnām tathā darśana samprakāśanayoḥ ayuktvāt  bhagavatā khalu ye āntara bahya vastūnām anekavidhāḥ pratītyasamutpādāḥ samupadiṣṭāḥ te api svabhāva virahitāḥ katham yujyante atyanta abhāvānām ākāśa puṣpa ādīnām na eva atyantikī utpattiḥ iti kuśala akuśala marmaṇām phala bhūtā deva naraka ādi gatayaḥ bhavanti iti svayambhuva upadeśāt  katham na virodhaḥ na eva yujyate atyanta asat bhūta kūrma roma ādibhiḥ vastra nirmāṇa upadeśaḥ atas  karmaṇā ām iṣṭa aniṣṭa phala apavādāt saṃkleśa pakṣa apavādaḥ sūtra ādiṣu āryāṇām mārga abhyāsa balena yā uttara uttara loka uttara jñāna phala vyavasthā sā api na syāt  gati gamya gamaka ādi abhāvāt śaśaśṛṅga kṛta sopāna mārge pādau nidhāya vandhyā putrasya aścaṅga samucchrita uttuṅga viśāla prāsāda ārohaṇam na sambhavati iti atas  vyavadāna pakṣa apavādaḥ  api syāt  iti evam ubhaya pakṣa apavādam anutiṣṭhantaḥ catvāri āri satyāni api niṣedhanti bhavantaḥ bīja ādiṣu janya janaka bhāvaḥ tāvat  āga upa aṅganā prasiddhaḥ atas  pratijñāyāḥ prasiddhi virādhaḥ  api hetu prayogeṇa pareṣu niścaya utpāda abhyupagamāt sva vacana virodhaḥ  api yaḥ ca bhagavatā pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇaiḥ bhāvānām sattā nirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ tasya api bādhā syāt  yatas  hiḥ  cakṣuḥ vijñāna samaṅgī nīlam vijānāti naḥ tu nīlam  ityādinā tāvat nīlādayaḥ  bhāvāḥ kalpān āpoḍha lakṣaṇena pratyakṣa pramāṇena jñāyanta iti pratipāditam na eva hi gagana utpala vartīni nīla ādīni cakṣuḥ vijñānena anubhūyanta iti  yad kiñcit samudaya dharmakam tad  sarvatra nirodha dharmakam  anena sādhya vyāpta hetunā anumāna pramāṇena upadarśitāḥ kṣaṇa sthita dharmiṇaḥ  bhāvāḥ prasiddhā iti spaṣṭam upadarśitam anena tāvat upadarśanena te bhāvā sa svabhāva tāyām nirucyante atyanta asat bhūta ākāśa puṣpa ādīnām utpāda avyaya dharma ayogāt   dhūmena jñāyate vahniḥ salilam ca balākayā  iti agni ādayaḥ  bhāvāḥ kārya liṅgena niyatam jñāyamāna tvāt niyatam svabhāvam avadhārayanti iti su spaṣṭam nirdiśyate balākā ādi hetūnām darśanāt marīcikā ādi abhāva anumānasya utpatteḥ abhāvāt  abhidharma ādau ye ṣaṣ  hetavaḥ catvāraḥ ca pratyayā abhihitāḥ te api sarva dharma anutpāda vāde tāvat katham yujyante utpādyasya kasyacid abhāvena hetu ādīnām ayukta tvāt  sūtreṣu sarve dharmāḥ skandha dhātu āyataneṣu saṅgṛhītāḥ samupadiṣṭāḥ skandha ādīnām bhagavatā kārya kāraṇa svabhāvatva samprakāśanāt katham te sarvedharma anutpādatāyām saṅgṛhītāḥ syuḥ yadi skandha divyatiriktasya kasyacid  dharmasya anutpādaḥ sādhyate tadā na asti kaścid  vivādaḥ vayam api tad vyatiriktam dharmam na aṅgīkurmahe yadi evam manyate yad saṃvṛtau pramāṇa ādīnām abhyupagamāt na eva eṣām sarveṣām dūṣaṇānām avakāśaḥ  yujyata iti ced  tadā saṃvṛtau bhāva abhyugama eva aṅgīkṛtaḥ syāt  yatas  hi yāni pramāṇa ādīni saṃvṛtau  abhyupetāni tāni niścayena sarva abhilāpa vidhura lakṣaṇa śaśa śṛṅga ādibhyaḥ  vyāvṛtta svabhāvāni eva vyāhatāni syuḥ yadi evam na syāt tatadā loka virodha āgama virodhaḥ ca katham parihataḥ syāt  vayam tu yad  sarva sāmarthya viraha lakṣaṇa śaśaśṛṅga ādi viparītam tad eva avastu iti abhidadhmahe yadi bhavantaḥ tān api saṃvṛti sat iti nāma mātram upacāra mātram vyavahāra mātram iti pravyāharanti tadā kāmam tathā abhilapantu iti na hi nāma mātreṇa bhāvaḥ tathāvidham svabhāvam anusarati iti atiprasaṅgāt  api ca kā nāma saṃvṛtiḥ iti api vaktavyam yadi sarvam asat iti kathyate tad api na yuktam paraspara virodhāt  tathāvidhā saṃvṛtiḥ tāvat asamartha eva ucyeta yadi utpādayati iti tadā sāmarthyam eva etad  tadā katham ekasmin paraspara viruddhayoḥ sāmarthya asāmathyayoḥ yoga iti katham asatā sanniṣpādayitum śakyate na hi sarvam asat iti tad katham iti ced  bhāva svabhāvā eva saṃvṛtiḥ iti tadā na asti vivādaḥ bhavataḥ pratijñāyā eva hāniḥ bhavaḥ  api utpadyata eva atas  saṃvṛtyā tad utpadyata iti katham evam ucyeta tadā tu anutpanna utpadyata iti uktam syāt  saṃvṛti viparītasya anutpādasya parama artha tvāt tadā paramārtha taḥ  anutpāda eva syāditi asambaddha bhidhānam syāt  upayataḥ  anubhayata iti eṣā api kalpanā na eva sambhavati paraspara viruddha tvāt yadi anitya arthaḥ saṃvṛti artha iti evam ced  tadā kim tāvat anityam yadi nitya abhāva mātram tadā katham tad loke pratītam syāt  yadi nityaditaram kim api anityam iti nigadyeta tadā nityasya vikalpa ātmaka tvāt tad itaram tāvat  sāmarthyāt nirvikalpam jñānam iti atasyat avasthāyām asaṃvṛtisa t iti kathanam tu nirvikalpaka jñānena tad pratīyata iti abhihitam syāt  yadi evam syāt tadā kim iva bhāva svabhāvaḥ  na abhyupeyate tathā tve ca anumāna kalpanāyāḥ  api tāvat  parihāraḥ syāt  sa vikalpaka tvāt tasyāḥ atha loka prati iti arthaḥ saṃvṛti artha iti evam ced  kaḥ tāvat loke  iti śāstra kārā vā prākṛtā vā janāḥ prathame vikalpe bhāvaḥ hi aneka paraspara viruddha svabhāvaḥ syāt  śāstra kāra ekasya api bhāvasya nānā ākāreṇa adhyāropaṇāt  dvitīye vikalpe nairātmya karma phala ādīni na abhyupetāni syuḥ prākṛtakaiḥ apratīta tvāt  atha māyā arthaḥ saṃvṛti artha iti ced  tadā kaḥ  hi nāma māyā artha iti vaktavyam yadi sarvam asat iti tadā pūrva doṣa eva samāpadyeta saṃkleśa vyavadānāni ca katham syuḥ iti ca atha bhrānti jñānena māyā iti ced  tadā ābhyantarika jñeya nayena kaḥ  hi viśeṣaḥ syāt  atha saṃvṛtiḥ nāma mātram iti tadā su bhāṣita durbhāṣitayoḥ bhedaḥ  aśakyaḥ syāt  asati abhidheye śabda mātre bheda abhāvāt atha śabda artha iti ced tadā katha bhedaḥ syāt  pratyātma adhigamyā ye sukha ādayaḥ te kutra saṃgṛhītāḥ syuḥ na hi tāvat  saṃvṛtau teṣām anirvacanīya tvāt saṃvṛti satām vyavahāra prajñapyamāna tvāt ca sūtre api evam uktamḥ  kim nāma saṃvṛti satyam yāvantaḥ  loka vyavahārāḥ ye akṣara pada niruktibhiḥ nidiśyanta iti  anena hi saṃkṣepataḥ saṃvṛti śabda arthaḥ  abhihitaḥ atha evam manyate yad ābhāsa parikalpyau vyāmiśrya sāmānya ākārena gṛhyanta iti tadā parama arthe api eṣa prasaṅgaḥ syāt  tasya api vacanīya sva abhāvye vyavasthita tvena abhidheya tvāt  na ca parama artha satye api saṅgṛhyante tad vastu sattayāḥ sattvāt  satya antara viśeṣa pūraka ākārā api te na bhavanti yadi pratītya utpannā rupādayaḥ pratyāma adhigamyāḥ sukha ādayaḥ ca api asaṃvṛti satyam it na āmrā prajñapyante tadā mudā tathā kuryuḥ iti kulmāṣam api dātavyam iti katipayena āvirpayayeṇa avivādaḥ ca iti atha kṣaṇa mātra anantara anavasthānena asthira arthaḥ saṃvṛti arthaḥ tad viparītaḥ ca nitya arthaḥ parama artha iti siddha sādhanam eva etad  bhavadbhiḥ evam vastunaḥ kṣaṇikatva svīkarāt  vayam api evam abhyupagacchamaḥ atas  na asti vivādaḥ tathā sāṃvṛtikānām vastu sāmānya lakṣaṇāmām yā nairātmya rupā dharmatā sā asti paramārthataḥ sā api utpādāt  vā tathāganāma nutpadāt  vā sarva kālam avikāra tayā nitya abhyupeyate atha asatya arthaḥ saṃvṛti artha iti tadā katham sā satyam iti paraspara viruddhayoḥ satya asatyayoḥ aikātmya anupapatteḥ bhāva svabhāvā eva kācana saṃvṛtiḥ abhyupagantavyā anyathā katham jagat  tathā satyam sidhyet  yadi tad abhyupagamyate tadā bhavataḥ pratijñāta artha hāniḥ syāt  anyat ca saṃvṛtiḥ pramāṇam apramāṇam vā yadi pramāṇam katham sā saṃvṛtiḥ atha apramāṇam tadā katham nairātmyam sādhayitum śakyeta avaśyam atas  saṃvṛti bījāni vijñāna ādīni paramārthataḥ santi iti aṅgīkartavyāni ṛte bījam saṃvṛti anutpatteḥ yad  bijam tad eva vastutas  sat iti api ca yadi bhāva svabhāvā abbhyupagamyante tadā teṣu āropitaḥ  mithyā svabhāvaḥ saṃvṛti satyam anāropitaḥ tu bhāva svabhāvaḥ parama artha satyam parama artha satyam tatas ca satya dvaya vibhājanam tāvat  yujyate yadi na abhyupagamyante tadā saṃvṛtiḥ api vitathā syāt  parama arthaḥ  api aśakya vyavasthānaḥ syāt  vyavasthā ākārāṇānām asattvāt yadi yathā kathañcana kañcid ekaḥ parama arthaḥ syāt tadā kimartham sa sādhayate sa na eva parama arthaḥ katham sa jñānena avadhārayitum śakyate na ca parama artha śabdena api abhidhātum arhaḥ evam tāvat na ayam parama arthaḥ na ca arthaḥ  api paramaḥ na api paramasya jñānasya ayam arthaḥ sādhāraṇa tvāt  yadi yathā kathañcana kiścid ekaḥ parama arthaḥ syāt  tadā paramārtha taḥ  asadbhāvasya ekasya yathā kathañcana nirākaraṇāt  bhāva sattāyā eva abhyupagamaḥ syāt  api ca yadi saṃvṛti parama arthau  abhinnau  iti manyate tadā satya dvaya vyavasthānām katham syāt  dvayoḥ ekatarasya parityāgāt  atha bhinnau tad ā ubhayoḥ pṛthak siddha tvāt  bhāva prasaṅgaḥ atha bhinna bhinnau tadā katham ekasmin paraspara viruddha tvam atas  pakṣaḥ  ayam ana bhinnaḥ na api abhinnaḥ iti na yujyate viruddha tvāt  evam bhinna abhinna tvasya anyaḥ  anya parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa tvena ekasya pratiṣedhe aparasya vidhānam na bhavet tadā asattvam eva sa tadā pratiṣeddhum api katham śaktaḥ ekasmin yugapad paryudāsa prasajyayoḥ virodhāt anyat ca bhavatām anusāreṇa tu puṇya jñāna sambhārau duṣparipūraṇau syātām tad abhāve ca buddha tvam api duṣprāpam syāt  pūjā anugraha kāmyayā yad  dīyate tad  dānam tu atyantam prasādam abhinirvartayati tad ca na asti deya dāyaka pratigrāhaka an upalambha āśrita tvāt  sa ca anupalambhaḥ kim deya abhāvāt  vā viṣaya abhāvāt  vā bhavati prathame tāvat  pakṣe na kaḥ  api kim api dadāti iti puṇyasya eva abhāvaḥ prasajyate sattva abhāvāt ca yaḥ  hi bodhisattvānām sattva artha pariśramaḥ sa nirarthaka eva syāt  atas  asattvam tu na asti eva viṣaya abhavaḥ  api tāvat na asti bhagavatā deyā ādi vastūnām paridṛṭa tvāt  yadi evam na syāuttadā bhagavatā bodhisattva avasthāyām katham arthibhyaḥ putra ādi dānam kṛtam bhavantaḥ tu ālambana āśritam dāna ādikam aviśuddham iti na abhyupagacchanti atas  sambhāra pāripūriḥ tāvat asambhavā eva tad abhāve hetu abhāvāt  buddhātvam api dūre apāstam syāt  api ca asarve dharmā niḥsvabhāvāḥ iti et tasya tāvat  kaḥ  hi arthaḥ yadi svayambhāvasya abhāvāt niḥsvabhāvā iti abhidhīyante tadā siddha sādhanam eva hetu pratyaya adhīna vṛtti tvāt sarva vastūnām na tāni ahetukāni iti vayam api abhyupagacchāmaḥ yadi evam na syāt tadā nirapekṣa tvāt nityam sattvam asat tvam vā syāt  yadi ucyeta vinaṣṭā bhāvāḥ sva svabhāvena anutpanna tvāt  sva svabhāvena na santi iti niḥsvabhāvāḥ iti etad api siddha sādhanam eva asmākam api vinaṣṭa utpatteḥ anabhyupeta tvāt  yadi ca abhidhīyeta tad svabhāvena eva sarva kāla anavasthānāt niḥsvabhāvā manyante tad api siddha sādhanam eva yasmāt utpatti samanantara vināśa sadbhāvāt kṣaṇikā eva kṣaṇikasya khalu vastunaḥ  dvitīye kṣaṇe avasthānam na abhyupeyate yadi ucyeta yathā bāla pṛthagjanaiḥ parikalpitasya grāhya grāhaka bhāvasya parama arthena svabhavataḥ  asattvāt  sa sattvam tathā niḥsvabhāva tvam iti tad api siddha sādhanam asmābhiḥ api parikalpita ātmanaḥ  niḥsvabhāva tvasya abhyupagamāt  yadi evam na syāt tadā sarve api tattva darśinaḥ syuḥ paramārthataḥ sarve bhāvā bāla pṛthagjanaiḥ parikalpitena grāhya grahakāreṇa virāhitā api ārya jñānasya advaita ātmanā gocara tvena sthitā eva yadi evam na sthitāḥ tathā api asattvena niḥsvabhāvāḥ tadā saṅkleśa vyavadānau na syātām tathā eva sarva dharma anutpādaḥ  api abhihitaḥ kim tad anutpada tāyāḥ tāvat artham manyase yadi ucyeta āditas  anutpanna tvāt  sarve bhāvā anutpannā iti tad api siddha sādhanam eva vayam api saṃsāram anādim manyāmahe atha pūrvam utpannasya vastunaḥ punar anupattyā sarve dharmā anutpannā iti tad api siddha sādhanam eva vayam api pūrvamatpannasya punar utpattim nābhyupagacchāmaḥ tasya vinaṣṭa tvāt  atha apūrva utpāda abhāvāt anutpādaḥ  abhidhīyate tasya vinaṣṭa tvāt  atha apūrva utpāda abhāvāt anutpādaḥ  abhidhīyate tad api na aniṣṭa sādhakam saṃsāre apūrva sattva anabhyupagamāt sarvadā ca pūrva vinaṣṭānām sajātīya utpatteḥ atha bāla pṛthagjana parikalpitasya sva lakṣaṇataḥ  anutpādāt anutpāda ucyate tadā api na asti virodhaḥ kalpitasya svabhāvata utpettara nabhyupagamāt  atha svatas  anutpādāt  anutpāda iti ucyeta tadā api na asti virodhaḥ hetu pratyaya adhīna tvāt  sarva vastūnām yathā pūrvam uktam yadi sarvaśas  sarva an utpādāt  anutpāda ucyate tadā darśana ādi virodhaḥ  durnivāraḥ syāt  yadi paraspara viśeṣa anutpādāt  anutpādaḥ  abhidhīyate tadā yadi tathatāsu abhavatām upādāya ucyate tadā na asti doṣaḥ kintu yadi loka prasiddha svabhāva tām upādāya ucyate tadā kena darśana ādi virodhaḥ  nivārayitum śakyate yadi svabhāva itara kriyā lakṣaṇa viyogāt  anupāda iti tadā api na asti doṣaḥ sarva bhāveṣu kriyāyāḥ  abhāvāt  atha īḥ cara ādibhiḥ itaraiḥ anutpādāt  anutpāda ucyate tadā api na aniṣṭam asmābhiḥ api īśvara ādeḥ anabhyupagamāt  evamādibhiḥ ākāraiḥ aādi śāntāḥ prakṛti parinirvṛttāḥ ityādi śabdānām api arthā vicāraṇīyāḥ api ca anyaiḥ aneka sūtraiḥ ca api virodhaḥ san  lakṣyate tathā hi ārya sandhi nirmocana sūtre hi uktam  atas  lakṣaṇa niḥsvabhāva tām abhisandhāya mayā sarva dharmaṇām anutpādḥ parikīrtitaḥ   parikalpita svabhāve hi lakṣaṇa niḥsvabhāva tā vyavasthāpyate mahāyāna prasāda prabhāvane nāma mahāyāna sūtre ca uktamḥ  kula putra bodhisattvaḥ dharmam ayoniśaḥ śabdaśas  pravicayya mahāyāna prasada āyatanaḥ  na bhavati śabdaśas  anabhipretya yoni śas  manasi kṛtvā mahāyāna prasāda āyatanaḥ  bhavati evam kula putra bodhisattvaḥ  ayoniśaḥ śabdaśas  dharmān pravicayya aṣṭāviṃśatim asat dṛṣṭīḥ utpādayati tad ayathā nimitta dṛṣṭiḥ adṛṣṭi darśana dṛṣṭiḥ vyavahāra apavāda dṛṭiḥ saṃkleśa apavāda dṛṣṭiḥ tattva apavāda dṛṣṭiḥ ca iti  iti evamādikam vistareṇa abhidhāyaḥ  kula putram kā hi tāvat nimitta dṛṭiḥ sāṃyogikasya svabhāvam abhisandhāya mayā sarva dharmāṇām yad asat tvam samprakāśitam tad śabdaśaḥ abhiniviśya ye sāṃkleśika dharmāṇām vaiyavadānīka dharmāṇām ca api asattve abhiniviśante asat nimitta upādānena teṣu asat dṛṣṭiḥ upajāyate atas  sā eva nimitta dṛṣṭiḥ uktā atas  bodhisattvasya śabdaśas  abhiniviṣṭāyām asat dṛṣṭi sā eva tasya mahatī dṛṣṭiḥ iti ata eva sā adṛṣṭi darśana dṛṣṭiḥ iti ucyate tatas  vyavahāra apavāda dṛṣṭi saṃkleśa apavāda dṛṭi tattva apavāda dṛṣṭa yaḥ tāvat jāyante tatas  vyavahāra apavāda dṛṣṭi saṃkleśa apavāda dṛṣṭi tattva apavāda dṛṣtayaḥ tāvat jāyante yadā nimitta dṛṣṭyā sarva apavādaḥ yadā kriyate tadā vyavahāra apavāda dṛṣṭeḥ api abhiniveśaḥ  jāyate saṃkleśa apavāda dṛṣṭeḥ api abhiniveśaḥ  jāyate tattva apavāda dṛṣṭeḥ api abhiniveśaḥ  jāyate  iti evam uktam laṅkā avatāra sūtre aupuktamḥ na asti vaikalpitaḥ  bhāvaḥ paratantraḥ ca vidyate samāropa apavādam hi vikalpantaḥ  vinaśyati parikalpitam svabhāvena sarva dharmā ajānakāḥ paratantram samāśritya vikalpaḥ  bhramate nṛṇām atas  pratītyasamutpannaḥ paratantra svabhāvaḥ paramārthataḥ san tatra parikalpita svabhāvaḥ  anutpādinā abhihitam iti eva tāvat nirdekṣyate punar tatra uktamḥ na hi ātmā vidyate skandhe skandhāḥ ca eva hi na ātmani na te yathā vikalpyante na ca vai na santi ca ābhyām dvābhyām pratiṣedhābhyām skandhānām sattā eva tāvat nirdiṣṭā mahā śūnyatā sūtre api yad uktamḥ  asti karma asti vipākaḥ kārakaḥ tu na upalabhyate  anena tāvat  vacanena virodhaḥ  api samupajāyate evam yadi paramārthataḥ karma api asti vipākaḥ  api asti tadā sarve dharmā niḥsvabhāvā bhavitum na arhanti yadi saṃvṛtau santi iti ced  tadā kartuḥ api saṃvṛtau sadbhāvāt   kārakaḥ tu na upalabhyate  iti evam na vaktavyam ārya laṅka avatāra sūtre ca uktamḥ astitvam sarva bhāvānām yathā bālā evirkalpyate yadi te bhavet  yathā dṛṣṭāḥ sarve syuḥ tattva darśinaḥ abhāvāt sarva dharmāṇām saṃśleṣaḥ  na asti buddhitaḥ na te tathā yathā dṛṣṭā na ca te vai na santi ca anena yadi sarva dharmāṇām asat tvam tadā saṃkleśa vyadānayoḥ apavāda doṣaḥ prasajyata iti nirdiṣṭam punar tatra eva uktamḥ bāhi artha darśanam mithyā na asti artham cittam eva tu yuktā vipaśyamānānām grāha grāhyam nirudhyate bāhyaḥ  na vidyate hi arthaḥ  yathā bālaiḥ vikalpyate vāsanaiḥ lulitam cittam artha ābhāsam pravavarte ārya daśa bhūmaka sūtre api uktam  citta mātram yad uta traidhātukam  iti tathā eva ārya sandhi nirmocana laṅkā avatāra ghana vyūha ādiṣu api sarva dharmāṇām citta mātra śarīra tvam nirdeṣṭum acitta mātram eva paramārtha sat  na itarathā iti sampradarśitam atas  sarve dharmā niḥsvabhāva tvena na sidhyanti āryātakūṭe api ullikhitamḥ  asti iti kāśyapa ayam ekaḥ  anta na asti iti kāśyapa ayam ekaḥ  antar  yad enayoḥ antayoḥ madhyam tad arupya nidarśa nam apraṣṭhimanābhā sam aniketam avijñaptikam iyam ucyate kāśyapa madhya tā pratipad  bhūta pratyavekṣā  iti anena tāvat  vijñānam eva parama artha sattva anidarśanatva ādi guṇa upetam śāścata ucchedānta dvaya vinirmuktam iti nirdiṣṭam etad adhikṛtya eva ārya ratna medhe api uktamḥ  kula putra yadi vijñānam paramārtha taḥ  na asti tadā brahmacarya ādīni nirarthakāni syuḥ  iti ārya ratna kūṭe hi uktamḥ  ye paramārtha sataḥ api vijñānasya apavādam kṛtvā sarva dharma śūnya tāyām abhiniviśya śūnyatā dṛṣṭikāḥ te acikitsyāḥ  iti tathā ca uktamḥ  varam khalu kāśyapa sumeru mātrā pudgala dṛṣṭiḥ na tu eva abhimānikasya śūnyatā dṛṣṭiḥ iti  ārya sandhi nirmocane ca api śūnyatā lakṣaṇam udbhāvitamḥ  paratantra lakṣaṇam maitreya pariniṣpanna lakṣaṇam ca saṃkleśaḥ  vyavadānam ca sarvathā atyanta viyuktam parikalpita lakṣaṇam yad tad na tena upalabhyata idam śūnyatā la kṣanam uktam bhavati  āryāṇām pratyātma vedyam avaśyam eva paramārtha taḥ  vastu sat anyathā ārya sandhi nirmocana uktāni vacanāni tāvāda sat arthakāni itī na eva yadi ucyeta kim khalu vastu yad ā ārya jñānena ārya darśanena vāniḥ vacanīya tvena parijñātam anirvacanīya dharmatā avabodhena saṃskāra asaṃskārābhyām prajñaptam iti yad uktam tena virodhaḥ syāt iti ekam eva yānam paramārtha taḥ  mahāyāna lakṣaṇam na avaśiṣṭam iti yad  bhavatā abhihitam tad api yukti āgamābhyām viruddham vipratipattinām sandarśanāt  sattveṣu tāvat  vividha adhimuktikā upalabhyante tathā hi kecana para hita āśayā eva pravartante atha apare niṣkāraṇam para duḥkheṣu spṛhante kecid tu alpa mātra eva ātmanaḥ  hita sukhe āsajyāyeṣu drahyanti tathā eva anye sva sukha sampatti sādhana tatparā anya vyāghātam kṛtvā tad duḥkha vinivṛttitaḥ  virajyate kecana saṃsāra sukha mātrasya eva abhilāṣeṇa puṇya ādīni sampādayanti tathā eva itare tāvat  bhava antara khecchataḥ  viramya sva mukti artham prayatante aye tu kevalam para vimuktim eva anucintayanti saṃbodhi nidānām ca dāna ādi pāramitā pravṛttim ālambante iti evam aprameya pratipatti ālambanāt  sattvānām chanda lakṣaṇaḥ  hetu viśeṣaḥ  anumīyate phala viśeṣaḥ  api hetu viśeṣa ākṣiptavāt tasya sva abhilāṣa dvāreṇa eva pravṛtti darśanāt  śraddhā eva hi pravṛtti hetuḥ iti niścitam sattva anām ayam śraddhā viśeṣaḥ  api gotra viśeṣeṇa avinābhūtaḥ atas  nānā gotra tvāt sattvānām tulya jātīya gotrakaiḥ vidhīyamāna pratipatti viśeṣa anurūpam phala lakṣaṇa yānam api nānā bhavati iti yuktibhiḥ nānā yānatā eva niścīyate bahu dhātuka sūtre api bahu dhātukāḥ sattvā vinirdiṣṭāḥ bhagavātā yad khalu dhātu jñāna balānām nānātvam abhihitam tad api nānā dhātu tvam kim iva asat  syāt  ārya kaṅkavatāra sūtre api pañca abhisamayotrāṇi abhihitāni ārya akṣayam ati nirdeśa sūtre api uktam trīṇi tau  atraiḥ yāṇikayānāni yad uta śrāvaka yānam pratyekabuddha yānam mahāyānam ca iti evam eva anekeṣu sūtreṣu api śrāvaka ādi yāna traya nirdeśāt  āgamataḥ  api tau  at nānā yānāni sidhyanti iti ārya sat dharma puṇḍarīka ādiṣu yad hi ekam hi yānam iti vyapadiṣṭam tadā abhiprāyikam iti draṣṭavyam samatā abhiprāya ādi pradarśanāt  dharmadhātu lakṣaṇa tayā yānānām bheda abhāvāt  ekam eva yānam iti tad abhiprāyaḥ athavā yānīkṛtam yānam iti yānikurvatām śrāvaka ādi pudgalānām nairātmye atulyatva abhāvāt  ekam eva yānam athavā ye vimuktāḥ teṣām abhinna tvāt  ekam eva yānam athavā aniyata gotrakāṇām śrāvakāṇām mahāyānena eva niryāṇāt  ekam eva yānam deśitam athavā sarva sattveṣu ātma adhyāśayena mahākaraṇa āmayā bhagavantaḥ pūrvam samudānīta bodhi sambhārāḥ śrāvaka gotrīyāḥ ca api buddhatva prāpti adhyāśayāḥ atas  abhinna adhyāśayāt  ekam eva yānam athavā bhagavatā svayam anekadhā śrāvaka yāna ādibhiḥ niryāṇa dvāraiḥ parinirvāṇa sandarśanāt  ekam eva yānam athavā na asti mahāyānāt  viśiṣṭataram yāna antaram iti tad adhikārāt  ekam eva yānam iti tad evaṃvidha abhiprāyeṇa ekam eva yānam iti deśitam athavā aniyatānām śrāvaka gotrīyāṇām ākarṣaṇa artham bodhisattva gotrīyāṇām ca sandhāraṇa artham iti abhiprāyaḥ  bhagavatā eva ārya daśa dharmaka sandhi nirmocana laṅkā avatāra ādiṣu sūtreṣu spaṣṭīkṛtaḥ anyat ca na eka bhava paramparāyām sambhārān paripūrya bodhisattvā buddhatva padam adhigamiṣyanti śrāvakā aśeṣa bhava saṃyojanam prajahanti iti teṣām na eka janma sādhyam buddhātu adhigantum kaḥ  api bhava pratī sandhiḥ na eva sambhavati tathā hi mūlam bhavasya anuśayāḥ yad uktam saḥ  api ātma graha prabhava eva iti niyatam abhīṣṭam ca āryaiḥ ātma dṛṣṭi viparītayā nairātmya mārga bhāvanayā sarva anuśayāḥ sa mūlam ucchināḥ tad samucchedena teṣām janmanaḥ  api ādhāra rasya abhāvāt tad  janma api samucchidyate phalataḥ kutas teṣām aneka bhava parampara asādhyaḥ  buddhātu alābhaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti ārya asat dharma puṇḍarīke bhagavatā yad śrāvakebhyaḥ  buddhātvā adhigateḥ vyākaraṇam kṛtam tad tu nirmita śrāvakāṇām nirmāṇasya yaiḥ bodhau pariṇāmanā kṛtā teṣām vā abhiprāyeṇa kṛtam iti draṣṭavyam idam tāvat  bhagavatā ārya laṅkavatāra sūtra ādiṣu nirdiṣṭam eva ārya samādhi rāja sūtre yad tāvat uktamḥ atra na asti kaḥ  api sattvaḥ  abhavyaḥ sampūrṇaḥ  ayam sattva lokaḥ  buddhaḥ  bhaviṣyati tad api ucyamānam upagatān abhipretya abhihitam iti jñātavyam katipayeṣu sūtreṣu  tathāgata garbhāḥ sarve sattvāḥ  iti yad uktam tad api tathatā lakṣaṇāyāḥ tathatāyā abhiprāyeṇa vyapadiṣṭam atas  paramārtha taḥ trīṇi eva yānāni sarve dharmāḥ ca sa svabhāvā iti abhidhīyate iti ayam pūrva pakṣaḥ tatas ca ayam pratyavasthīyate tatra tāvat  anāgamataḥ sarve dharmā niḥsvabhāva tvena sādhayitum śakyāḥ kena api tathā abhyupagama abhāvāt iti ādi uktam tad nirucyate kim kena api anabhyupeta tvāt āgama ekāntena anupādeya eva bhavati uta uta deyaḥ  api iti prathamaḥ tāvat  pakṣaḥ  na yuktaḥ tathā sati na kaḥ  api kam api āgamam āśrayiṣyati kenacid api tad anabhtu peta tvāt tatra kaścid  abhimānitayā vā anarthitayā vā pāpa mitra saṃsargeṇa vā vimūḍha citta tayā vā sukalyā mitrānupalambhena vā para pratyaneya tayā vā śraddhā indriya ādi vaikalyena vā tad vidān sudhiyām viraheṇa bhagavata ādi madhya paryavasāna kalyāṇam pravacana ratnam anāśritā api kim tāvat adhigata su apa rahita sampādana ūna upāyam tarka nipuṇam vidvāṃsam api na āśrayiṣyante athavā ajñā vaṇijaḥ  yathā vimugdha tayā anargham ratnam api parityajanti tathā su vijñāḥ tarka nipuṇā api vaṇijaḥ tad na parigṛhṇanti iti na tāpāt ca idāt ca nikaṣāt  suvarṇam iva pratyakṣa anumāna pūrva parāviruddha āgamaiḥ aviruddhātvāt  pareṣān ca āgamānām tad viparīta tvāt  ābhyudayikanaiḥ śreyasikanaiḥ śreyasika phalam āptu kāmā aśeṣa sampadam adhigantu kāmā vipaścitaḥ tam viparīta āgamam parityajya yad ekānta kuśalam tad pravacana ratnam eva āśrayanti iti yaḥ pakṣaḥ sa ced  samyak iti tadā bhavantaḥ  api yadi bhagavat pravacanam suparīkṣya eva abhyupayanti iti atas  bhagavatā prajñāpārāmita ādiṣu yaḥ  hi madhyamaḥ  mārgaḥ su spaṣṭam ādiṣṭaḥ tam kinna āśrayiṣyanti iti yadi svayam tam āśrayitum na śaktāḥ tathā api āri anāgāt juna pādaiḥ yaḥ  hi aneka yukti pradīpa prakāraiḥ su spaṣṭam nirdiṣṭaḥ tad balena api kim iva na abhyupagacchanti yatas  hi sa ācāryaḥ tāvat  bhagat vacana nirdiṣṭa tvena prathamām bhūmim āsādita tvena cārī alaṅkā avatāra ādau vyākṛtaḥ tasya api yadi nirdeśaḥ  viparyastaḥ syāt tadā na eva tāvat  bhagavatā tathā vyākṛtaḥ syāt  atas  yad ayā cārya vacānam tyajyate bhagavat vacanam api nūnam parityaktam bhavet  phalata ārya nāgārjuna pāda pratipadītam mārgam parityajya anārya pudgala pradarśita patha āśrayaṇam tāvān na eva yujyate na vayam śabdānām bhāvikaḥ kaścana sambandha iti manyāmahe atas tad niṣedha taḥ na te anabhyupagatā bhaviṣyanti iti te tāvat  śabdāḥ saṅketa abhijñānena vyavahāre vaktuḥ icchām dyotayante artha avasthā ādibhiḥ abhra anta puruṣaiḥ abhihitāḥ śabdāḥ vivakṣita artha asambaddhā iti na sarvathā niścetum śakyate anyathā sarva vyavahāra uccheda eva syāt iti kṣīṇa rāga dveṣa mohānām śabdā aviparīta arthā iti pratipādanena sarveṣām śabdā viparīta arthā evati na sva santatau viniyata tvāt teṣām atas tris upapaliṅgāni parikṣaṇa pariśuddhāni ādi madhya anta kalyāṇa niyatāni tāvat  vacanāni avisaṃvādaka tvāt  vidvadbhiḥ samāśrayaṇīyāni eva na vayam tathāgata vacana pratihatebhyaḥ tīrthikebhyaḥ tāt siddhaye bhagavat vacana prāmāṇyam pratipādayāmāḥ tathā api yadā āgama artham vinintayāmaḥ tadā vyākaraṇa pramāṇa tvena sampradarśayāmaḥ tad pratipādakam bhagavat vacanam na asti iti etad api kathanam na ucitam bhagavatā api evam eva nīta artha sūtra samāśrayaṇam eva abhihitam na neyārtha sūtra samāśrayaṇam iti yadi ucyeta kaḥ  ayam parama arthaḥ  nāma iti ced  pramāṇa upapatraḥ parama artha adhikṛtaḥ ca iti athavā yad arthaḥ  na anyatra netum śakyata iti sarva dharma anutpādāḥ tāvat  pramāṇa upanna arthaḥ atas  yukti anvita tvāt sa parama artha iti ucyate ārya dharma saṃgītau  uktam anutpādaḥ satyam utpādādayaḥ  anye dharmā asatyāḥ mṛṣā moṣa dharmaka tvāt  ārya satya dvaya nirdeśe api uktam  deva putra arthaḥ  hi paramārtha taḥ  anutpādaḥ ayam tāvat  sarva saṃkleśa vyavadāna dharmeṣu vyavasthāpyate na katipayeṣu  avam eva punar tatra eva uktam  tad yathā api nāma deva putra yad ca mṛd bhājanasya abhyantaram ākāśam yad ca ratna bhājanasya ākāśam ākāśa dhātuḥ eva eṣaḥ tatra paramārthanaḥ  na kiñcid nānākaraṇam evam eva deva putra yaḥ saṃkleśaḥ sa paramārtha taḥ  atyantān utpādatā yad api vyavadānam tad api paramārtha taḥ  atyantān utpādatā saṃsāraḥ  api parama artha atyantān utpādatā yāvat nirvāṇam api paramārtha taḥ  atyantān utpādatā na atra kiñcid  paramārtha taḥ  nānā karaṇam tad  kasmāt hetoḥ paramārtha taḥ  atyanta an utpāda tvāt  sarva dharmāṇām iti  evam ayam anutpādaḥ  api parama artha anukula tvāt  parama artha ucyate na vastutas  sarva prapañci tīta tvāt hi vastutas  parama arthasya atas  yāni ca yāvanti ca parama artham adhikṛtya anutpādīni lakṣaṇāni nirdiṣṭāni tāni sarvāṇi nīta artha tvena grahītavyāni atas  viparītāni neyārthān iti ārya akṣayam ati nirdiśa sūtre tāvat na īya nīta artha lakṣaṇam nirdiṣṭam tathā hi ke sūtrāntā neyārthāḥ yāvat  ye sūtrāntā saṃvṛti pratipattaye nirdiṣṭāḥ ta ucyante neyārthāḥ yāvat  ye sūtrāntāḥ parama artha pratipattaye nirdiṣṭāḥ ta ucyante nīta arthāḥ yāvat  ye sūtrāntā nānā pada vyañcanāni nirdiśanti ta ucyante neyārthāḥ yāvat  ye sutra antā gambhīra durdarśa durjñeyāni nirdiśanti ta ucyante nīta arthāḥ yāvat  ye sūtrāntā ātma sattva jīva puruṣa pudgalam anujamāna vakāra vedakān aneka rutaiḥ asvāmikān svāmina iva nirdiśanti ta ucyante neyārthāḥ yāvat  ye sūtrāntāḥ śūnyatā nimitta apraṇihita anabhisaṃskāra āja anutpāda abhāva nirātma niḥsattva nirjīva niḥpudgalā svāmika vimokṣa mukhā nirdiṣṭāḥ ta ucyate nīta arthāḥ iti vistaraḥ sutra antareṣu atāvat anutpāda ādi nirdeśā abhiprāya antareṇa nīta artha iti abhihitāḥ iti yad uktam tad api na samyak  ekam hi sthitau ātma ādi nirdeśā api nīta arthāḥ syuḥ atas  parama artha abhidhāyakaḥ  nīta arthaḥ tad viparītaḥ  neyārtha iti avaboddhavyam ārya sarva buddha viṣaya avatāra jñāna āloka alaṅkāre api uktam ayaḥ  hi nīta arthāḥ sa parama artha iti  ārya akṣayam ati nirdeśa sūtre ca anutpādāt ayaḥ  nīta arthā uktāḥ atas ca evam anutpāda ādaya eva parama arthā iti niyatam yadi evam tadā katham bhagavatā ārya sandhi nirmocana sūtre trividhasya svabhāvasya trividhām niḥsvabhagavatām abhipretya sarve dharmā niḥsvabhāvāḥ proktā iti ced  na asti doṣaḥ ye tāvat  kecid  saṃvṛti svabhāvam api apavadanti atha ca asat śastra śravaṇa abhiniśavaśād viparyasta matayaḥ saṃvṛtau asantam anṛtam api nitya ādi vastuḥ upatayā samāropya yathā rūpa pratibhāsam tathā eva parigṛhṇanti te āropa apavāda anta dvaya patitatam atitayā anta dvaya rahite parama gambhīre parama artha naya sāgare na anupraviśanti ataeva tāvat  bhagavān aanutpāda ādi nirdeśaḥ paramārtha adhikṛtaḥ iti nirucya trividha niḥsvabhāvatā abhiprāya pratipādakam anta dvaya rahitam madhyama patham madhayma patham prakāśayitum nīta artham eva matam pratiṣṭhāpitavān na ca mādhyamikāḥ trividha niḥsvabhāva tā vyavasthānam na abhyugacchanti iti anyathā darśana ādi viparītam katham parihareyuḥ iti tatra vicāritam tāvat  vastu yathā pratibhāsam māyāvat  pratītyasamutpannam tad ca paratantra svabhāvam tatra api saṃvṛtau māyāvat  para pratyayena tasya utpādaḥ na tu svayaṃbhāvaḥ ata eva utpatti niḥsvabhāva tāyām tad  vyavasthāpyate ayaḥ pratti asamutpannaḥ sa svabhāvataḥ śūnya iti vidvāṃsaḥ  nirdhārayanti na hi svabhāvaḥ  nāma kṛtrimaḥ abhūtvā bhāvaḥ bhūtvā ca abhāvaḥ  api tāvat nasti krameṇa api ekasya sat asat tvāmyām viruddha tvāt  yad uta na sambhavaḥ svabhāvasya yuktaḥ pratyaya hetubhiḥ hetu pratyaya sambhūtaḥ svabhāvaḥ kṛtakaḥ  bhavet  svabhāvaḥ kṛtakaḥ  nāma bhaviṣyati punar  katham akṛtrimaḥ svabhāvaḥ  hi nirapekṣaḥ paratra ca kutas  svabhāvasya abhāve para bhāvaḥ  bhaviṣyati bhagavatā api ārya anava tapta nāga rāja paripṛcchā sūtre nirdiṣṭam yaḥ pratyayaiḥ jāyati sa hi ajātaḥ  na tasya utpādu svabhāvataḥ  asti yaḥ pratyaya adhīnu sa śūnya uktaḥ  yaḥ śūnyatām jānati saḥ  apramattaḥ ārya sāgara rāja paripṛccha sūtre api uktam yad  pratītyasamutpannam tad ca śūnyam svabhāvataḥ yad ca śūnyam svabhāvena na hi tad casti kutracid  etad artham eva ārya pitā putra samāgama sūtre api pratītyasamutpāda pravṛttyā dharmadhātu pravṛttiḥ nidiṣṭā yad uta  tatra bhagavan avidyā tu avidyā tvena eva asatī tad katham iti ucyeta tarhi evam avidyā tu svabhāvena virahitā yasmin dharme na asti svabhāvaḥ sa na tāvat  vastu yad ca na asti vastu tad apariniṣpannam yad apariniṣpannam tad anutpannam aniruddham ca yad anutpannam aniruddham tad  aatītam iti prajñaptum na eva śakyate na ca tad anāgatam pratyatpannam iti api vā prajñaptum śakyate yad ca kāla traye api anupapannam tad nāma lakṣaṇam nimittam prajñaptam iti vā na bhavati yatas  hi tad  sattvānām grahaṇa artham nāma mātra saṃketa mātra vyavahāra mātra saṃvṛti mātra abhidheya mātra prajñapti mātrebhyaḥ  atiriktam na asti avidyā tāvat  paramārtha taḥ  anupalabdhā yaḥ ca dharmaḥ paramārtha taḥ  anupalabdhaḥ na tad  prajñaptaḥ na vyavahāryaḥ na abhidheyaḥ ca atas  hi bhagavan yad ca nāma mātram saṃketa mātram na tad tathyam iti  vistareṇa abhihitam ata eva paratantra svabhāvaḥ  na tathyatve yujyate anyathā māyā ādīnām api vastutva prasaṅgaḥ tāni api pratyaya sāpekṣatāyām na santi bhinnāni ata eva māyā bhinna tvena paratantra svabhāvaḥ tāvat utpatti niḥsvabhāva tāyām vyavasthāpyate ārya sandhi nirmocana sūtre ca abhihitam yathā māyā kṛtam tathā eva utpatti niḥsvabhāva tāyām upalakṣaṇīyam māyā āditaḥ  abhinnaḥ yaḥ  hi paratantra svabhāvaḥ sa eva nityān iti ādibhiḥ paramārtha ta upacaritaḥ sa eva ca parikalpita svabhāvaḥ saḥ  api yathā parikalpyate tathā lakṣaṇena asiddha tvāt lakṣaṇa niḥsvabhāva tāyām vyavasthāpyate sā api niḥsvabhāva tā vastutas  paratantra svabhāve eva sthitā yatas  hi tasmin  eva parikalpitaḥ sa lakṣaṇaiḥ upacaryate ata eva yathā anitya ādibhiḥ parikalpitāḥ sarve dharmāḥ paramārtha taḥ  lakṣaṇa śūnya tvena anutpannāḥ ata eva ca aniruddhāḥ ata eva ādiśāntāḥ ata eva hi prakṛti parinirvṛtāḥ ārya sandhi nirmocane api yathā uktam ye tāvat  sva lakṣaṇena āsantaḥ te anutpannāḥ ye hi anutpannāḥ te aniruddhāḥ ye ca aniruddhāḥ ta ādiśāntā ādiśāntā ye hi ādiśāntāḥ te prakṛti parinirvṛtā iti ata eva aham lakṣaṇa niḥsvabha vāta abhisandhāya asarve dharmā anutpannāḥ iti yad upadiśāmi tad api yathāśabdam artha parikalpanam nirākaroti paratantra svabhāvaḥ ca yathā saṃvṛtau hi uktaḥ tathā parikalpita ātmanā virahita tvena prasidhya saṃvṛti svabhāvasya anapavādam api nirdiśati na tu paramārtha tvena alakṣaṇa svabhāvaḥ tu na kaścana yujyate yathā uktamḥ alakṣaṇaḥ  na kaścid ca bhāvaḥ saṃvidyate kvacid  sarve dharmāḥ paramārthataḥ sadā bhāva niḥsvabhāva tāyām eva pratiṣṭhitā bhavanti ayam eva tāvat  pariniṣpatraḥ svabhāvaḥ nityam tasya anāropita tvena sthita tvāt  sa hi pramāṇaiḥ samyugupapatranna svabhāva tayā parama artha iti ucyate niḥsvabhāvatā prabhāvitā tvāt ca niḥsvabhāvaḥ  api atas  ayam pariniṣpannaḥ parama artha niḥsvābhāva iti ārya sandhi nirmocane api uktam  sa ca parama arthaḥ  api dharma niḥsvabhāvatā prabhāvitaḥ  api iti atas  parama artha niḥsvabhāvaḥ  iti yad nidānam anena niḥsvabhāvena sarve niḥsvabhāvāḥ tad nidānam anutpāda ādi deśanā nītarthā parama artha abhiprāya nirdeśāt  sa na tāvat  darśana ādi viruddhaḥ na ca yathāśabdam parikalpitaḥ ca ata eva nābhi prāya nirdeśaḥ  api nīta artha viruddhaḥ parigrahītavyaḥ atas ca abhiprāya nirdeśaḥ  api na nīta artha viruddhaḥ  bhavati iti phalataḥ anutpādideśanām nīta arthām sādhayitum darśana ādi virodham parihartum yathā śabda parikalpanam ca nirākartum ārya sandhi nirmocane tāvat abhihitam api ca parama artha samudgat parama artha niḥsvabhāvam dharma naiḥ ātma prabhāvitam iti abhipretya mayā sarve dharmā anutpannāḥ sarve dharmā aniruddhāḥ ādiśāntāḥ prakṛti parinivṛtta aśva deśitāḥ yadi evam mahāśraddadhā sūtre  prayoga jam svabhāvam abhipretya yad mayā asarve dharmā asantaḥ iti yad uktam tatra yathāśabdam abhiniviśca saṃkleśa vyavadāna dharmāṇām api abhāva mātram abhiniviśca asat nimitta grahaṇāt  asat darśanam tad  bhavet iti atas  nimitta darśanam tad ucyate evam vistareṇa yad abhihitam tad katham grāhyam iti ayam api yathā uktaḥ paratantra svabhāva eva yaḥ  hi saṃvṛtau hetu pratyaya bala sambhūta tvena māyāvat nisvabhāva tvena ca aprayoga jaḥ iti uktaḥ prajñāpāramitāyām api uktam  prayoga jaḥ svabhāvaḥ tāvat asat  pratītyasamunpanna tvāt   iti etad arśam yaḥ  hi parikalpita svabhāva uktaḥ saḥ  api āgantuka eva kalpanābhinirhata tvāt  ata eva saḥ paratantraḥ prayoga ja iti uktaḥ svabhāvaḥ  ayam dvidhā api paramārtha taḥ  na eva yujyate atas  sarve dharmāḥ svabhāvena anena paramārtha taḥ  niḥ svabhāvāḥ na hi abhāvāt  saṃvṛti svabhavaḥ  bhavati yadi sa tāvat asat  svāt tadā saṃkleśavyadāna dharmā na eva vyavasthāpayitum śakyeran yatas  hi tad prabhāvitā hi te na tu parama arthena prabhāvitāḥ evam hi sūtrānteṣu api pratipāditam iti atas  ye parama artha abhiprāyam na eva jānanti te pūrva svabhāvam api vastuḥ upeṇa parigṛhya paścāt tasya api abhāvam matvā anutpanna ādi deśanānām śabdaśas  artha abhiniveśam kurvanti te ca abhāva ādi nimitta grahaṇena nimitta ādi dṛṣṭayaḥ bhavanti atas tad niṣedhāya eva etad uktam na tu mādhyamikebhya etad uktam iti te tu tathatām sarva nimitta grāha pratipakṣām pracakṣate atas teṣu abhāva ādi nimitta grāha u na eva sambhavati tathā hiḥ apara pratyayayam śāntam prapañcaiḥ aprapañcitam nirvikalpa manāna artham etad tad tasya lakṣaṇam api ca asti iti śāśvata grāhaḥ  na asti iti uccheda darśanam tasmāt astitvana astitve na aśrīyeta vicakṣaṇaḥ yeṣu bhāva abhāvādayaḥ  nimitta grāhā bhavanti teṣu na eva sambhavati tattva darśana avakāśaḥ  api tathā ca uktam svabhāvam para bhāvam ca bhāvam ca abhāvam eva ca ye paśyanti na paśyanti te tattvam buddha śāsane yaḥ  ayam bhāva abhāva abhiniveśaḥ sa tāvat  bhāva abhiniveśa pūrvaka iti sūtreṣu pratipāditam tathā hi laṅkava tāra sūtre proktam astitatva pūrvakam na asti asti nāstitva pūrvakam atas  na asti na gantavyam astitvam na ca kalpayet  atas  ye khalu bhāva abhiniveśa paraśāste tāvat  paratantram sa nimittam paśyanti ye tu vyapagata bhāva grāhāḥ te tathā na kurvanti kutra api anavasthita tvāt tathā hi uktam siddhim āśrita bhāvānām icchanti tattvataḥ tu ye tatra nityādayaḥ  doṣāḥ sambhavanti na vā katham bhāvānām āśritānām tu hi asattvam sattvam eva vā jala induvat na ca icchanti te dṛṣṭvā na apahāritāḥ rāga dveṣa udbhavaḥ tīvra duṣṭa dṛṣṭa parigrahaḥ vivādāḥ tad samutthāḥ ca bhāva abhyupagame sati atas  ye anutpāda ādi deśanāsu śabdaśas  abhiniviśante tān pratiṣeddhum nimitta ādi dṛṣṭayaḥ vigarhaṇīyāḥ mādhyamika abhidhāḥ tu anutpāda ādi deśanāsu na abhiniviśante paramārtha taḥ  anutpāda ādīnām abhyupagamāt  saṃvṛtya utpāda ādīnām api vyāharaṇāt  tathā hi tattvam anveṣṭum ārambhe sarvam asti iti kathyatām jñātvā arthān khalu vairāgye paśca anūnam vivicyate anājñāya vivikta artham śruti mātre praviśya ca ye puṇyāni na kurvanti narāḥ te kutsitā hatāḥ phala yuktāni karmāṇi gatayaḥ ca su deśitāḥ tad svabhāva parijñānam anutpādaḥ  api deśitaḥ mama iti aham iti priktam yathā kārya vaśāt jinaiḥ tathā kārya vaśāt  proktāḥ su andha āyatana dhātavaḥ yadi evam ced  ārya laṅka avatāra sūtre na asti vaikalpitaḥ  bhāvaḥ paratantraḥ ca vidyate samāropa apavādam hi vikalpantaḥ  vinaśyati yad hi proktam tad katham iti cintāyām atra api yathā kathitasya parikalpita svabhāvasya samāropaḥ  bhavati tasya parihāra artham  nā asti vaikalpitaḥ  bhāvaḥ  iti uktam yathā uktaḥ paratantra svabhāvāḥ tu saṃvṛti niṣedha karaṇāt parāyatta vṛti tayā asan iti evam uktaḥ ucyamānam idam dvayam ye anta dvaya rupeṇa parikalpiyanti te na eva madhyama mārge pravṛttā bhaviṣyanti prapāta sthāna sthita skandha sadṛśa tvāt  atas   samāropa apavādam hi vikalpantaḥ  vinaśyati  iti uktam ata eva ca parikalpitam svabhāvena sarva dharmā ajānakāḥ paratantram samāśritya vikalpaḥ  bhramate nṛṇām yad uktam tena api tad nirākaraṇam bhavati anena api ca uktayoḥ samāropa apavāda antayoḥ nirākaraṇam kriyate tathā hiyathā vikalpyate tathā paramārthataḥ paratantrasya anutpanna tvāt  parikalpita ātmanā anutpanna eva tad anena samāropa anta svāvat nirākriyate saṃvṛtyā paratantra tayā samutpanna tvāt  tad āśritā anye vikalpā nirmāṇa nirmita sadṛśā samutpadyante ata eva paratantram samāśritya vikalpaḥ  bhramate nṛṇām iti evam uktam anena tāvat apavāda antaḥ  nirākriyate saṃvṛtya utpādasya anapavādāt  atas tatra tatra yā paratantra svabhāva astitatva deśanā yāḥ ca bhāva utpatyādi deśanāḥ tāḥ sarvāḥ deśanāḥ bāla pṛthagjanānām bhaya hetu parivarjana artham saṃvṛtya utpāda āśayena abhiprāyataḥ pravṛttā iti avagamāya na tu paramārthataḥ tad niṣedhaḥ tu sūtre kṛtaḥ yathā uktam laṅkā avatāra sūtre buddhayā vivecyamānam hi na tantram na api kalpitam niṣpannaḥ  na asti vai bhāvaḥ katham buddhayā prakalpyate na svabhāvaḥ  na vijñaptiḥ na vastu na ca ālayaḥ bālaiḥ vikalpitā hi ete vaśa bhūtaiḥ ku tārkikaiḥ ārya dharma saṅgītau ca api uktam kula putra lokaḥ  ayam jāti nirādhayoḥ adhyavasāyena tiṣṭhati atas  mahā karuṇa āmayena tathāgatena loka bhaya viṣaya parivarjana artham vyavahāra vaśena tasya utpatti nirodhau bhavata iti upadiṣṭam kula putra na atra kaścid  dharma utpadyata iti ārya prajñāpāramitā sūtre api  āyuṣman śāradvatī putra evam rūpam svabhāvena śūnyam yad ca svabhāvena śūnyam tad na utpadyate na ca niradhyate yasya natpatti nirādhau tad na anyathā bhavati iti evam yāvat  vedanātaḥ  vijñāna paryantam  iti vistaraḥ na atra parikalpitasya svabhāvaḥ  yuktataraḥ āgantuka tvāt  bhāva bahis bhūta tvāt ca tasya evam śabda arthaḥ  api na upapadyate yadi api rupādayaḥ paramārtha taḥ  anutpannaḥ tathā api bāla pṛthagjanaiḥ te utpāda ādi svabhāve parikalpyante iti evam taiḥ yadi tad svabhāve parikalpita tvāt  svabhāva śabdena ucyante tadā na doṣaḥ iṣṭa artha aviruddha tvāt  sūtra antare api  kula putra yaḥ  bodhisattvaḥ dharmān ayaḥ niśaḥ manasikṛtya śabdaśas  pravicinoti sa mahāyāna śraddhā āyatanaḥ  na bhavati yaḥ ca aśabdaśas  abhisandhi artham yoni śas  manasikaroti sa mahāyāna śraddhā āyatanaḥ  bhavati  yad uktam tad tu ye parama artha abhiprāya anabhijñāḥ saṃvṛti svabhāvam api apavadante te ayoniśaḥ dharmān pravicinvanti iti hetoḥ mahāyāna śraddhā āyatanā na bhavanti iti atas tad niṣedha artham idam iti uktam nikhileṣu api sūtreṣu śabdaśas  artha abhiniveśa pariharāya abhipreta artha avabodhāya ca samyak  yatna utpāda artham sarveṣu ca adhimaktyu pāda artham eva abhihitam na tu mādhyamika mata niṣedha artham na hi mādhyamikāḥ śabdaśas  artham parikalpayanti iti pūrvam eva ukta tvāt ārya ratna megha sūtre api uktam yathā  katham iva bodhisattvaḥ parama artha nipuṇaḥ  na bhavati kula putra bodhisattvaḥ samyak  prajñayā rūpa pratyavekṣaṇam yāvd vijñāna pratyavekṣaṇam pratyavekṣate yadā sa rūpam pratyavekṣate tadā na rupa utpādam upalabhate na samudayam upalabhate na ca nirodham upalabhate yāvat  vijñāna paryantam yathāvat utpādam na upalabhate yatas  hi saḥ  api tāvat  anupalambhaḥ paramārtha taḥ  anutpāda pravṛttayā prajayā bhavati na tu sāṃvyāvahārika svabhāvena  iti evam nirdiṣṭam ārya laṅkā avatāre api sarvam vidyati saṃvṛtyām parama arthe na vidyate dharmāṇām niḥsvabhāva tvam parama arthe api dṛśyate iti uktam ye tāvat anutpāda ādi nirdeśān asarve dharmāḥ paramārtha ta utpadyante saṃvṛti svabhā bhāvataḥ ca na utpadyante iti etasmin mate sthāpayanti te sarve ārya ratna megha ādi nirdiṣṭaiḥ samasta vacanaiḥ virudhyante vipratipanna tvāt  teṣām teṣu sūtreṣu tu rupādayaḥ sarve dharmāḥ paramārtha taḥ  anutpannāḥ saṃvṛtitaḥ ca utpannā iti nirdiṣṭāḥ satya dvaya nirdeśa ādiṣu tāvat  deva putra sarve dharmāḥ śāntāḥ paramārtha taḥ  anutpanna tvāt  iti evamādikam yad uktam tena api saha virudhyante punar ca ārya laṅkā avatare abhihitam bhāvā vidyanti saṃvṛtyā parama arthe na bhāvakāḥ niḥsvabhāveṣu yā bhrāntiḥ tad satyam saṃvṛtiḥ bhavet  ārya prajñāpāramitāyām api  subhūte viparyayam atiricya bāla pṛthagjanāḥ kutra avatiṣṭhante karma arbhi saṃskāra vastu tāvat  keśa agra tulyam api na vidyate  iti ādikā yā deśānā tayā api virudhyante vastutas  ātmanaḥ  ati sūkṣma svabhāvasya api niṣiddha tvāt  yadi viparyayasya apratiṣedhāt  asti viparyayam vastu tatra eva tathā prokta tvāt iti ced  tathā hiḥ niḥsvabhāveṣu yā bhrantiḥ tad satyam saṃvṛtiḥ bhavet  iti tad api na eva upapadyate viparyastam vastu yadi vidyeta tadā ati sūkṣma bhāva svabhāva niṣedha vacanam katham nāma upapadyeta asatīṣu api samasta bhāva vāsanāsu bāla pṛthagjanāḥ asat viparyaya upakalpitānām bhāva svabhāvānām abhiniveśena kamāṇi abhisaṃskurvanti iti yadā evam sūtra arthaḥ  vivecyeta tadā evaṃvidhena tāvat  vivecanena bhavat abhyupagatam abhyupagantum śakyeta ārya samādhi rāja sūtre svabhāva śūnyāḥ sada sarva dharmāḥ vastum vibhāventi jināna putrāḥ sarveṇa sarvam bhava sarva śūnyam prādeśikī śūnyatā tīrthikānām iti yad uktam tad api abhyuddhartum śakyate anyatra api sūtreṣu tāvat  prajñapti mātram tri bhavam na asti vastu svabhāvataḥ prajñapti vastu bhāvena kalpayiṣyanti tārkikāḥ iti yad ucyate tad api uddhariṣyate viparyayāt ayaḥ  hi vastu tvena tāvat na eva yaujyante iti evam bhavadbhiḥ citta caitta ātmakasya traidhātukasya yad asamyak tvam parikalpyate tad api asamyak ākāra upagrahaṇa avabhāsa tvena viparyaya ādi tayā procyate mithyā svabhāvena upagrahaṇāt  yaḥ tasya ātma tvena avabhāsaḥ sa katham samyak  bhāva iti bhavet  tattva anyatvayoḥ paraspara hāra sthita lakṣaṇa tvāt tattvasya tāvat anya ātmaka tvam hi viruddham yadi evam na asti tadā sāṃkhya ādi parikalpiteṣu pradhāna ādi vikāreṣu bhavatām kaḥ  dveṣaḥ svād bhavadbhiḥ teṣām anabhyupagamāt  ata evaḥ kasya syāt anyathā bhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ  yadi vidyate iti evam uktam ārya satya dvaya nirdeśe apiḥ  deva putra yathā ātmā nānti paramārtha ta ātmā tathā eva deva putra kleśā api paramārtha taḥ  na santi kleśāḥ deva putra yadi ātmā paramārthataḥ tattvam svāt tadā deva putra anena eva hetunā kleśā api paramārthataḥ tattvāni syuḥ   iti evam kathitam anena tāvat  ātma ādīnām mithyā ākāra upagrahaṇena pravṛtta tvāt  ātma ādivat  kleśā api sarve mithyā ākāra upagrahaṇena pravṛtta tvāt  ātma ādivat  kleśā api sarve mithyā svabhāvā eva iti evam tāvat nirdiśyate iti evam traidhātukāḥ khalu citta caitasikā mithyā ākāra graharaṇa pravṛtta tvāt su ākāra iva tad abhinna tvāt ca mithyā svabhāvā eva iti nirdiṣṭāḥ bodhisattvebhyuḥ tu viśeṣataḥ kliṣṭa tvāt  sarva parikalpānām te mithyā eva atas   mithyā sarva vikalpāḥ  iti evam tāvat  pratipāditam yadi na asti paramārtha taḥ  vastunām svakīyaḥ kaścana svabhāvaḥ tadā na hi ātmā vidyate skandhe skandhāḥ ca eva hi na ātmani na te yathā vikalpyante na ca te vai na santi ca yadi yad uktam tad  yadi evam uddhriyate yad anena nioṣedha mukhena su andha ādīnām tāvat  sattā eva nirdiśyata iti ced  tad na pramāṇa yogyam iti yatas  hi atra  na te yathā vikalpyante  iti yad uktam tena sat tayā niṣedhaḥ  vidhīyate  na ca vai na santi ca  iti amunā ca ye yathā saṃvṛta vavabhāsante te tathā eva sat iti nirdiśyante phalataḥ ca tairthika parikalpitasya ātmanaḥ saṃvṛtta vapi asattvam skandha ādīnām tāvat  vyavahāre sattvam na tu tathatāyām iti vispaṣṭam ādiṣṭam yadi evam na bhavet tad ā ekasmin  asattva bhidhāya punar  sattvena nirdeśaḥ katham sambadhyeta ārya brahna parivarta sūtre ca uktam yad uta yena skandhasya na utpattiḥ anupattiḥ ca jñāyate samudācarati tad loke na ca loke sthitaḥ ca saḥ iti ārya ratna meghe api na skandhāḥ paramārthataḥ santi saṃvṛtya eva te santi iti apaṣṭa tayā nirdiṣṭamḥ  kula putra daśa dharma samanvāgataḥ  bodhisattvaḥ saṃvṛti satye kuśalaḥ  bhavati ke ca daśa iti tad yathā rūpa prajñaptim karoti na ca paramārtha taḥ  rūpam upalabhate na abhiniveśam karoti vedanā saṃjñā saṃskāra vijñānani api tadvat iti vistaraḥ   ārya ratnākare apiḥ  sūryadatta  evam asti yathā vyomni citra aṅkanam na bhavati na bhaviṣyati yatas  hi tad abhūtam aniruddham anāgamam anirgamam anutpannam acyum anabhiniṣpannam anirvacanīya tvāt  vyavahāra mātram saṃvṛti mātram bhavati sūrya datta tathā eva rupa ādi vijñāna paryantam na bhūtam na bhaviṣyati ita ārabhya saṃvṛti mātram bhavati  iti etad paryantam yad  vistareṇa abhihitam tad artha sambaddham karaṇīyam iti nanu mahā parama artha śūnyatāyām aasti karma asti vipākaḥ kartā tu na upalabhyate yad evam uktam tad tāvat  etad viruddham syāt  yatas  hi yadā karma ādayaḥ paramārthataḥ santi tadā na bhavanti sarve dharmā niḥsvabhāvāḥ yadi saṃvṛtitaḥ te santi tadā kartuḥ api saṃvṛtitaḥ satvāt  akartā tu na upalabhyate iti etad kathanam na yukti saṅgatam syāt iti ced  yadi evam ucyeta tadā atrā api na asti virodhaḥ pūrvavat eva karma phalayoḥ saṃvṛtau  eva sattvāt  tairthika parikalpitasya ca kartuḥ saṃvṛtau  api asattvāt iti evaṃvidha nirdeśataḥ kutas tāvat  virodha avasaraḥ yadi evam ced  anyeṣu sūtreṣuḥ astitvam sarva bhāvānām yathā bālaiḥ vikalpyate yadi te bhavet  yathā dṛṣṭāḥ sarve syuḥ tattva darśinaḥ abhāvāt  sarva dharmāṇām saṃkleśaḥ  na asti śuddhitaḥ na te tathā yathā dṛṣṭā na ca te vai na santi ca yad uktam tad katham iti ced  idam api purvam aktam eva atra api ayadi sarvāṇi vastūni yathā avabhāsante tathā eva paramārtha taḥ  vidyante iti tadā asarve api tattva darśinaḥ syuḥ iti syāt  atas  anena api tāvat  paramārthataḥ sarva dharma anutpāda matam eva saṃsthāpyate yad hi aabhāvāt  sarva dharmāṇām iti uktam tena vastūnām saṃvṛti sattvam pratipāditam ana te tathā yathā dṛṣṭāḥ iti vacanāt  prajñāpāramitāyām api saṃkleśa vyavadāna vyavasthā khalu vyavahāra satyam āśritya eva kṛtā iti tad yathāḥ  subhūte prāptiḥ abhisamayaḥ  jātiḥ nirodhaḥ saṃkleśaḥ  vyavadānam iti vyavahārata eva saṃvidyante na tu paramārthataḥ iti   yadi evam tarhi tatra evaḥ  bāhya artha darśanam mithyā na asti artham cittam eva tu ayuktyā vipaśyamānānām grāha grāhyam virudhyate abāhyaḥ  na vidyate hi arthaḥ  yathā bālaiḥ vikalpyate    vāsanaiḥ lulitam cittam artha ābhāsam pravartate    citta mātram bhaḥ jinaputra yad uta traidhātukam  iti yad uktam tad katham nīyate evam eva āryān dhimiḥ mocane ārya ghana vyūha ādiṣvāpi sarva dharmāṇām cittamātra kāya tvena nirdiṣṭa tvāt cittam eva hi tāvat  paramārthataḥ sat  na anyat iti sādhyate atas ca sarve dharmāḥ niḥsvabhāva tvena na sādhyitum śakyante yadi evam ucyeta tad api na samucitam kāraṇam yatas  hi yathā citta sattā nirdiṣṭā tathā eva rūpasya api sattāyā nirdeśaḥ tad tad sūtreṣu anekadhā kṛtaḥ  vidyate atha pramāna bādhita tvāt  suttra antareṣu ca niṣiddha tvāta paramārthataḥ sattvena vyavasthāpayitum na śakyate tadā pudgala nairātmya mātra praveśa abhisandhinā tathāvidha vineya jana āśaya apekṣayā kathana mātram eva etad iti yadi evam ucyeta tadā cittam api vakṣyamāṇa pramāṇaiḥ bādhitam bhavati sūtra antareṣu api niḥsvabhāva tvena nirdiṣṭa tvāt  paramārtha taḥ  agṛhītā api sā cittamātra tā kramaśas  parama artha naya samudra avagāhana hetu mātra tayā nirdiṣṭā iti evam grahaṇanīyam iti iti evam ye tāvat  sarva dharmān niḥsvabhāva tayā yugapad jñātum akṣamāḥ te kadācana cittamātra tām āśritya kramaśas  bāhya artha niḥsvabhāva tāyām praviśanti ata eva yuktyā nirīkṣamāṇānām grahya grāhaḥ  nirudhyate iti uktam tad anantaram yadi krameṇa citta svabhāvaḥ pratyavekṣyate tadā tam api niḥsvabhāva tvena avabudhya nitarām gambhīra naye praviśanti yathā uktam bhagavatā cittamātram samāruhya bāhyam artham na kalpayet  tathāta ālambane sthitvā cittamātram atikramet  cittamātram atikramya nirābhāsam atikramet  nirābhāsa sthiotaḥ  yogi mahāyānam sa paśyati anābhoga gatiḥ śāntā praṇidhānaiḥ viśodhitā jñānam anātmakam śreṣṭham nirābhāse na paśyate anye tu bruvate cittamātra tā hi tavat  sva prasiddha svabhāvā atas  saṃvṛtya eva sthitā bāhya arthāḥ tu na khalu saṃvṛtya api citta kāram atiricya na sidhyanti ata eva bhagavatā tad pradarśana artham vastūni cittamātra tāyām nirdiṣṭāni sā api na paramārthataḥ sidhyati sūtra antareṣu api niḥsvabhāva tāyām eva nirdiṣṭa tvāt  yathā uktam ārya sarva buddha viṣaya avatāra jñāna loka akaṅkāre sarve buddhāḥ sadā sarvān dharmān jānanti sarvathā na upalabhya kvacid cittam na upalambha karam numaḥ ārya ratna kuṭa sūtre api cittam hi kāśyapa parigaveṣyamāṇam na labhyate yad na labhyate tad na upalabhyate yad na upalabhyate tad na eva atītam na anāgatam na pratyutpannam yad na eva atītam na anā gatam na pratyutpannam tad  tri kāla atītam yad  tri kāla atītam tasya sat asat tvam api na asti yasya na asti sat asat tvam tasya na asti utpādaḥ yasya na asti utpādaḥ tasya na asti svabhāvaḥ yasya na asti svabhāvaḥ tasya na asti utpādaḥ yasya na asti utpādaḥ tasya na asti nirodhaḥ yasya na asti nirodhaḥ tasya na asti viyogaḥ yasya na asti viyogaḥ tasya na asti āgamaḥ nirgamaḥ cyutiḥ jātiḥ yasya na asti āgamaḥ  nirgamaḥ cyutiḥ jātiḥ tasya na santi saṃskārāḥ yasya na santi saṃskārāḥ tad asaṃskṛtāḥ yad asaṃskṛtam tad ā āryaiḥ viditam iti vistaraḥ punar ca tatra eva  nitya iti kāśyapa ayam ekaḥ  antar  anitya iti kāśyapa ayam ekaḥ  antar  tathā asti iti kāśyapa ayam ekaḥ  antar  na asti iti kāśyapa ayam ekaḥ  antar  yad anayoḥ antayoḥ madhyam tad arupyamanidarśanam apratiṣṭham anābhā sam aniketam avijñaptikam iyam ucyate kāśyapa madhyamā pratipad  bhūta pratyavekṣā  iti yad evam uktam tad madhya bhūtam na tasya vastu satā vijñāna svabhāvena sattva siddhiḥ dharmadhātuḥ hi dvābhyām antābhyām vinirmuktaḥ sarva dharma nisvabhāva lakṣaṇaḥ niṣprapañca iti vacanīyaḥ sa ca api dharmadhātuḥ aayam saḥ iti ākāreṇa nirupayitum aśakya tvāt  arupyaḥ parebhyaḥ  nidarśayitu samartha tvāt  anidarśanaḥ ādhyātmike dhātau āyatane vānavasthita tvāt  apratiṣṭhaḥ bāhyānām dhātūnām āyatanānām iva anavabhāsita tvāt  anābhāsaḥ cakṣuḥ vijñāna ādi dhatu svabhāva atikrānta tvāt  avijñaptikaḥ rāga ādi samasta kleśānām āśraya abhāvāt  aniketaḥ iti evam uktam yadi madhye citta svabhāva tāyāḥ kaḥ  api aṃśaḥ paramārtha san syāt tadā tad sattayā nitya anitya abhiniveśaḥ khalu kathaṅkāram ekaḥ antar  syāt  yatas  hi yathā vastu tattvam tathā yathāvat anugamya manaskaraṇam patana sthānam iti na eva yujyate nitya ādi svarua upamatiḥ ijya vastu bhūtaḥ kaścid anyaḥ  vastu ākāraḥ  asambhavī madhye hi vastu khalu sva svabhāvasya asattvāt  abhūtam iti grahaṇam na asti tāvat  anta iti evam yadi cintyeta tad api na yuktam asat iti graḥaṇam satta grahaṇa abhāve abhāva eva viṣaya abhāva niṣedhaḥ tu na tāvat  san bhavati atas  yasya abhāva grahaṇam st niyatam tasya sattā grahaṇam api sat eva tatas  dvau  api antau bhavataḥ yadi madhye vastunaḥ sattvam tadā tad sattva grahaṇam kena tad sattva grahaṇam kena niṣiddham syāt  ārya samādhi rāja sūtre madhye sataḥ parama artha sthitasya vastunaḥ  niṣedhāya yad uktam tena api saha virodhaḥ syāt  asti iti na asti iti ubhe api antā śuddhī aśuddhi iti ime api antā tasmāt ubhe anta vivarjayitvā madhye api sthānam na karoti paṇditaḥ iti evam uktam ayam tāvat  sūtra arthaḥ āśrayaṇīye madhye yadi vastu satām na asti kim api svarūpam tadā eva amadhye api sthānam na karoti panḍitaḥ iti yad uktam tad  yuktam syāt iti ucyate yadi asti kim api vastu tadā katham na paṇḍitaḥ tasmin sthānam na grahīṣyati iti ārya loka uttara para varte tāvat uktam api ca he jinaputrāḥ trayaḥ khalu dhāvataḥ  vijñaptimātra tāyām pracaranti yatas  hi adhva trayam cittavat  pratibudhyate tad api tāvat cittam madhya anta rahitam eva pravartate idam tāvat  sūtrasya tātparyam utpāda bhaṅgayoḥ sthiti lakṣaṇe ca madhye paramārtha taḥ  asattvāt cittam tāvat madhyā rahitam sat  pravartate pratibudhyate ca iti ucyate apere khalu abhidadhate saṃvṛtau hi vijñānavat  bāhya arthā api saṃvidyanta iti anyathā daśa bhūmaka sūtre aṣṭabhyām hi bhūmau saṃsthitā bodhisattvā lokadhātu antargatānām paramāṇu ādīnām saṃkhyām parijānanti iti yad uktam tena saha virodhaḥ syāt iti tathā hi  sa paramāṇu rajaḥ sūkṣma tām ca prajānāti mahat gata tām ca apramāṇa tām ca vibhaktim ca prajānāti apramāṇa paramāṇu rajaḥ vibhakti kauśalyam ca prajānāti asyām ca lokadhātau yāvanti pṛthvī dhātoḥ paramāṇu rajāṃsi tāni prajānāti yāvanti ap dhātoḥ tejaḥ dhātoḥ vāyudhātoḥ prajānāti  iti vastaraḥ vijñānavat  bāhya arthānām api prasiddha tvāt  pratīti virodhaḥ yatas  hi yuktibhiḥ vicāraṇāyām satyām ubhau  api na eva parīkṣām sahete atas tau avtusthitim api na kṣamete vyavahāra satye saṃvṛtau tvāgopāla aṅganām yāvat  prasiddhau vijñapti mātra tā kathanasya tāvat  phalam tu para parikalpitānām kartu bhoktra ādīnām niṣedha eva vyavahāre api citta tiriktānām teṣām kartṛ ādīnām saṃsiddheḥ abhāvāt  athavā sarva dharmeṣu pūrvaṅgam atvāt cittam sarva dharma apekṣayā pradhānam sidhyate yāvat  yathā  nāsti artham cittam eva tu  iti yad uktam yathā vā  vāsanaiḥ lulitam cittamārtha ābhāsam pravartate  ityādi yad uktam yathā vā  vāsanaiḥ lulitam cittamārtha ābhāsam pravatate  ityādi yad uktam tad api nirākāreṇa cittena viṣaya grahaṇam katham api na yujyata iti avaśyam tad  sa ākāram eva mantavyam atas citta ākāram vyatiricya artha ākāra avabhāsā bhāvāt tad niṣedhena sa ākāra cittam eva tāvat nirdiśyate na tu tena bahya arthā bhāvaḥ avabodhyate athavā ātma disattā nirdeśa iva tad vineya jana apekṣayā yathā sat vaidya āturān puṣṇāti tathā bhagavantaḥ  na anavidyā deśānāḥ pravartayanti yathā uktam laṅkā avatāra sūtre āture āture yadvat  bhiṣaj  dravyam prayacchati buddhā hi tadvat  sattvānām cittamātram vadanti vai na anyān visaṃvādayati iti vineya janānām hita sukha kara tvāt sārthakam vacanam para hitam tāvat ekānta tayā satyam iti hetuḥ bhagavatsu tāvat na asti mṛṣāvādaḥ  api ata uktam asatyam yad  visaṃvādi na asat ca api artha saṃhitam dhruvam para hitam yuktam hita abhāvāt na ca aparam iti evam kim sṃvṛtau  asti bāhya artha sattvan varam tāvat cittam atra tā kintu niḥsandigdham sūkṣma vastu svabhāvam samyak  sādhayitum na asti sarvathā kaḥ  api āpta āgamaḥ ārya ratna megha sūtre tāvat   kula putra yadi bhavet  paramārtha taḥ  asattvam tadā nirarthakam brahmacaryam  iti yad uktam tad kim na asti sat  yadi evam ucyeta tad na eva yujyate yatas  hi tad pramāṇa bhūtam parama artham kaḥ  hi nāma tyajet  ayam tāvat  sūtra arthaḥ iyam hi pudgala dharma nairātmya lakṣaṇā tathatā eva parama artha śabda vācyā paramasya jñānasya gocara tvāt  yuktimat tvāt ca sā eva svayam parama iti yadi tad api asat syāt tadā yathā pudgalaḥ  dharmāḥ ca bāla pṛthagjaneṣu prasiddhāḥ tathā eva syuḥ tathā sati sarve janā anāyāsena ādita eva tattva darśinaḥ syuḥ tattva darśana artham ca prayatnaḥ  api nirarthakaḥ syāt iti su spaṣṭam eva atas  na asti idam pramāṇa upapannam iti ārya ratna kūṭa sūtre tāvataḥ  kāśyapa varam khalu sumeru mātrā pudgala dṛṣṭiḥ nābhimānikasya śūnyatā dṛṣṭiḥ  iti uaduktam tena katham na virodhaḥ syāt iti ced  tarhi na asti virodhaḥ ye khalu paramārtha sat  vastu abhyupagamya punar tasya asattvam parikalpayanti evañca yeṣām vināśa artham śūnyatā deśānā teṣām rāga ādīnām samyak  sattvam eva iti parikalpayanti te pūrvam sattvam parikalpya paścāt  tad asattvam parigṛhṇanti atas  sat asat antayoḥ patita tvāt  te anta dvaya rahitam sarva prapañca paśamam śūnyatā artham na eva adhigacchanti iti  abhimāninaḥ ata eva bhagavantaḥ tathāvidhāyā dṛṣṭeḥ niṣedhena paramārthataḥ sat asat sarva prapañca jāla virahitasya jñāna artham niyojayanti iti anyaiḥ api sūtreḥ svayam bhagavatā etad nirdhāryate laṅkā avatāra sūtre apiḥ  dvaya niśritaḥ  ayam mahāmate lokaḥ  yad uta astitva niśritaḥ ca nāstitva niśritaḥ ca bhāva abhāva  chanda dṛṣṭi patitaḥ ca aniḥśaraṇe niḥśaraṇa buddhiḥ tatra mahāmate katham astitva niśritaḥ  lokaḥ yad uta vidyamānaiḥ hetu pratyayaiḥ loka utpadyate na avidyamanaiḥ vidyamānam ca utpadyamānam utpadyate na avidyamānam sa ca evam bruvan mahāmate bhāvānām astitva hetu pratyānām lokasya ca hetu astivādī bhavati tatra mahāmate katham nāstitva niśritaḥ  bhavati yad uta rāga dveṣa moha abhyupagamam kṛtvā punar api rāga dveṣa moha bhāva abhāvam vikalpayati yaḥ ca mahāmate bhāva abnām astitvam na abhyupaiti bhāva lakṣaṇa vivikta tvāt  yaḥ ca buddha śrāvaka pratyekabuddhānām rāga dveṣa mohāt na abhyupaiti bhāva lakṣaṇa vinirmukta tvāt  vidyante na iti katamaḥ  atra mahāmate vaināśikaḥ  bhavati mahāmatiḥ āha ya eṣa bhagavan abhyupagamya rāga dveṣa mohān na punar abhyupaiti bhagavān āha sādhu sādhu mahāmate sādhu sādhu punar tvam mahāmate yaḥ tvam evam prabhāṣitaḥ kevalam mahāmate na rāga dveṣa moha bhāva abhāvāt  vaināśikaḥ  bhavati buddha śrāvaka pratyekabuddha vaināśikaḥ api bhavati idam ca mahāmate sandhāya uktam mayā avaram khalu sumeru mātrā pudgala dṛṣṭiḥ na tu eva nāsti astitva abhimānikasya śūnyatādṣṛṣṭiḥ iti ata eva bhagavatā avastu vādina eva abhimāninaḥ iti uktāḥ atas tatra eva uktam abhutvā yasya utpādaḥ  bhūtva vā api vinaśyati pratyayaiḥ sat asat ca api na te śāsane sthitāḥ yasya na utpadyate kiñcid na ca kiñcid nirudhyate tasya asti na asti na upaiti viviktam paśyataḥ  jagat  dvitīya padya artha dvāreṇa sva matam saṃsthāpya aparikalpita svabhāva vivikta tvāt  viviktam jagat iti eva tāvat  sūtra arthaḥ atas ca na asti virodhaḥ iti abhidadhadbhiḥ kaḥ parikalpitaḥ svabhāvaḥ iti abhidhātavyam atha pramāṇa viruddham api yad  bālaiḥ satyam iti gṛhyate tad iti ced  tadā aśeṣam jagat  paramārtha taḥ  anutpannam api bālaiḥ yad utpatti ādikam paramārthataḥ sat iti āropyate tad  vakṣyamāṇa pramāṇaiḥ niṣiddha tvāt  saṃvṛti svabhāvam iti kasmāt na gṛhyate yadi evam na asti tadā yad hi bhagavatā bāhya arthāḥ parikalpita svabhāvatva āchūnyāḥ iti yad uktam tasya paramārtha taḥ  na santi iti vyākhyānam kasmāt na kriyate pramāṇa viruddha tvāt tathā vyakhyānam na karttavyam iti ced  tadā vijñānasya api tathā vyākhyānam na kartuvyam bāha arthavat  tasya api pramāṇa viruddha tvāt  pramāṇai katipayaiḥ yadi vijñānam vastu sat sidhyati tadā dvividham eva parikalpitam na anyat iti samyak  vyākhyātam bhavet  kintu tad api na eva sidhyati iti nirdeṣṭavyam atas ca jagat idam yathā ukta parikalpita svabhāva viviktam iti asmābhiḥ api abhyupeyata iti na asti sarvathā durūham ata eva ārya sandhi nirmocana sūtre  maitreya paratantra pariniṣpanna lakṣaṇayoḥ parikalpita saṃkleśa vyavadāna lakṣaṇam yad ca atyanta viviktam tad na ālambanīkriyate sarva śūnyatā lakṣaṇa tvāt tasya iti yad uktam tad api anena nirākṛtam bhavati  iti uktam tatra api rāgādayaḥ  ye saṃkleśa ātmaka saṃvṛti svabhāvānām paratantra lakṣaṇānām samyaktayā saṃkliṣṭa karaṇena saṃsāre niyojanena pratipakṣe ca yathākramam vidhyana bhūta abhūtatva ādinā ca āropyante te teṣām kṛte parikalpita lakṣaṇāni eva yogi saṃvṛtau aviparyasta pariniṣpattyā tāvat  pariniṣpanna lakṣaṇam atas  pariniṣpanna lakṣaṇa yuktāni bodhi pakṣa anukūla vyavadānāni api vipakṣa atyanta pratighāta rupeṇa parinirvāṇe ca niyojana ādinā samyaktayā vastu dharma tāyām āropitāni tāni api teṣām parikalpita lakṣaṇam eva yaḥ ca dharmadhātuḥ prakṛti prabhāsvaraḥ tasmin  asambhavaḥ paramārthataḥ saṃkleśa ādīnām atas  parikalpita dharma tvāt  tayoḥ svabhāvayoḥ saṃkleśa vyavadā dharma tvam asambhavam eva saṃkleśa vyavadāna pakṣa sarva dharmāṇām paramārtha taḥ  anutpāde hi eka rasībhūta tvena nānā karaṇam ayuktam atas  dvau  api samyak rupeṇa śūnyau  eva tathya saṃvṛtau tu dvayoḥ api bhāvāt  saṃkleśabyadāna pakṣayoḥ abhāvā doṣaḥ  api na khalu prasajyate ārya sārdha dvi sāhasrikā sūtre  na hi su vikrānta vikrāmin rūpam rāgadharmi vā virāga dharmi vā evam vedanā saṃjñā saṃskārāḥ na vijñānam rāgadharmi vā virāga dharmi vā yā ca rūpa vedanā saṃjñā saṃkāra vijñānānām na rāga dharma tā na api virāga dharma tā iyam prajñāpāramitā na hi su vikrānta vikrāmin evam dveṣa dharma vā adveṣa dharmi vā evam vedanā saṃjñā saṃskārāḥ na vijñānam dveṣa dharmi vā adveṣa dharmi vā yā ca rūpa vedanā saṃjñā saṃskāra vijñānānām na dveṣa dharma tā na api vigata dveṣa dharma tā iyam prajñāpāramitā na hi su vikrānta vikrāmin rūpam moha dharmi vā vigata moha dharmi vā evam vedanā saṃjñā saṃskārāḥ na vijñānam moha dharmi vā vigata moha dharmi vā yā ca rūpa vedanā saṃjñā saṃskāra vijñānānām na moha dharma tā na api vigata moha dharma tā iyam prajñāpāramitā na hi su vikrānta vikrāmin rūpam saṃkliśyate vā vyavadāyate vā evam vedanā saṃjñā saṃskārāḥ na vijñānam saṃkliśyate vā vyavadāyate vā yā ca rūpa vedanā saṃjñā saṃskāra vijñānānām asaṃkleśa tā avyavadāna tā iyam ucyate prajñāpāramitā  iti uktam ārya satya dvaya nirdeśa sūtre api  katamayā punar mañjuśrīḥ samatayā yāvat  paramārtha taḥ  yad samam vyavadānam tad samāḥ sarva dharmāḥ paramārtha ta iti mañjuśrīḥ āha deva putra paramārthataḥ sarva dharma anutpāda sama tayā paramārthataḥ sarva dharma atyantā jāti samatayā paramārthataḥ sarva dharma abhāva sama tayā paramārthataḥ samāḥ sarva dharmāḥ  iti uktam ārya sarva buddha viṣaya avatāra jñāna āloka alaṅkāra sūtre ca  saṃkṣepataḥ  hi sarve akuśala manaskārāḥ tāvat  saṃkleśa hetavaḥ  bhavanti sarve ca kuśala manaskārā vyavadāna hetava iti tatra ye ca api saṃkleśa hetavaḥ  vā vyavadāna hetavaḥ  vā dharmāḥ te sarve svabhāvataḥ śūnyāḥ niḥsattva nirjīva niḥpudgala nirātmaka māyāvat niḥsva lakṣaṇa tvebhyaḥ atas te antar śāantāḥ ye antar śāntāḥ te praśāntāḥ ye praśāntāḥ te tāvat tad prakṛtikāḥ ye khalu tad prakṛkāḥ te na upalabhyante ye na upalabhyante te na eva upatiṣṭhante ye na upatiṣṭhante ta eva tāvat ākāśam ākāśam ca abhyavakāśaḥ sarva dharmān ākāśa samān vijñāya api saṃkleśaḥ vyavadānam ca iti vyavahiyete ākāśa dharma tā ca api na apanīyate katham idam iti ced  mañjuśrīḥ jāti nirodha dharmavān na kaḥ  api dharmaḥ  bhavati  iti uktam yadi punar  parikalpita lakṣaṇa śūnyaḥ kaḥ  api dharmaḥ syāt  tadā asmin  eva sūtre  mañju śrīḥ advayā sarve dharmāḥ arthāt niḥsva lakṣaṇā advaidhīkārā anāmikā animittā amanaḥ citta vijñāptikā anutpannā aniruddhā ahetukā asañcārā asanudācārā anakṣarā anirghoṣa svarāḥ santi  iti yad uktam api ca  mañju śrīḥ yad śūnyam tad abhiniveśa grahaṇa abhāvasya eva etad adhivacanam mañjuśrīḥ na upalabhyate paramārthataḥ kaścana śūnyatā ākhyaḥ  dharmaḥ  iti ca yad uktam tad  virudhyate yadi evam tadā ārya sandhi nirmocana sūtre  abhilāpaḥ tāvat na asti asat bhūtaḥ  bhāvaḥ tatra kaḥ  hi nāma bhāva iti ced  yaḥ khalya vārya jñānena ārya darśanena ca anirvacanīyatāyām avabudhyate sa eva tad anirvacanīya tāyām avabuddha tvat  asaṃskṛta nāmnā kevalam vyavahiyate  iti ādikam yad uktam tathā bhagavat pravacaneṣu ca yad ā ārya jñāna gocaram pratyātma vedanīyam tad  bhāva svabhāvena sat iti nirdiṣṭam tad katham sambhavet iti ced  na virodhaḥ atra ārya jñāna gocarāṇām sarva dharmāṇām yaḥ  hi nairātmya lakṣaṇaḥ  dharmadhatuḥ sa eva bhāva śabdena vivakṣayā vastu abhiniveśa śālinām bhaya sthānam parihartu kāmena tathā deśitam athavā ārya jñānāni sarve ca dharmāḥ tathatā āpannāḥ atas  vastu śabda āśraya pratipipādayiṣayā dharma dhātuvā abhihitaḥ syāt iti bhagavat bhitṛ api vineya jana āśaya anurodhena tāvat  sā dharmatā eva vividhaiḥ upāyaiḥ upadiṣṭā ārya laṅka avatāra sūtre  mahāmate padārthānām tathāgata garbha upadeśam kṛtvā tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksambuddhā bālānām nairātmya santrāsa pada vivarjana artham nirvikalpa nirābhāsa gocaram tathāgatarbhakha upadeśena deśayanti tad yathā mahāmate kumbhakāra ekasmāt mṛd paramāṇu rāśeḥ vivadhāni bhāṇḍāni karoti hasta śilpa daṇḍa udaka sūtra prayatna prayogāt  evam eva mahāmate tathāgatāḥ tad eva dharma nairātyam sarva vikalpa lakṣaṇa vinivṛttam vividhaiḥ prajñā upāya kauśalya yogaiḥḥ garbha upadeśena vā nairāmya upadeśena vā kumbhakāravat citraiḥ pada vyañcana paryāyaiḥ deśayante  tathā tāpiyam sarvathā vācyā api vyavahāra vaśena aśeṣa
