saṃskṛta dharma tā atas  saṃkṛtā iti nāmnā vyavahiyate utpādāt  vā tathāgatānām anutpādāt  vā tathāgatanām sarva kāleṣu sthita tvāt  asaṃskṛtā iti nāmnā api vyapadiṣṭā tathatā tāvat  sarva svabhāva atīta lakṣaṇā atas  na antyu bhaya svabhāvā api ittham eva avabudhyate anyathā bhavat sammatam asaṃskṛtaḥ tu api tad  katham bhavet  yatas  hi bhavatā tad asaṃskṛtam vastu iti api abhidhīyate saṃskṛtam eva vastu iti api ca abhidhīyate ārya ratna kara sūtre api uktam vadanti ye vai tathatām asaṃkṛtām tathā eva ca anye kṛtakān yatas tām na utsāhavantaḥ  hi ubhaye bhavanti dharmasya jñāne sugata upadiṣṭe atas tad ittham saṃskṛta asaṃskṛtayā uḥ vastutva grāhaḥ tāvat  anta grāha iti athavā śrāvaka pratyekabuddhanām yad  gocaram tad sva lakṣaṇam vastitvati abhyupagacchātām bālānām kevalam santrāsa pada vivarjana artham eva ārya jñāna gocaram vastu sat iti abhihitam buddha bodhiattvānām atyanta loka uttara jñānasya viṣayaḥ tu pāramārthikam vastu sva lakṣaṇam sarvathā asat sarva dharma anutpāda anirodha viṣayaka tvāt  sat asat pakṣa virahitam eva tad iti sūtre aupuktam  kim loka uttara jñānam śrāvaka pratyekabuddhānām sva sāmānya lakṣaṇa patita āśayānām yaḥ  hi abhiniveśaḥ kim atyanta loka uttara jñānam buddha bodhisattvānām nirābhāsa dharpra vicayena anutpāda anirodha darśanāt sat asati akṣa vivarjitam tad iti   śrāvaka ādayaḥ tāvat  tathya saṃvṛti saṃgṛhītam skandha mātram sva sāmānya lakṣaṇa ākareṇa bhāvayanti atas  pudgala nairātmya mātra gṛhīta tvāt teṣām tad jñānam vastu viṣayakam iti vyavahriyate na tu parama artha tayā yadi buddha bodhisattvānām jñānasya viṣayaḥ parama artha lakṣaṇena saha ekībhūtam tadā katham tad jñānam sat pakṣa vivarjitam syāt  ata eva hi bālānām santrāsa pada vivarjana artham ārya jñāna gocaram vastu sat iti upadiṣṭam na tu paramārtha taḥ  vastu sva lakṣaṇa sat iti kathana artham yadi evam na asti tadā buddhām bodhisattvāḥ ca sa dvikalpa sambaddhā na bhavanti iti yathā bālānām santrāa pada vivarjana artham iti uktam na tu paramārtha taḥ  vastu sat iti pratipādana artham tathā bhagavatā api sūtra antareṣu deśitam tathā hi ārya kaṅka avatāra sūtre  kim idam bhagavan sattvānām tvayā na asti asi dṛṣṭim vinivārya vastu svabhāva abhiniveśena ārya jñāna gocara viṣa aabhiniveśāt na astitva dṛṣṭiḥ punar nāstitva dṛṣṭiḥ punar nipātyate vivikta dharma upadeśa abhāvaḥ ca kriyate ārya jñāna svabhāva vastu deśanayā bhagavān āha na mayā mahamate vivikta dharma upadeśa abhāvaḥ kriyate na ca na ca asti itu adṛṣṭiḥ nipātyate ārya vastu svabhāva nirdeśenaḥ kintu uttrāsa pada vivārjana artham sattvānām mahāmate mayā anādi kāla bhāva svabhāva lakṣaṇa abhiniviṣṭānām ārya jñāna vastu svabhāva abhiniveśa alakṣaṇa dṛṣṭyā vivikta dharma upadeśaḥ kriyate na mayā mā ahamate bhāva svabhāva upadeśaḥ kriyate kim tu mahāmate svayam eva adhigata yāthātathya vivikta dharma vihāriṇaḥ  bhaviṣyanti  iti vistaraḥ atas  yad ā ārya jñāna gocara viṣayaḥ  vastu sva lakṣaṇa tvena nirdiṣṭa nirdiṣṭaḥ sa tāvat  bhagavata upāyena eva deśanā mātram atas  bhagavataḥ  asandigdham pravacana nayam anupādāya te mithyā moṣa dharmakam vastu svabhāva tvena vikalpayanti te tāva abhimāninaḥ  bhagavantam api apavādya svayam vinaśyanti parān  ca api nāśayanti evam ittham asnin  eva sūtre vastu sabhāva abhiniveśinaḥ ātma grāha gṛhīta tvāt na muktā bhaviṣyanti iti evam samupadiṣṭam  punar aparam mahāmate pramāṇa traya avayava pratyavasthānam kṛtyā ārya jñāna pratyātma adhigamyam svabhāva dvaya vinirmuktam vastu svabhāvataḥ  vidyata iti vikalpayiṣyanti na ca mahāmate citta manaḥ  manaḥ vijñāna citta parāvṛtti āśrayāṇām sva citta dṛśya grāhya grāhaka vikalpa prahīṇānām tathāgata bhūmi pratyātma ārya jñāna gatānam yoginām bhāva abhāva saṃjñā pravartate sa eva eṣām ātma grāhaḥ poṣa grāhaḥ puruṣa grāhaḥ pudgala grāhaḥ syāt   api ca yadi paramārthataḥ syāt  kim api vastu sat tadā tad avaśyam nityam vā anityam vā syāt  aparāyāḥ koṭeḥ abhāvāt  tasmin vastūni nitya anityatva cintayā pravṛttā yā prajñā sā vastunaḥ  yathā svabhāva jñāna anukūla tayā samyak  prajñā eva na tu prajñāpāramitā iva prativarṇikā ata eva tathāgatena prajñāpāramitāyām yad uktam tena api virodhaḥ syāt  tathā hi  kauśika ye kula putrāḥ kula duhitāraḥ  vā yadā prajñāpāramitām upadiśanti tadā prajñāpāramitāvat eva upadiśanti tatra te prajñāpāramitā iva kurvanti yatas  hi rūpam anityam iti upadiśanti tathā eva duḥkha tām nirātmatām aśucitām ca upadiśanti evam eva vedanā saṃjñā saṃskārā vijñānam skandhā dhātava āyatanāni dhyāna apramāṇārupa anu smṛti satmyak prahāṇa arddhi pāda indriya bala bodhi aṅgāni tathāgatasya daśa bala vaiśāradya pratisaṃvid āveṇīkā buddha dharmāḥ sarva ākāra jña tā ca iti sarvam duḥkham anātmaka śucī iti upadiśanti evam eva yad ācaranti tad api prajñāpāramitāyām eva ācaranti kauśika tad  prajñāpāramitāvat eva kurvanti tatra ye prajñāpāramitāvat na kaurvanti tad katham iti ced  te itthum upadiśanti kula putrāḥ atra agacchatha prajñāpāramitā bhāvanāyam rūpam anityam iti mā anupaśyatha sarva ākāra jña tā paryantam duḥkha tām nirātmaka tām aśucitām ca mā anupapaśyatha yathaḥ hi rūpa miti svabhāvataḥ śūnyam rūpasya yaḥ  api svabhāvaḥ sa sarvathā asan yad ca asat  sā eva prajñāpāramitā tasyām nityam anityam iti na upalabhyate yatas ca yatra rūpam eva na asti tatra kutaḥ nityam anityam vāāa sarva ākāra jña tā paryatantam ittham eva evam ye hi upadiśanti te prajñāpāramitāvat na upadiśanti api tvevam upadeṣṭavyam kula putrāḥ atra agacchatha prajñāpāramitām bhāva yatha mā ca kam api dharmam samatikramatha mā ca kasmitrapi dharme tiṣṭhatha tad  kimartham iti ced  prajñāpāramitāyām na asti kaḥ  ama dharmaḥ yaḥ samatikramitavyaḥ yatra vā sthātavyam iti yatas  hi sarve dharmā svabhāvataḥ śūnyāḥ ye svabhāvataḥ śūnyatā te asantaḥ sā eva prajñāpāramitā yā ca prajñāpāramitā tasyām na kaḥ  api grāhyaḥ  heya utyādyaḥ  nirodhyaḥ ca iti yadi evam upadiśanti tadā praġyā pāramitāvat eva upadiśanti atas  sarve vastuvādinaḥ tāvat  dharma tathatām viparīta tayā nirdiśanti atas  tad nirdeśaḥ prajñāpāramitā upadeśa iva prativarṇika eva sarva dharma niḥsvabhāva tā vādinaḥ tu aviparīta tayā nirdiśanti atas  sopattikā eva ta iti bhagavatā su spaṣṭam nirdiṣṭam iti evam bhagavān tad tad sūtre anekaśas  aśeṣa dharman niḥsvabhāva tvena eva upadiṣṭavān vistara bhiyā asmābhiḥ na bahunyapitu katapayāni eva atra uddhṛtāni ata eva bhagavatā tāvat asandigdham samyak pravacana nayam avadhāayitum aśaknuvatām anaiva tāvat āgamat vara sarve dharmā niḥsvabhāva tvena sādhayitum śakyāḥ iti abhidadhatām pratividhānam anuṣṭhitam tatra yadi alpam ati tayā evaṃvidham gambhīra dharma tām na adhimoktum pārayanti tathā api sa vikalpam ātmanaḥ  manda prajñatva daḥ samavalokayadbhiḥ tad parityāgaḥ  na eva yujyate ātmānam vināśya pareṣām api mahā artha viraham kṛtvā praṇāśaḥ  na eva samīcīnaḥ evam hi sati sva para droha eva sa syāt  atas  prajñāvantaḥ śraddhāvantaḥ ca gambhiḥ adharma parityāda gṛṣṭim parivarjya bhagavantam pramāṇīkṛtya ātmanaḥ  ajñāna doṣa kāraṇāt tad aparijñānam sambhāvyata iti vicārya gambhīra sūtreṣu śraddhām utpādya śravaṇa cintā bhāvanā ādiṣu yogam kuryuḥ parān  ca api samyak  tad adhigantum avatārayeyuḥ svayam ca tad adhimoktum praṇidadhyuḥ iti ata eva ārya ratna kūṭa sūtre proktam  ye asya gambhīra dharmasya gāmbhīrya prajñayā avaboddhum aśaknuvān āste tathāgatam eva pramāṇam kurvanti anantā buddhobodhiḥ iti kṛtvā yatas ca vividha adhimokṣa anusāram tathāgatā eva dharma upadeśe pravartante atas tathāgatā eva jānanti na asmādṛśaiḥ jñātum śakyata iti vicārya tad parityāgaḥ  na eva yukta rūpaḥ  iti uvama āgama mukhena sarve dharmā niḥsvabhāvā eva iti siddhā bhavanti ye api tāvat utpatti ādi vibhāgam dvaya ābhāsinā jñānena eva kurvanti na tu sva saṃvitti mātreṇa te dvaya ābhāsasya mithyātvena tad vyavasthāpitaḥ svabhāvaḥ  api mithā eva iti abhidadhate tān adhikṛtya idānīm ucyate yadi sarva dharmāṇām utpāda ādi dharma tā mithyājñāna avabhāsita tvena vyavasthāpyate tadā katham sā parama artha satī bhavet  dvaya ābhāsaḥ  api yadi mithyā eva tadā ka tad jñāna rūpam avaśiṣyate yad  khalu parama artha sad bhavet  anyat tad  vijñānam grāhaka ākāra rahitam tad arvāc darśibhiḥ na anubhavitum yujyate sarveṣām sarva darśitva prasaṅgāt  na anumānena api niścetum śakyam tathāvidha hetoḥ eva bhāvāt  tatra na tāvat  svabhāva hetukam anumānam sambhāvyate tad svabhāvasya eva sādhya tvāt  na ca kārya hetuḥ api yatas  hi kāmam syāt tad advaya viruddham tathā api tena kārya kāraṇa bhāva eva na siddhaḥ indriya anubhava atītatatvāt na ca etad vayatiriktam anyat kāryam vidyate tathā sati bhavat matena advayam eva kāryam syāt  kintu sādhya avasthā āpanna tvāt na eva tad  pramāṇaiḥ prasidhyati yaḥ  hi dvaya ābhāsaḥ sa tāvat  śaśa śṛṅgavat na eva kāryam atas ca pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām sādhya bhūtasya kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya siddhaye parama arthe advaya jñānena gṛhyamāṇam kim api na asti anupalabdheḥ api pratiṣedha sādhana tvāt na bhavati sā sattva siddhi sādhikā yathā ucyate kaiścid  yaḥ  hi yad svabhāva viruddhaḥ sa tad svabhāva viviktaḥ yathā śīta svabhāva viruddham uṣṇa tvam śīta svabhāva viviktam tathā ca pratītiṣu abhāvaḥ  dharmī dvaya svabhāva viruddha tvāt vyāpaka viruddha upalabdheḥ na ca api hetoḥ āśraya asiddhiḥ sāamānya sukha duḥkha ākāra vedakasya dharmiṇaḥ  jñāna ākhya pratīti svabhāvena siddha tvāt  na ca svabhāvaḥ  api asiddhaḥ grāhya ākārasya eka aneka svabhāva viyogena asattve tad āśritaḥ parikalpitaḥ  grāhaka ākāraḥ  api niḥsvabhāva eva na ca api sarva abhāva prasaṅgaḥ kevalena kartu karma svabhāvena kalpita tvāt mithyā eva na eva ātmanā ātma tvam iti api yujyate yadi sāmānyena paramārtha taḥ  dvaya viviktaḥ tvam sādhayitum iṣyate tadā siddha sādhanam eva yatas  hi vayam api paramārtha taḥ  dvayasya mithyā tvāt  vivikta tvam eva abhyupagacchāmaḥ yadi hi abhāva svabhāvaḥ khalu paramārtha ta ākāra virahita vijñāna tvena sādhayitum iṣyate tadā api siddha sādhanam eva yatas  hi vayam api paramārthataḥ sarva dharmāṇām anutpanna tvāt sarva vijñānāni tāvat  paramārtha taḥ  asiddhāni dvaya ākāra su viyuktāni iti abhyupagacchāmaḥ yadi vijñāna ākhyam dharmiṇam dvaya viyukta tvena vastu sattvena ca sādhayitum iṣyate tadā dṛṣṭāntavayā siddha tvāt anaikāntikattvam hetoḥ bāhya artha svabhāvānām śītoṣṇī dīnām samyak asiddha tvāt  ekasmin  eva jñāne jñāna tad avabhāsayoravabhāsita tvena avirodhaḥ  api syāt atas  sādhya vikalam dṛṣṭāntam api syāt iti yadi vijñānam dvaya viyuktam sidhyati tadā tad balena svabhāva sattvam api sidhyati iti ced  durmatiḥ eṣā sambandha abhāvāt yad hi dvaya viyuktam tad avaśyam samyak  vastu sat iti kaḥ  hi atra sambandhaḥ yatas  hi yadi tad nivartate tadā anartha upasaṃhitam pramāṇam api nivartate api ca tathāvidha dṛṣṭāntaḥ  api asiddhaḥ vandhyā putra ādibhiḥ tena dvayena ca api anaikāntikaḥ tasmin dvaye na anyat  dvayam api sambhāvyate anavasthā prasaṅgāt  śīta ādi sparśa viyuktānām ūṣma ādīnām svabhāvavat  dvaya svabhāva atiriktaḥ tad viyukta svabhāva tvena siddhaḥ pratīti svabhāva bhinnaḥ tad samāna svabhāvaḥ kaścid api dharmī na asti eva dvaya ātmakasya eva pratīti svabhāva tvāt  evam hi anya vyakti nirapekṣaḥ san yaḥ ca svayam eva ātmanā abhivyajyate sa pratīti lakṣaṇaḥ kāya bhūmi parvata nadī sāgara ādayaḥ  vividha ākārā ye pugataḥ  avabhāsamānā bāhya arthāḥ te svayam eva ātmanā abhivyajyamāna tvāt  pratīti svabhāva atikrāntā eva pravartante evam api ye mithyatmanā kuleṣu gṛheṣu ca pravṛttim ācaranti teṣām sva kāya upagūḍha dayitayā pratīti svabhāva āliṅganam iva ācaraṇāt  asat dvaya samāyogaḥ  ayam dūṣita tvāt na viśvāsa yogyaḥ tathā ca dvaya svabhāva ātmakāt priyatamād viyoge sati kim iva na anyena saha samāyogaḥ syāt atas  kevalam asya eva dharmitvā avasthā na eva upapadyate phalataḥ ca āśraya asiddha eva ayam hetuḥ sautra antikāt ayaḥ  api jñānam paramārtha taḥ  dvaya svabhāvam na aṅgikurvanti aṃśa abhāvena virodhāt  atas tasya advaya svabhāva siddhyā kasya siddhiḥ bāhya arthānām api tad aviruddha tvāt  ye anyaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ bāhya arthā nirākriyanta iti bruvate teṣām jñānam api kinna tathā ye tāvat  kartṛ karma bhāva apekṣayā prajñaptatvāt mithyā eva iti kathayanti tad api anubhāva viparītam iti bhavantaḥ  api vijñānam paramārtha taḥ  advaya ākāram eva abhyupagacchanti tathā sati ye nīla ādi vividha citta ākārā bāhya artha tvena vijñāne avabhāsante te karma kartṛ vyavahāra anabhijñaiḥ kalpanā doṣa vinirmukte citte spaṣṭataḥ  anubhūtā bhaviṣyanti iti vividha vastu viśeṣa apekṣayā ta upalakṣyanta iti ced  tasya tāvat  viśeṣasya bāla paryantam na asti su spaṣṭā avabodhaḥ yadi niyata deśa kāla avasthitasya tasya ākāra rāśeḥ tathāvidha spaṣṭa avabhāsataḥ bhinna anubhavaḥ  mithyā eva iti bhavantaḥ svīrkunti tadā vimikti kāṃkṣiṇaḥ  bhavantaḥ tirobhūta dvaya svabhāva rahita ātmakam pratīti svabhāvam vivikta svabhāva tvena abhiniviśya āsaktā eva iti kim anyat  tad etad alpīyasaḥ chidrāt nirgate api vipula kāye hastini tad puccha avarodhavat cira kālam viduṣām āścarya adbhutam eva iti atas ca sva tīkṣṇa prajñā khaḍgena tām āsaktim chittvā kaścana tādātmya lakṣaṇaḥ  vā tad utpatti kṣaṇaḥ  vā sammbandhaḥ satya asatyayoḥ anyā uparihāra sthita lakṣaṇa tvāt tāḥ dārmya virodhaḥ asataḥ  api na kutaścid api utpattibhyupeyate utpattau satyām api na yugapad tādātmyena avabhāsaḥ  yujyate kārya kāraṇayoḥ kāla svabhāvābhyām bhinna tvāt  asambaddhaḥ  niyata avabhāsaḥ  api na yujyate atiprasaṅgāt  iti evam avaśyam kalpanā bhinnasya asatsvabhāva ākāra avabhāsasya svīkāraṇāt  tad lakṣaṇa anvita eva abhyupagantavyaḥ ata ubhau  api mithyā eva bhavataḥ yadi evam na syāt  katham nāma mithyā ākāra kalpanā svabhāvoyoḥ tādātmyena anubhavaḥ  jāyeta atas ca satya abhiveśa pāśam utkhātamulam kuruta bhagavatā api tāvat uktam  yaḥ  hi dharmaḥ tathāgatena abhisambuddhaḥ sa na satyam na api mṛṣā  iti tad api yuktibhiḥ api sādhayitu na eva śakyate evam katipayaiḥ pratyakṣaiḥ asarve dharmā viviktā iti jñātum aśakyatvat  vastu eva teṣām viṣaya iti abhidadhānāḥ tāvat  praṣṭavyā kim sarvesām puruṣāṇām yāni pratyakṣāṇi tāni sarva dharma nairātmyam na avaboddhaum samarthāni uta ahaḥ ghana ājñana timira upahatam atiyanānām bhavadṛśānām pratyakṣāṇi na avaboddhum iti tatra prathamaḥ tāvat  pakṣaḥ  na eva yujyate pramāṇa abhāvāt  sarveṣām puruṣāṇām pratyakṣāṇi na pravartanta iti niścāyakasya pramāṇasya abhāvāt  sva ālambana nivṛtti mātram tāvat  bhrāntam eva yadi tad upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ eva asattvena sādhyate tadā yatas  hi kāraṇāt  svena anupalambhaḥ tasmin apravṛtti jñānām sarveṣām strī puru sāṇām citta santatau pravartamānā yā citta pravṛtiḥ sā tāvān na eva arvāk darśinām upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptāḥ apareṣām hi nivṛtti upalabdhiḥ api aniyatā atas  prekṣāvatām pratyakṣeṇa tad jñānam na eva bhavati iti yad uktam tad na yuktam iti atha dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā siddha sādhanam eva vayam api hi arvāc darśibhiḥ tathāvidhasya tāvat  gambhīra dharma tattvasya pratyakṣataḥ darśanam na eva manyāmahe yadi api bhavādṛśāḥ khalu tathāvidhatatva avabodhe asamarthāḥ tathā api parama yoginaḥ ye kalpaiḥ anekaiḥ aprameya puṇyak jñāna sambhāra arjanam kṛtvā anurūpa kṛtsnā upāya samanvitāḥ bhūta artha bhāvanā prakarṣa paryanta jamya jñāna prabhābhiḥ nirasta samasta āvaraṇa andhakārāḥ teṣam pratyakṣeṇa tāvat  sarva dharma nairātmya bodhaḥ  bhavati eva iti kasmātra sambhavati viṣayam amum adhikṛtya paścāt  yuktiḥ api pradarśayiṣyate vastu viṣaya kāṇi pratyakṣāṇi iti yad ucyate na eva sidhyati evam arvāc darśinām yāni pratyakṣāṇi tāni timira upahata pratyakṣavat  rupādi mithyā viṣayaka tvāt  vastu svabhāva viṣaya tvena samyak viṣaya tvena vā tāvat na eva yujyante anyathā sarveṣām khalu tattva darśitva prasaṅgaḥ buddhānām bodhisattvānām mahā yoginām ca api jñānāni na eva tāvat  vastu viṣayaka tvena prasidhyanti yasmāt na taiḥ kaścana api aviparītaḥ  vastu svabhāvaḥ paridṛṣṭaḥ ārya bodhisattva sūtra piṭake auyuktam yad uta sarve taiḥ dharmā nisvabhāvāḥ aniruddhāḥ prakṛtya upaśāntāḥ atyantam ajātāḥ atyantam abhūtāḥ atyanta parinirvṛtā eva dṛṣṭāḥ taiḥ tāvat  yena dṛṣṭam tad api anidarśanam avidarśanam ca yatas  hi tad  samyak darśanam yathāvat  yena dṛṣṭam tad api anirdarśanam avidarśanam ca yatas  hi tad  samyak darśanam yathāvat  darśanam ca iti kim punar  sarva dharmāṇām yathāvat  darśanam iti ced  tad eva yad anidarśanam iti ārya dharma saṅgītau nāma sūtre api uktam  sarva dharmāṇa adarśanam eva paramam darśanam  iti atas  pratyakṣa viṣayāṇām samyak vastu tvam na sidhyati yad hi asad bhavati vastu tad na katham api vijñānam utpādayitum kṣamam iti yad ucyate tad api na eva yujyate asmābhiḥ api tāvat  śaśaśṛṅga samebhyaḥ  avastubhyaḥ pratyakṣa jñāna utpādaḥ  na eva abhyupagabhyate tathā api mahā yoginaḥ ye marīci pratiśabda nibhān sarva dharmān yathāvat  bhāvayanti teṣu samyak artha bhāvanā balena prānta koṭika dhyāna avāptitaḥ  anuttara acintya prabhāva sampanna tayā tad pratyakṣeṣu sarva dharma nairātmya jñānam bhavati eva aśeṣa dharma nairātmsa akṣāt kāri su spaṣṭam tāvat jñānam udeti eva ata eva tad  tattva adarśanam iti abhidhīyate na tu niṣedhya svabhāvasya asattvam iti atha yad tāvat pratyakṣam tad  sa svabhāvam iti yad uktam tad  sarveṣām dharmāṇām anutpāda eka rasa tvat pratyakṣam api paramārtha taḥ  niḥsvabhāvam eva tathā api yā saṃvṛti satya āśritā pratyakṣa vyavasthā sā sarvā tāvat avyāhaya eva sarveṣām dharmāṇām paramārtha taḥ  niḥsvabhāva tve api mādhyakāḥ sarva vyavahārāṇām vyāvahārikāṇām yogi jñānānām apareṣām pṛthagjana jñānānām ārya pudgala ādīnām ye hetavaḥ tātān na eva na abhyupagacchanti kintum ye tāvat  saṃvṛtitaḥ  api ahetukāḥ te khalu vyavahārataḥ  api anutpannā eva śaśaśṛṅgavat  yad  sat  tad  paramārtha taḥ  niḥsvabhāvam api tāvat utpadyate māyā pratibinba ādivat  māyā ādīnām sarveṣām pratītyasamutpanna tve api na asti vastu tā prasaṅgaḥ sādhaka bādhaka pramāṇa bādhita tvāt  tathā eva pratītyasamutpanna tve api sarva dharmāṇām na asti vastu tā prasaṅgaḥ pramāṇa bādhita tvāta yathā eva hi mantra uṣadha ādi prabhāveṇa gaja ādi vividha māyā prādurbhāvaḥ tathā eva karma kleśa ādi prabhāveṇ sattvānām utpāda ādayaḥ prādurbhavanti yaginām tāvat  svakīya puṇya jñāna sambhāra sañcaya vaśena yogi jñāna ādi māyā prādurbhāvaḥ yatas  hi vividhaiḥ hi pratyayaiḥ sā māyā api vividhā eva avabhāsate ārya prajñāpāramitā sūtre auyuktamḥ  kaḥ cichrāvaka nirmitaḥ kaścid  pratyekabuddha nirmitaḥ kaścid  bodhisattva nirmitaḥ kaścid  tathā aganitmitaḥ kaścid  karma nirmitaḥ anena subhūte paryāyeṇa sarva dharmā nirmita utpannā iti  bāla pṛthagjanebhyaḥ tāvat  yoginām etad eva vaiśiṣṭayam yad te māyā kāra iva yathāvat māyām parijānanti na ca tathā eva tasyām abhiniviśante ārya dharma saṅgītau  api uktamḥ māyā kāraḥ  yathā kaścinirmitaḥ  mokṣam udyataḥ na ca asya nirmite saṅgaḥ  jñāta pūrvaḥ yatas  asya saḥ tri bhavam nimita prakhyam jñātvā sambodhi pāragaḥ saṃnahyate jagat hetoḥ jñāta purvam jagat  tathā yathā bāla pṛthagjana jātīya darśakeṣu utpatti ādi māyabhāsaḥ  bhavati tathā eva ye tasmin satyataḥ  abhiniviśante te viparīta abhiniveśa vaśāt   bālāḥ  iti abhidhīyante atas  saṃvṛti yoga hini yogi pratyakṣe tathā sthita tvāt teṣām śaśaśṛṅga iva atyanta abhāvaḥ  na eva bhavati ata eva pratyakṣataḥ aśeṣa dharma naiḥ ātma jñānam tāvat  sat eva avirodhaḥ  api tatas  eva iti paramārtha taḥ  niḥsvabhāva tve api yoginaḥ pṛthagjana iva vyavahāra tayā vyavasthāpayanti ārya parama artha saṃvṛti satya nirdeśa sūtre tāvat uktamḥ  paramārthataḥ  atyanta abhāvaḥ ca saṃvṛtyā ca mārgam bhāvayati iti kathanavat  ayat artha antara vivikta pākṣikena pratyakṣeṇa parigṛhya tad itara śūnya pratyakṣeṇa tāvat avabudhyate iti ādikam yad uktam tad api na eva yujyate itaretara śūnya tvāt asya nayasya na tu lakṣaṇa śūnya tvāt iti lakṣana śūnyatve u sarve dharmāḥ tāvat  paramārtha taḥ  niḥsvabhāva tvena eva abhyupagamyante yatas teṣām sva sāmānya lakṣaṇāni paramārtha taḥ  yathā vyavasthitāni tebhyaḥ tad śūnya tvāt yā hi vastūnām itaretara śūnyatā sā na eva parama arthaḥ vyavahāra satyam āśritā khalu sā iti evam anutpāda rasa eka tve api sarva dharmāṇām na eva bheda abhāvaḥ tathā api svapna ādi avastha ādivat  bāleṣu paraspara bhinnāni avabhāsante ata eva atra yathā prasiddhim artha antara vivikta grahaṇa mukhena tāvat itaretara śūnyatā vyavasthāpyate na tu parama artha tayā yatas  hi svapna māyā ādi sadṛśa vastūnām svabhāvaḥ paramārthataḥ parasparam abhinnaḥ ata eva bhagavatā abhihitam parama artham anāśrita tvena iyam sarvatas  pratikruṣṭa iti parivarjanīyā eva ārya laṅka avatāra sūtre tāvat uktamḥ  evam mahāmate itaretara śūnyatā sarva jaghanyā sā ca tvayā parivarjayitavyā  yā khalu sarva dharma lakṣaṇa śūnyatā yā ca tasyāḥ sva sāmānya kakṣaṇa vyavasthā sā upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptā api satī yogibhiḥ parama artha tayā anupalabdha ākārā eva atas  sarve dharmā nirābhāsa jñāna utpattyā jñātā bhavanti iti vyavasthāpyate ata eva ca itaretara śūnyatā bāla pṛthagjanānām parikalpa nāma śrityā eva abhihitā asambadhā eva ca eṣā sā ca ayogi pratyakṣeṇa samyak avagamye ti kathanam na eva viduṣām ruci karam yukti abhāvaḥ tatra iti yad  kathanam tad api na asti yukti saṅgatam yuktīnām tāvat  saṃvidyamāna tvāt  vidvāṃsaḥ kalpanā apoḍham abhra antam iti pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam samudīrayanti artha abhāve api bhāvanā balena arthavabhāsi su spaṣṭam jñānam utpadyāte tathā hi yathā kāma śoka bhaya unmāda ādi upahateṣu asakṛt abhāsa balena pramadā ādi avabhāsi spaṣṭam jñānam upajāyate yena te tān puras sthitan iva dṛṣṭvā sahasā vividha śarīra kampa ādibhiḥ ceṣṭamānā dṛśyante atas ca yathā ukta ta tvam bhāvayatsu tad jñanam utpatsyata eva iti sambhāvyate yad ca spaṣṭa avabhāsi jñānam tad nunam nirvikalpakam eva kalpanā vāyu prakampita kāya ākārasya sua paṣṭam anupapanna tvāt  pradīpavat  prayogaḥ ye tāvat  kecid nirantaram sādaram bhāvanām anutiṣṭhanti te bhāvanā phalam prakarṣa paryanta jam sfuṭa avabodham anubhavanti eva rāga ādi upahataiḥ pramadā ādi bhāvanāvat  yatra cira kālam nirantaram sādaram sarva dharma nairātmya bhāvanam svabhāva hetuḥ tatra pramāṇa upapanna artha visaya kamavisaṃvādakam jñānam bhavati eva vyavahāreṇa dhūma ādi liṅga janita niścayena utpanna agni ādi jñānavat yoginām khalu tad naiḥ ātma jñānam api pramāṇa upapanna artha viṣayakam iti svabhāva hetuḥ asya pramāṇa upapanna tvam paścāt  prakāśayiṣyate spaṣṭa avabhāsamānam sat  yad jñānam avisaṃvādaṇam janayati tad  pratyakṣam pramāṇam rupādi vyavahāra artham anupahata cakṣuṣām cakṣuvirjāna ādivat  sarva dharma nairātmya viṣaya kam yoginām jñānam api spaṣṭa avabhāsamānam sat  avisaṃvādakam iti svabhāva hetuḥ yadi evam sarva dharma nairātmya jñānam yuktibhiḥ su sādhyam tadā katham iva vidvāṃsaḥ tatra na pritāḥ yad api yogi jñānam tad asat iti yad ucyate tad pūrvam asmābhiḥ samyak uttaritam sarva dharmāṇām śaśaśṛṅgavat atyanta abhāvasya abhāvāt  tathā api paramārthataḥ teṣām abhāva eva māyāvat  atas  na eva asmābhiḥ sarve vyavahārāḥ tāvat niṣidhyante na ca te asmābhiḥ na abhyupeyanta iti yad uktam tad tathā yaiḥ tāvat   anumānena api sarva vastuni niḥsvabhāva tvena sādhayitum aśakyāni kasya api dharminaḥ viṣayasya asiddha tvāt dṛṣṭānta ādīnām ca anutpanna tāvat  sarvasām yuktīnām viṣayasya svabhāvasya ca asiddha tvāt  iā iti avamuktam tad api asambaddham eva ittham asmābhiḥ niḥsvabhāva tvena abhyupete sati yadā bhavantaḥ prasaṅgam āpādayanti tadā sa prasaṅga eva na asti yaiḥ khalu hetubhiḥ asmābhiḥ vastūnām niḥsvabhāvatā abhyupeyate tatra paramārtha taḥ  hetu dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇām asattvāt  yadi anumāna anumeya ādi sarva vyavahāra abhāva prasaṅgaḥ  asmāsu āpādyate tadā sa prasaṅga eva na bhavati iṣṭa āpatteḥ yatas  vayam api anumāna anumeya ādi sarva vyavahāra ādīnām paramārtha taḥ  apravṛtibhyupagacchāmaḥ phalataḥ katham iva tāvat tad abhāva prasaṅga āpatet iti asvīkaraṇam hi nāma prāṅga lakṣaṇam vayam tāvat  bhavadbhiḥ prayuktam dūṣṇam api paramārtha taḥ  anutpannam eva abhyupagacchāmaḥ atas  na asti kaḥ  api doṣa avasara leśaḥ ata eva ācārya pādaiḥ yadi kiṃcid upalabheyam pravartayeyam nirvartayeyam vā pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ arthaiḥ tad abhāvāt me anupālambhaḥ iti aktam yad  paramārtha taḥ  asat  tad  vyavahāre api pravartitum na śakyata iti evam yaḥ  hi prasaṅgaḥ sa prasaṅga eva na bhavati vyāpti asiddheḥ yatas  hi yena kāraṇena yasya ātma nivartanam tena tasya vyavahāra nivartanam tu na asti parama artha svabhāva vyāptam api tu tad viparyaya vyāptam iti vyavahāraḥ tu paramārtha taḥ  abhāva svabhāva eva parama artha svabhāva virāhitā api svapna āt ayaḥ  vividha vyavahāreṣu pravartamānā dṛśyante atas  sarve api tāvat  vyavahārā nirmāṇa svapna ādivat aviruddhā eva nirmitakaḥ  nirmitakam māyā puruṣa sva māyayā sṛṣṭam pratiṣedhayase yadvat  pratiṣedhaḥ  ayam tathā eva syāt  sarvatra sādhya dharmyādīnām parama artha bhūta tvāt eva anumāna ādi vyavahārāḥ pravartanta iti hetoḥ paramārtha taḥ  niḥsvabhāva tve sati na anumāna ādi vyavahārāḥ pravartsyanta iti yaḥ  hi doṣa āropyate saḥ  api tāvat  doṣa abhāva eva nirvivāda rūpa tayā sa prasaṅga tvāt  parama ārta dharmī ādibhiḥ anumāna ādi vyavahārāḥ kutra api na eva siddhāḥ tathā api loke yathā prasiddha eva dharmiṇi vyavahārā bhavanti yatas  hi pravādinaḥ  hi tattva anirṇaya artham eva anumāna ādi vyavahārān prayuñjanti yathā uktam dharma dharmi vyavasthānam bhedaḥ  abhedoḥ ca yādṛśaḥ asamīkṣita tattva arthaḥ  yathā loke pratīyate tam tathā eva samāśritya sādhya sādhana saṃsthitiḥ parama artha avatārāya vidvadbhiḥ avakalpyate punar ca yathā anudarśanam ca iyam meyamāna phala sthitiḥ kriyate vidyamānā api grāhya grāhaka saṃvidām anyathā ekasya bhāvasya nānā rupāvabhāsinaḥ satyam katham syuḥ ākārāḥ tad ekatvasya hānitaḥ idam tāvat  vyavahārika pramāṇa lakṣaṇam iti api kathyate pramāṇasya tāvat  sarvāṇi lakṣaṇāni tattva pravṛti artham eva bhavanti anyathā vyarthāni eva tāni syuḥ iti pramāṇa lakṣaṇa śāstrāṇi anadhīyānāsu gopālaka aṅganāsu evam upadeśa abhāve api dhūma ādi liṅga darśanataḥ  agni ādīnām jñānam utpadyata eva ata eva vayam api tattva praveśāya tathatā avyavahārābhyām anumāna ādi pravartanāt  doṣa rahitā eva api ca ye vyavahāreṇa anumāna ādi pravṛttau yatra anityādi vastu dharmam sat svabhāvam sādhayanti teṣām niḥsaṃśayam tatra vyavahāreṇa vastu bhūta dharma ādayaḥ syuḥ eva yatas  hi tatra tathāvidhā āśraya hīnā sādhya disthitiḥ na eva siddhā yadi tatra tathāvidha āśrayaḥ  na asti tadā sādhya niṣedhanāt  āśrayā siddhi ākhyaḥ  doṣaḥ  dīyate saḥ  api yadi yathābhūta dharmiṇaḥ  nivṛttiḥ ced tadā niḥsaṃśayam sādhya ādi dharmiṇaḥ  avinābhāvasya niṣedham karoti yatas  hi asiddhe sati hetu asiddhayā ādi doṣā dīyante svayam upakalpitānām katipaya dharmiṇām nivṛttau  api sādhaya ādeḥ kasya api niṣedhasya abhāvāt  asiddhayā ādi doṣā na eva yujyante tad abhilaṣita artha siddhau bādhā bhāvāt  ye vastu dharmam sattsvabhāvam sādhayitum na abhilaṣante api tu tad āropita dharmāṇām vyavacchesiddhi mātram vivakṣante tebhyaḥ  asiddhayā ādi doṣān āpādayitum vyavahāre api vastu bhūta dharmī na eva āvaśyakaḥ tasya tad dharma abhāvāt tad apekṣayā api tad dharmitā na upapadyate tad asiddhau  api sādhya āvinā bhāvī hetuḥ abhiṣṭa artha sādhakaḥ bādhaka abhāvāt vādinaḥ  abhīṣṭa artha siddhau prativādina upaghāta kāmanayā dharmiṇaḥ sat asat tvam anveṣayanti na tu kāmacārataḥ dharmiṇaḥ  asattva ādi carcayā api kim yadi vādinaḥ  abhiṣṭa artha hāniḥ na syāt  acodakaḥ  doṣa hīnaḥ iti api kathanam viparyaya doṣāṇu paripūrite paridhāvana mātram eva anyatra abhāvāt  ata eva sādhya dharmam tad anukūla dharmiṇam ca avagantum pakṣa lakṣaṇa velāyām eva yukti vidbhiḥ viśeṣeṇa asvadharma iti abhidhīyate evam yaḥ tāvat  sva kāryāṇi yugapad na sādhayati sa na bhavati apratihata nitya eka svabhāvaḥ vandhyā putravat paraiḥ iṣṭam ākāśa ādikam api śabda ādi kāryam na sādhyati iti vyāpaka anupalabdhi iti abhihite ayam tāvat na viruddha hetuḥ api itī kecid  sādhya sādhanayoḥ iva ākāśa ādiḥ na eva vastu bhūtaḥ svabhāva dharmī iti sādhana bhūtaḥ  ayam hetuḥ āśraya asiddha iti apare tatra api ākāśa didharmiṇām vastu tāyāḥ kṛte api atra nirākaraṇe sādhya abhāva mātram abhyupagacchatām na asti kaḥ  api doṣaḥ hetu abhāva mātreṇa ca nasti svabhāvaḥ  api asiddhaḥ vastu tāyā abhāve api dharmiṇām siddheḥ atas  vipratipatti nirākaraṇāya sva abhimata dharmī ā iva yadi bādhyate ced tadā sādhya eva tāvat niṣedhyaḥ  bhavati na tu dharma antara yuktaḥ  dharmī iti evam nirdeśa kāle sva iṣṭa pratyakṣa anumāna āpta prasiddhi dvārā niṣedham avidhāya svabhāvasya eva tāvat niṣedhaḥ sva dharmī bhavati iti atra pakṣa dharmatā avasthāyām ācāryeṇa sva dharmī kathita iti vārtikakāraḥ tathā hiḥ sarvatra vādinaḥ  dharmaḥ  yaḥ sva sādhyatayā īpsitaḥ tad dharmavati bādhā syannānya dharmeṇa dharmiṇi anyathā asya uparodhaḥ kaḥ  bādhite anyatra dharmiṇi iti vastaraḥ vipratipatti nirākaraṇa artham ca uktamḥ yathā paraiḥ anutpādya āpūrvarūpam na kha ādikam sakṛt śabda ādi ahetu tvāt iti ukte prāha dūṣakaḥ tadvat  vastu svabhāvaḥ  asan dharmī vyomādiḥ iti api na evam iṣṭasya sādhayasya bādhā kācana vidyate dvayasya api hi sādhya tve sādhya dharma uparodhi yad  bādhanam dharmiṇaḥ tatra bādhā iti etena varṇitam avaśyam ca etad avagantavyam anyathā krama yaugapadyābhyām abhivyaktena artha kriyā sāmarthya viyogena para parikalpitaḥ padārthāḥ katham iva niṣeddhum śakṣyante sat vastunaḥ tān na eva katham api niṣedhaḥ kartum pāryate āśraya asiddha doṣeṇa yadi asataḥ  api na eva kartum pāryate tadā niṣedha eva kasya api katham api kartum na eva śakyate ata eva yoga ācāraiḥ tāvat uktam viṣaya tvam na ca ekasmin  anekam api na asti aṇau na asti tad  kṣaṇikam vā api sat ca api na hi vidyate krameṇa yugapad ca api sa viruddhaḥ  bhavet iti ityādibhiḥ bāhyādi niṣedhaḥ katham iva karttum śakyaḥ syāt  tairthikaiḥ parikalpiteṣu dravya guṇa karma sāmānya ādiṣu niṣeddhum iṣyamāṇeṣu api katham tatra āśraya asiddha āt ayaḥ  doṣā na eva pravartsyante yadi prasaṅga sādhana mātreṇa eva niṣedha nātra pravartsyanta iti evam brūyāt tadā apramāṇam hi tatra prasaṅga sādhanam phalata ekāntena eṣām abhāvaḥ  vyavahāre katham siddhaḥ syāt  pramāṇa apekṣitā tvāt tasya atha pramāṇam eva prasaṅga sādhanam iti ced tadā kim iva tatra āśraya asiddha āt ayaḥ  doṣā na pravartante yuktti balena āgantu śīleṣu doṣeṣu prekṣāvadbhiḥ svatas  sva pakṣataḥ siddhiḥ na eva yuktimatī atha bāhya artha ādīn niṣeddhu kāmānām vidyata eva vastu bhūtaḥ  buddhi lakṣaṇaḥ  dharmī yatas tena eva bāhya artheṣu pradhāna ādiṣu ca utpatti niṣedhaḥ sādhayate atas  āśraya asiddha āt ayaḥ  doṣāḥ tatra na pravartanta iti ced tadā eka aneka svabhāva viyuktatva kramayā aupadya vyāpta artha kriyā sāmarthya virahita tvāt aḥ hetavaḥ tadā aprasiddha tad dharmatva dharmiṇi abhīṣṭa sādhya dharmam sādhayiṣyanti eva apakṣa dharma tve api sādhya avinābhāva mātra hetuḥ sādhya sādhane asamarthaḥ yadi evam syāt tadā cākṣuṣa tvam api śabda dharmaṇi katham anityatva sādhane aśaktam yadi te tad prasiddha tvam abhyupagacchanti tadā bāhya pradhāna ādivat  buddhiḥ eva śaktatvā eka anekatva vyāpta dharma viyukta tvat niḥsvabhāva eva tāvat  setsyati teṣām tad dharma tvāt anye api dharmā na anya siddhām bhavanti sāmarthya ādi virāhitam vastu tāvat asiddham eva anyathā yadi evam na syāt tadā tatas  bahya pradhānāt ayaḥ  na niḥsvabhāvāḥ sā ityanti niḥsvabhāva tve khalu siddhe āśraya asiddha didoṣāṇām tādavasthye api na asti sva pakṣa hāni prasaṅgaḥ buddhau tāvat  siddhe api bāhya pradhāna ādibhiḥ utpatti niṣedhe pradhāna ādīnām parikalpita svabhāva niṣedhaḥ tu asiddha eva ākāra antara tvāt tasya yadi asiddha  eva saḥ tadā para kalpitāḥ pradhānāt ayaḥ  asanta eva evaṃvidhe tāvat  dharmiṇi katham asat vyavahāraḥ  api pravarteta na khalu anyeṣu anya vyavahāra pravṛttiḥ yajyate kecana tāvat ajñāninaḥ triṣu pratisaṃkhyā nirodha asaṃskṛteṣu kasya api utpatti mattva abhāvam parama artha vastuḥ upeṇa parikalpayanti tad niṣegha sādhane ca buddheḥ tāvat  katham nāma viṣayi bhāvaḥ  bhaviṣyati yatas  hi anye vādinaḥ teṣu tayā utpattimattva abhāva dharmam na abhyupayanti atas  tad niṣeghaḥ tāvat na katham api sādhayitum śakyaḥ atha anādi kālina sva bīja paripāka pariniṣpanna bālānām buddhau vidyamānaḥ  bāhya vastu vikalpa eva dharmī tad ādhāreṇa pradhāna ādīnām niṣedhyamāna tvāt  sa paramārthataḥ svabhāva virahitaḥ  api bhrāntyā bāhyam iva pradhāna ādya bhinnam iva sarva sāmarthya śūnyam ca sarva dharma samavetam iva kalpayati tatra pradhāna ādi svarūpa niṣedhe pradhāna ādi svarūpa niṣedhaḥ tāvat  sādhya sādhana viṣayakaḥ sidhyati yatas  hi sa bālaiḥ bāhya padhāna ādi upagṛhīta vādi prativādibhiḥ api taimirikaiḥ dvi candra darśanam iva tad abhinnatayā eva vyavahriyate sa hi yadi api sarvathā buddhayā parikalpita mātra eva tathā api tad ākāratayā buddhiḥ iti evam upacaryate vastu tas  ayam na asti katham api buddhi svabhāvaḥ tad vilakṣaṇa svabhāvena  avabhāsamāna tvāt tasya atas  siddhe api tasya niḥsvabhāva tve buddhiniḥ svabhāva tāyāḥ  na asti prasaṅgaḥ yatas  hi bāhya pradhāna ādīnām tāvat niṣedhaḥ tu pramāṇaiḥ sādhyate na tu kadācid  tattva niṣedhāya hetavaḥ prayujyante vastu satām śabda ādi bāhya dharmiṇām anitya ādi dharma siddhaye te bāhya śabda ādayaḥ ta bhinnāḥ ca buddhi stha upacāra dharmiṇyeva āśrayante yatas  hi te deśa kāla ādi bhīt na avasthā niyatā bāhya śabda āt ayaḥ  vādi prativādinām buddhau sva svabhāvena na eva pratyakṣībhavanti sādhya sādhana ādi viśeṣāṇām api asambhavaḥ niraṃśa tvāt  atas  anumāna āmeya ādayaḥ sarve vyavahārā buddhi stha eva dharmiṇī āśritāḥ pravartante prakāra antara asambhavat yadi evam tadā paramārtha taḥ  niḥsvabhāva tve parikalpita dharmiṇam niḥśritya niṣedha ādi siddhayartham āśraya asiddha ādi doṣāṇām apravṛtta vapi kāmam balena asmāsu apālambhāḥ kriyante yathā hi parama artha pravṛtti artham bhavantaḥ pradhāna ādi niṣedhye parikalpita dharmiṇī eva sādhya sādhana ādīn manasikurvanti tathā eva vayam api prasiddheṣu rūpa śabda ādiṣu ye tāvat  sat asat ādi svabhāvā āropyante tad niṣedhāya bālebhyaḥ tān māyā marīci svapna pratī bimba ādi samān nirdiśāmaḥ tatra yathā āropite dharmiṇi vastutva āropaṇa niṣedhae api vādi prativādiṣu pratībhāsamāna tvāt  asat ādi doṣā na pravartante tathā eva rupādayaḥ api tāvat āgoālaṅganānām avabhāsante tad katham nāma te asiddhā bhaviṣyanti iti avabhāsaḥ  hi tad kāraṇa nivṛttyā jāyamānena satya svabhāvena tāvat nasti vyāptaḥ alīkasya api avabhāsamāna tvāt  yadi evam naḥ ced tadā sarve puruṣa astad arśinaḥ syuḥ kevalasya tattvasya eva avabhāsamāna tvāt  yathā eva hi tasmin parikalpita dharmiṇi sāmarthya śūnyatva vyāpti upanyāsena niḥsvabhāva tvam prasādhya pradhāna ādayaḥ sādhyante tathā eva asmābhiḥ api parikalpita vastuni tad  niḥsvabhāva tvam samyaktāa sādhayitum yathā uktaḥ sāmarthya abhāva ādiḥ katham na siddhaḥ syāt  prekṣāvadbhiḥ tu svīkaraṇam vicāra arham bhāva ātmaka tāyā nirṇayasya ayukta tvāt  vicara avasthāyām tu na asti eva atat s tad nirṇayaḥ  na kṛtaḥ vicāraḥ  api nirṇaya arthaka eva yatas  pramāṇādvārā siddhānta nirṇaya kāle kaḥ  api siddhāntaḥ  na abhyupagataḥ  bhavati iti atas tasmin kāle kasmin āśraya asiddhi mukhena dharmya siddhayā ādi doṣaḥ pradātum śakyate atha vādī pramāṇaiḥ tattva nirṇayam kṛtvā parebhyaḥ tad pratipādayitum pravṛtaḥ atas  sa siddhānta abhyupagamāt pūrva vartī iti manyate tadā api tāvat na ujyate sva pratīti kāle siddhāntaḥ  na abhyupagamyata iti pūrvata eva siddhāntam anabhyupagacchantaḥ  vādinaḥ svayam pramāṇataḥ tattva jñānam kurvanti taiḥ eva ca aparān api bodhayanti iti katham siddhantaḥ  abhyupagataḥ syāt  pūrvam svayam pramāṇaiḥ tattvaḥ ciyam kṛvā siddhāntena aparebhyaḥ  avabodhanam api na asti siddham apare api prekṣāvantaḥ tāvat  tad śabda mātreṇa eva pramāṇaiḥ anupapanne arthe na eva viśvasanti atas  svam irṇa yava t  aparebhyaḥ  api nirdeśa samaye tādavasthyāt  sarvatra pramāṇaiḥ eva tattva nirṇayaḥ kriyate atas  siddhāntaḥ  na abhyupagataḥ  bhavati iti ata eva katham tena dharmiṇaḥ tāvat asiddha ādayaḥ pratīpa ādi ante samyak pramāṇa balena vādinām abhīṣṭa sādhya siddhau  api asiddhānta abhyupagamāt tebhyaḥ  doṣā jāyante iti ye vadanti kim teṣām yukti antaram iti vastutas tattva vimarśa avasare siddhānta prasiddhe dharmiṇi na ke api āśrayante tathāvidhasya dharmiṇiḥ kutra api vādi prativādiṣu asiddha tvāt eva yathā bauddheṣu śabda ādayaḥ  bhautikā iti abhyupagamyante na tathā vaiśeṣika ādiṣu ākāśa guṇa tvena tasya abhyupagamāt yadi tathāvidhaḥ dharmi siddhaḥ  na syāt tadā na kaḥ  api kutra api tad sādhana artham pratvarteta yadi tathāvidhaḥ siddhaḥ tadā tad dharmom api ubhaya sammataḥ siddha eva atas  na asti vivāda avasaraḥ ata eva sarve tattva jijñāsavaḥ siddhānta viśeṣa siddham dharmiṇam apahāya āgopāla prasiddham eva tam āśritya sādhya sādhana viṣaya kam cintanam parivardhayanti atas  siddhānta āśrayaṇam kṛtyā āśraya asiddha ādi vacanam asambaddham eva vyavahāre ye aprasiddhā dharmiṇaḥ teṣu codanam idam samucitam eva asmāsu rupādayaḥ tāvat  vyavahāre api na aprasiddhāḥ  yad khalu para prasiddha pramāṇaiḥ sva pakṣaḥ sādhanīyaḥ  iti yad ucyate tad  dūṣaṇam eva tāvat na bhavati anabhyupagamāt  atas  vyavahāre vayam ubhaya siddhaiḥ hetu ādibhiḥ sādhyam sādhayāma iti evam paścāt nirdekṣyāmaḥ  sarve dharmā viviktāḥ na kena api samyak liṅgena āliṅgitā ati parokṣa tvāt   iti yad uktam tad api tāvat na eva yujyate siddhe api sādhyarmiṇi sādhya dharma samyak liṅgayoḥ paraspara āvinābhūtasya sādhya sādhana bhāvasya apravartanāt  vivāda abhāvāt ca tatra tathā api katipayeṣu dharmisu sa siddhaḥ katipayeṣu ca sandigdha  iti atas  avinā abhauva niyama nirdeśena sāmānya dharmiṇi sādhya dharmam sādhayeyuḥ iti kathanam yujyata eva tadvat atra api māyā marici svapna gandharva nagara ādi sadṛśeṣu katipayeṣu eva dharmiṣu sa sidhyati iti atas  paramārtha taḥ  niḥsvabhāva tvāt  eka aneka svabhāva ādi dharmeṣu vyāptiḥ siddhā eva api ca asmābhiḥ anyatra sa vivādeṣu rupādiṣu vyāpti dharma upadarśanena sādhita tvāt na asti doṣa iti ye kecana  kārya svabhāvābhyām hetubhyām na eva sarve dharmā niḥsvabhāvā iti sādhayitum śakyante vastu sādhana tvāt tayoḥ  iti yad  kathayanti tad api na eva yujyate paramārtha taḥ  bhāva svabhāva sādhanau  etau  iti kutra api anullikhita tvāt  yadā sādhana svarupāntar praviṣṭatva āt imau vastu sādhanau  iti ucyete tadā niḥsvabhāva tāyām api prayoga viśeṣa vaśena sādhana svabhāvau  eva atas tad sādhyāmānāyām katham na tau hetū sambhavataḥ svabhāva hetuḥ eva kārya ādi hetubhyaḥ prayoga bhedena vividha ākāreṣu prapañcitaḥ ata eva vidvadbhiḥ  pakṣa dharmaḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ  hetuḥ  iti sāmānyena hetu lakṣaṇam nirdiṣṭam atas  atra api prayoga bhedena svabhāva ādayaḥ aucitya vaśān na virudhyante paścāt api evam nirdekṣyāmaḥ tatra sarve dharmā paramārtha taḥ  anutpannā niḥsvabhāvāḥ ca tathā api imau dvau  api teṣu vyavahāra satya tvena vidyete eva atas  katham tau  ekasmin  sambhavataḥ  kevalam samyak  kārya mātreṇa svabhāva mātreṇa vā hetunā bhavitavyam  iti yad uktam tasya api kim api kāraṇam na asti yatas  hi pratibimba phalam api unumānam eva sva hetutayā ālambanīkaroti  ādarśa digataḥ pratibimbaḥ  hi tāvat anyat ekam rūpam  iti yad uktam tad api na yucyate sa pratigha tvasya ekasmin  eva viṣaye anupapanna tvāt   tad eva rūpam tathā eva ālambyate  idam api kathanam na eva samīcīnam tathāvidha viṣaya ākāra samba baddha svabhāvena virahita tvāt  yadi api pratibimba ādaya ādarśadi āśraya āśritā bhavanti tathā api yadi viṣaya ākāra ādi bheda anurūpa tayā ālambyeran tadā tad rūpam tathāvidham sthira svabhāvam na asti eva anya ākāra grahanam api tāvat na eva yujyate atiprasaṅgāt  avijñānasya eva pratibimba ākāra tayā pratibhāsanāt asti sa ākāraḥ vijñāsvabhāvena vastusan idi yad uktam tad api na yukti yuktam yatas  hi amūrtam nīla ādi vijñānam niraṃśa tayā sthitam vividha ākāra rahitam eva bhavati iti ucyate pratibimba vastu tad vilakṣaṇa tayā pratibhāsata iti atas  katham sa ākāraḥ tad svabhāvena san syāt  yathā uktam bhavatā api triṃśikāyām pudgala niḥsvabhāvatam pratipādayatā yad  yaḥ  hi parikalpitaḥ svabhāvaḥ sa sarvathā nithyā eva vandhyā putra ādivat  ātma ādayaḥ parikalpita svabhāvā eva ityādibhiḥ prayogaiḥ svabhāva hetuḥ eva ucyate tathā eva anye api para parikalpita dharmā na eva ālambitā bhavanti iti katham na ucyate yathā ācāryaiḥ nirdiṣṭam tathā sarva dharma niḥsvabhāva tā sādhanāyām vyāpya anupalabdhi kṣaṇā dharmāḥ katham na uktāḥ tathā paścāt nirdekṣyāmaḥ yad khalu svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ asambhava iti uktam tad tāvat  pūrvam kṛta uttaram iti nayaḥ  ayam anyaḥ  anya śūnyatāyāḥ  iti api aśakya sādhanaḥ tadā kim iti praśne lakṣaṇa śūnyatā iyam iti viruddha upalabdhi ādayaḥ  asambhavā iti yad uktam tā ati asambaddhā eva iti yatas  hi sarve dharmā viviktāḥ katipaye ca saha viruddhā iti na sidhyanti tathā api māyākha puṣpa ādayaḥ ca sāmānyatayā niḥsvabhāvāḥ saha viruddhāḥ ca iti sidhyanti eva yadi evam na asti tadā katham bhavadbhiḥ para parikalpitā īśvara ādayaḥ  niḥsvabhāva tvena sādhayitum śakyante atas  sāmānyena niḥsvabhāva tā mātreṇa yadi vyavahāre viruddha ādayaḥ sidhyanti tatas  sarveṣām dharmāṇām paramārthataḥ sattva abhyupagame virusśa adharma ādīn upadarśaya niḥsvabhāva tvena teṣām samyak  sādhanāt  kim atra tāvat  virodha tad viruddha ādīnām vastu tāyām prasaṅgaḥ  na yukta rūpaḥ yatas  hi paramārtha taḥ  niḥsvabhāveṣu dharmeṣu bhūtarupa abhivyaktiḥ tu kutra api samyak bhāva svabhāve na utpatiṣṭhati yadi tiṣṭhet tadā viruddhāt ayaḥ  na sidhyeyuḥ atas  yadi sarve dharmā niḥsvabhāvāḥ sahānava sthāna viruddhāḥ ca sidhyanti atas tad viruddheṣu vastu tā prasaṅga iti na vaktavyam viruddha ādīnām vyavahāra siddha tvāt  na tu paramārthataḥ evam eva dīpaka ādau adṛḍha lakṣaṇe vastuni paricchinne sati dṛḍha ākāra vivikta tā eva tāvat  paricchidyate yatas  na vyavahāre vyavacchedaḥ atas pariccheda anupapattiḥ eva tatra yaḥ  yathā parichidyate yatra ca tathā paricchedaḥ  na asti sa abhāva eva tāavat  paraspara parihāra sthita lakṣaṇaḥ  viradhaḥ  vyavasthāpyate sat asatoḥ kramākramayoḥ ca virodhayoḥ api tathā eva draṣṭavyam na asti āsanne deśe agni avikala śīla sparśat iti ādi sthaleṣu sa virodhadhastāvat  saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇaḥ  vyavasthāpyate prasiddhe api tasmin virodhe dīpakādayaḥ  hi vastuḥ upeṇa atyantam anupapannāḥ māyā ādi mithyā vastuṣu api jāti vināśayoḥ avabhāsamāna tvāt  ata eva ācāryaiḥ parama artha pravṛtti artham yathā dīpaka ādiṣu nityān ityādi virodhaḥ  avabhāsate tathā eva vyavasthā kṛtā dīpakādayaḥ  bāhya artha tvena vijñāna rūpa tvena vā paramārtha taḥ  asiddhāḥ ubhayoḥ svabhāvayoḥ taiḥ eva nirākṛta tvāt  parama artha vastu svabhāvena saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇa virodhasya sākṣātkāri jñānam parama artha vastu svabhāve na kathañcid  pravartate arvāk darśinām darśana mārge apravṛta tvāt  saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇaḥ  virodhaḥ tāvat  sāṃvṛtika eva vastūnām svayam eva vinaśyamāna tvāt na anya kāraṇaiḥ yadi pratyaya antaraiḥ vināśa iti tadā na vināśa hetubhiḥ tatra kim api upakriyate pratyaya antaraiḥ kriyamāṇe api vināśe sa sva hetubhiḥ eva kriyate na anya kāraṇaiḥ iti yadyavastu tvāt  vināśasya tattvena anya tvena vā tasya vijñaptiḥ na yujyata iti cintyate tadā ātyantika tayā sa vināśa kāraṇaiḥ na kriyate niḥsvabhāva tvāt  atas  akiñcitkarā agni ādayaḥ  hi katham nāma paramārtha taḥ  viruddhāḥ setsyanti tathā api agni ādayaḥ śīta ādīn kramaśas  niḥsāmartha lakṣaṇān anityān prakarṣatamān utpādayantyata eva te hi agni ādayaḥ  viruddhā iti kevalam vyavahriyanta eva ata ācāryaiḥ virodhana yaḥ ayam iti uktaḥ  na tu virodha eva iti uktaḥ atas ca virodhaḥ  ayam vyavahāra mātra āśrita eva uktaḥ  na tu parama artha āśritaḥ agni śīta ādayaḥ ca na paramārtha taḥ  bāhya artha svabhāvāḥ sidhyanti teṣām tāvat jñāna ākāra svabhāvaḥ  api ca kalpita eva ekasmin jñāne śīta uṣṇayoḥ avabhāsaḥ sambhavati anekāni sajātīya vijñānāni yugapad na eva sambhavanti atas  śīta ādayaḥ svapna ādit mithya avabhāsa eva atas  na asti teṣu paramārtha taḥ  virodhaḥ vṛkṣa śiṃśapa ādīni vyāpya vyāpaka vastūni api vyavahāram āśritya parikalpita sāmāanya viśeṣa vyavasthayā vyavasthāpyante yatas  hi vṛkṣādayaḥ  vyāpakāḥ vastutas  sāmānya ātmakāḥ paramārthataḥ tu etad kim api na asti eva viśeṣa ādayaḥ tāvat na bāhya artha svabhāvāḥ jñāna ākārā api parama artha tayā siddha tvāt tathā api ukṣita tattvarthā vidvāṃsaḥ  gaja avalokanam iva svapna dṛṣṭa khadira ādi vividha mithyā viṣayāṇām anubhūtivat  vṛkṣa ādi vastūnām mṛṣā tvam eva āśritya tathatāyām pravṛtti artham parama artha anukūla tayā vyāpya vyāpaka ādi vyavasthām kurvate tathā eva bīja aṅkura ādīni kāraṇa kārya ādīni api saṃvṛtya āśrayeṇa eva vyavahriyante na tu parama artha sattayā bīja ādīnām paramārtha taḥ  asiddha tvāt  bitathānām api svapna ādīnām tathā eva avabhāsamāna tvāt ca jāgrat avasthāyām māyā kārya kāraṇa ādīni vitathāni api upalabhyanta eva atas tāni vyāvahārikeṇa kārya kāraṇa bhāvena vastu svabhāva tvena vyāptāni bhavanti kintu tāvatā tāni parama artha svabhāvatayā na samavatiṣṭhante yatas  hi vyāpake vidyamāne api sati vyāpyasya siddhiḥ na niyatā tathā api vastu svabhāva tvena su vyāptāni kārya kārana vastūni yadi nivatante tadā māyā ādivat  paramārthataḥ parikalpitaḥ  vastu svabhāva eva nivartate atas  virodha ādi sarvā vyavasthāḥ tattva pravṛtau samarthā bhavanti atas  eva vidvadbhiḥ tathatāyā nirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ tairthika parikalpitatāni pramāṇa ādīnī tathā tāyā ananukūla tvāt  parītya ājyāni itī sanyak pramāṇa lakṣaṇa pratipādakasya śāstrasya praṇayanam kṛtam iti ittham katipaye tairthikāḥ piṇḍa ātma ādikam mithyāvastu tattvam sisā dhayiṣayā sarvajña tā virāgitā karma phala sambandha ādīnām sāṃvṛtikīm vyavasthām nirākartum pramāṇānām viparīta lakṣaṇāni kurvanti atas  sudhiyaḥ tāvat tad niṣidhya pudgala dharma nairātmya tathatāyām praveśa anukūlām sāṃvṛtikīm karma phala sambandha ādi vya avasthām pratiṣṭhāpayitum pratyakṣa ādīnām viśuddhāni pramāṇa lakṣaṇāni viracitavantaḥ tāni api bhagavatā tathāgatena anujñātāni eva atas  vayam parama artha anukulāni viśuddha pramāṇa lakṣaṇāni eva tāvat manyāmahe atas  virodha ādi vyavahārāṇām svīkṛtiā atreṇa yaḥ  hi bhāva svabhāva abhyupagama prasaṅgaḥ sa tāvat anaikāntika eva tad abhyupagame api bhāa svabhāvasya asiddheḥ nanu evam anumānena saha sambandha prasidhi artham pratyakṣa pramāṇam yadi abhyupagamyate tadā vastunaḥ tāvat  siddhiḥ eva kalpanā apoḍha tvāt abhrānta tvāt ca pratyakṣa pramāṇasya abhrānta jñānena adhyavasitaḥ khalu vastu svabhāvaḥ katham nāma anumānena nirākartum śakyate yadi nirakriyate tadā pratyakṣam eva tāvat  bādhitam syāt  yadi tad  bādhitam syāt tadā anumānam eva tāvat na syāt  sisthitam pratyakṣa sambaddhena api unumānena pratyakṣam bādhyata iti kathanataḥ  na eva ācitam anyat yadi pratyakṣa siddhaḥ  arthaḥ  anumānena na eva bādhyate tadā prāpyasya prāptyā susthita eva tāvat  vastuvādi iti kathanam api samyak nirākṛtam eva iti iti am ācāryaiḥ tāvat pratyakṣasya dvaividhyam abhihitam yagi pratyakṣam sāmānya pratyakṣam ca tatra yad hi sādharaṇam pratyakṣam tad  parama artham adhikṛtya na asti abhrāntam anyathā sarvam yogi pratyakṣam eva syāt na ca syuḥ kecana api arvāk darśinaḥ yogi pratyakṣa atiriktam sāmānya pratyakṣam yadi api abhra antam na asti tathā api vyavahāre svapna ādivat  yathā prasiddhena arthena saha avisaṃvādāt tad abhrāntam ucyate śrāvakīyāṇi yogi pratyakṣāṇi pudgala nairātmya mātra sākṣāt kārīṇi iti atas tad avisaṃvādena pratyakṣa pramānāni na tu sarva ākāra gocara tvena iti kevalam bhagavata eva pratyakṣam sarva ākāra tattva gocaram atas tad eva tāvat aviparītam avisaṃvādakam phalataḥ yad eva sarva ākāra tattvam adhikṛtya abhra antam tad eva sarva ākāra tattva avisaṃvādāt  yathārtham abhra antam iti ata eva bhagavadbhiḥ eva tāvat  sarva dharma lakṣaṇa rahita tā parijñātā tasya sarva ākāra jñānasya na asti vastu tā prasaṅgaḥ  api sarva dharma saṃgṛhīita tvāt tasya atas tena lakṣaṇa abhāva tāyām abhisaṃbudhyate ārya prajñāpāramitāyām api  yad uta pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam sarva ākāra jñānam alakṣaṇe abhisambuddha tvāt tathāgatānām   iti yad uktam tad tathā eva vyavahāra arthaḥ tāvat  pratyakṣa gocara arthaḥ mithyā abhāsita svapna ādivat  sa yadā bālaiḥ vastutas  paramārtha tveropyate tadā sa anumāna bādhitaḥ  bhavati na tu darśana ādi vyavahāra arthaḥ bādhyate atas  yad abhra antam tad  pratyakṣam na ca anumāna bāghitam iti yaḥ ca paramārtha tvena āropaḥ sa eva bādhyate tad abhra antatva abhāvāt atas  na asti anena pratyakṣa apavāda prasaṅgaḥ arvāk darśinaḥ tāvat anumānena pratyakṣa sambaddha tve api na paramārthatva prāptā bhavanti api tu kevalam saṃvṛtau  eva tiṣṭhanti yatas  hi arvāk darśibhiḥ vāstavikaḥ parama arśa svabhāvaḥ pratyakṣa tayā pṛthak  pṛthak  na anubhūyate atas  na eva vastu svabhāvaḥ saṃvṛtim api bādhate kintu yaḥ  hi tatra sati ākāratva āropaḥ tad nirākṛtiḥ eva sādhyate phalanaḥ  vastuvādinaḥ  artha abhāve api artha abhiniveśinaḥ te katham susthitā iti ekataḥ anumānam vyavahāreṇa pratyakṣa sambaddham sat  sthitim pratnoti aparatas ca pratyakṣam kāṣṭha dvaya gharṣaṇa jatita agniḥ iva tad bādhām karoti iti bādhitam eva tad iti ced na etāvatā asmāsu aniṣṭāpattiḥ iti yathā sarve jāgatika dharmā yathāvat pravicaya agneḥ indhanāni bhavanti sa ca mithyā indhanāni bhasmīkṛtya svayam api upaśāntaḥ praśānta vikalpa lakṣaṇam uttamam nirvāṇam avabodhayati iti yad uta vijñāna agneḥ jat dharmāḥ sarva evandhanam matāḥ tān yathāvatiḥ avicayya jvālaiḥ dagdhvā upaśāmyati atas  yadi tadtva jñānam utyadyate tadā anumāna lakṣṇā kalpanā nivṛttā satī nirāśrayā api na anabhyupagatā bhavatī ata eva bhagavatā ratnakūṭe sa vikalpā api samprati avekṣaṇā nirvikalpa jñāna phala utpatteḥ kāraṇam iti matvā mahā phala abhinirvṛttaye kāṣṭha dvaya gharṣaṇa janita agneḥ dṛṣṭāntena nirdiṣṭā api ca sarva dharmāṇām niḥsvabhāvatva sādhane yadi ekaḥ  hetu bhūtaḥ  dharmaḥ  nīrdiśyate tadā nivṛti sādhakaḥ sa dharmaḥ  viruddhaḥ  jāyate yad i asan sa dharmaḥ tadā asataḥ  abhāvena asambaddha tvāt  katham hi sa abhāvam sādhayet iti yadi ubhaya ātmaka sa dharmaḥ tadā api anaikāntika eva atas  ahetukam eva niḥsvabhāva tvam iti ye pratividadhati tad api asambaddham eva yatas  hi anena tāvat  sat asat ubhaya dharmāṇām paramārthatva sādhane hetoḥ asambhavatvavā ucyate yukti jñaiḥ na tu niḥsvabhāvatā ādi sāmānya dharmāṇām lakṣaṇa sādhane sambhava tvam iti yadi tathā eva syāt tadā para parikalpitānām īśvara ādīnām api niḥsvabhāvatva sādhane katham nāma te sarve codyā na abatariṣyanti itī tad  yathā īśvara ādiṣu sāmarthya vyāpya vastutva niṣedha artham vastu svabhāve samāropam ca nisedha artham asat dharmā na bhavanti asambaddhāḥ evam eva paramārthataḥ kārya kārāṇa ādi vastu dharmeṣu vyāpaka niṣedhena samāropa niṣedham sādhayitum katham na asmāsu sādhya sādhana sambandhaḥ anyathā praśāna āt ayaḥ  aśakya niṣedha ābhaveyuḥ yatas  hi vastusati svabhāve na tathā kartum śakyate yadi asatā asambaddha tayā asāmartham tadā kutra sāmarthyam syāt  param arthataḥ  asat vastuni na bhavati kaścana sambandhaḥ  nāma yatas  hi vyāpaka niṣedhena vyāpya nivṛttiḥ tāvart nirdeśa mātram eva yathā sat vastuni dharma dharmi bhāva ādi sarvāṇi vastu jātāni kalpitāni iti vyavasthāpyante tathā asat vastuni api katham tāni na eva vyavasthāpyante api ca yadā kaḥ  api kadācid api sva lakṣaṇa tayā bhāva tvena paramārtha taḥ  na eva sidhyati tadā vastu lakṣaṇasya tathābhūta tvāt  tad abhāvaḥ  api asiddha  eva paramārthataḥ tatra sat asat ubhaya dharma tvena kasya api hetoḥ asambhavāt  atas teṣām prativādaḥ  vā parīkṣaṇam vā katham yujyeta sarveṣām vastūnām māyā ādivat  sat asat ubhaya dharma atīta tvāt sattvasya tad abhāvasya ca api hetoḥ ānukūlyena vādi prativādinoḥ yathā prasiddha tvena te prasiddhayavinā bhūtā eva uktāḥ atas teṣu dharma dharmi tvam viruddha tvam vyāpya vyāpaka tvam svabhāvaḥ kāryatva ādīni ca yathā ābhāsante tathā eva sarvā api vyavasthā aviruddhā eva kaiścid  vidvadbhiḥ yadi darśanasya asya dharma dharmi viruddha ādi ādhāreṇa prativādaḥ kriyate tadā tatra parama artha vyavahāra nayā anava bodha eva kāranam bhavati iti atas  anavamardanīyam etad iti grāhyam tad api na śabda mātreṇa sidhyati iti yad uktam tad na duṣanam anabhyupagamāt  na vayam api śabda mātreṇa śūnyatām sādhayāmaḥ na ca prasaṅga mātreṇa api tu samyak prāmāṇena eva iti iti evam yadi vastuṣu parama artha svabhāva ekaḥ  bhavati tadā prakāra dvayam eva tatra bhavet  hetu pratyaya apekṣita tvāt sarveṣām utpadyamāna svabhāvatayā anitya tvāt ca yathā atra sautra antika yoga ācārāṇām aikamatyam svabhāvena siddha tvāt āśritantarbhūtam vā tairthika parikalpa ātma ādivat  na ca nitya anityayoḥ anyā uparihāra sthita lakṣaṇa tvāt tṛtīīnā kācana gatiḥ svabhāve asmin ubhayam api prakā dvayam parama artha tayā na sambhavati sādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt  bādhaka sambhavāt ca yadi pratyakṣam anumānam vā tatra sādhaka pramāṇam tadā vastu svabhāva eva pūrvam tāvat ubhābhyām na siddhaḥ sa tu vastu svabhāvaḥ tadā eva syāt  kintu kārya kāraṇa bhāva eva tāvat  pratyakṣeṇa na paramārthataḥ siddhaḥ saḥ  api tāvat indriya pratyakṣeṇa sva saṃvedana pratyakṣeṇa vā sidhyati yatas  hi na arvāk darśinaḥ  mānasa pratyakṣam vyavaharanti na api ca tad mānasa pratyakṣam kutra api sidhyati iti tatra āmāṇyam aṅgīkriyate tatra kecid indriya pramāṇena na sidhyati iti bruvate pṛthak artha viṣayi tvena nirdiṣṭa tvāt tasya kintu kārya kārana bhūtasya tasya anya arthasya paramārtha taḥ  jñāna grāhya tvam na eva yujyate vijñāne sva pratibhāsa iva yaḥ  hi jñāna itara svabhāvaḥ  anya avabhāsaḥ pratīyate sa na eva jñānāt  anyaḥ anya an anyau hi paraspara viruddhau atas tad ākāreṇa jñānena anyasya pratītiḥ iti yad ucyate tad api na upapadyate atiprasaṅgāt  yadi evam tadā ghaṭa ādayaḥ ye anya prakārān anuvidhāya prādurbhavanti te api sarve parasparam gṛhīta svabhāvā eva yaḥ  api tad ākāraḥ tad jñāna ākāram eva iti viśeṣa abhidhāne sati api vijñāna sadṛśyena eva anya avabodhaḥ saṃjāyate na ghaṭa mātra ādinā iti evam viśeṣaḥ  na asti vijñāna svabhāva tve api teṣām sva svabhāva sthita tvāt anyeṣu akiñcitkara tvam eva yadi na asti viśeṣaḥ tadā artha kriyā arthinaḥ svatas  vastu anudhānena samprayujyate tathā api pratiniyata artha kriyā svabhāvaḥ kutra api na sidhyati atiprasaṅgāt  nāṭaya candra malla darśanavat  yugapad aneka darśanena tad vijñāneṣu api paraspara sāmyam syāt  jñāna svabhāva sāmyena ca teṣām api parasparam pratyakṣa tvam prasajyeta tad udbhūta tve sati iti viśeṣa antara upādāne api anya arthasya pratyakṣa tvena pratyatiḥ asambhavā eva yatas  hi abhyupagama mātreṇa upacarita tvāt  viśeṣaḥ  na prasidhyati iti anayat ca anya arthaḥ  yadi pratyakṣa tvena prasidhyati tadā jñāna viśeṣaḥ tāvat tad sadṛśaḥ tad udbhūtaḥ  vā sādhanīyaḥ katham jñānena anya arthaḥ  gṛhyata iti evam vicāryamāṇe anya arthaḥ  yadi pratyakṣataḥ asiddhaḥ tadā katham tāvat asiddhena svabhāva biśeṣeṇa siddhā mārga viśeṣāḥ setsyanta iti yāvat  tad vijñāna kṣaṇika tvasya api samanantara pratyaya artha anubalena upapanna tvāt  yathā jñānāni pūrva kṣaṇa sāpekṣa tayā samudbhavanti tathā janma antarāṇi api sambhavanti atas  pūrva vartinām para varti jñāna grāhyatva prasaṅgasya nivṛtiḥ duṣkara eva api ca ye tāvat avayavi ādi bāhya vastūnām pratyakṣa tvam āmananti sva siddhānta anusāram ca yathā tad darśana upacāram kurvanti tathā pratyakṣa tayā avabhāsaḥ  na asti eva kadācid api avayavinaḥ tad ākāra grāhi jñāne pratyakṣa anubhavaḥ  na bhavatī sarvadā eva pāṇi ādi aneka avayava samūha ākāra jñānam eva pratyakṣatayā anubhūyate nīla ādi vayavinaḥ  guṇeṣu sat iti ākārakam jñānam na eva anubhūyate ādhārasya apratyakṣa tve tad guṇa ādi mātrāṇām grahaṇa asambhavāt ariṣṭa nīla akṣa pīta akṣa timira ādi apahata netreṣu dūra samīpa sthita ekasmin  api vastuni vibhinnāni viṣama ākārāṇi jñānāni utpadyante atas  bāhya avaya vi viṣaya kam kalpanā jālam citte na asti eva vidyamānam tathā tve tasya pṛthak grahaṇa prasaṅgāt  atas tadātve tad svabhāva guṇa ādi utpattiḥ sarvathā asatī eva viruddha dharmāṇām api guṇānām yadi eka tvam tadā bhinna sattākānām api ekatva prasaṅgaḥ bādhaka abhāvāt  guṇa ādīnām sarveṣām dharmāṇām pratyakṣatva prasaṅgaḥ svapna ādiṣu tathā nīla ādi guvatām artha antarāṇām vidyamāna tve api nīla ādi ābhāsi jñānānām pṛthak anubhavaḥ  bhrānta evam na ca ākāra vaśena artha antara grahaṇa vyavasthā yuktimatī ye khalu paramāṇu ātma kalīā ādi arthānām pratyakṣa tvam āmanvate teṣu api tāvat  samāna doṣa tā prasaṅgaḥ niravayavānām sūkṣma padārthanām bhinna ākāreṣu jñāneṣu pṛthak anubhava abhāvāt samūha viṣayāṇi tāni jñānāni abhyupeatāni svapna ādivat ca tāni sthūla avabhāsīni anubhūtāni na samavāyi bhinnaḥ samavāyaḥ samasti na api samavāya kalpanayā tad upacāraḥ sambhavati yadi sañcita aneka vastu grahaṇāt  sthūleṣu bhrāntiḥ upajāyate tadā tadānīntana jñānasya aprāmāṇya prasaṅgaḥ bhrānta tvāt iti yadi sā sthūla bhrāntiḥ cittena upakalpitā tadā abhivyaktau anābhāsata aprasaṅgaḥ kalpanā viṣayāṇām sarvadā aspaṣṭa avabhāsanāt  yadi tāni indraya jñāna antargatāni tadā paramāṇunām sarvadā agrahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ sarvadā tad ākāra jñāna anutpatteḥ yasthūle bhrāntam tad tathāgrahaṇataḥ pūrvam api na abhra antam sidhyati ārambhe utpattau  eva sthūle bhrāntatva abhyupagamāt puratas  pramāṇaiḥ yadi pramāṇyam sidhyati tadā yā sthule bhrāntiḥ sā grahaṇa pūrvikā eva ekā sidhyati yadi na tathā sidhyati tadā sā bhrāntiḥ gṛhīta iti eva na sambhavati svapna ādiṣu anya pramāṇāni na gṛhyante tathā api sthūle bhrāntiḥ tu tatra dṛṣṭā eva atas tasyāḥ tad pūrvaka tvam na yujyate maru bhūmau laghu api vastu jātam mahat iti avalokyate tatra dūrādūra bhedena spaṣṭāṣpaṣṭa avabhāsa bhedaḥ  api na eva bhavati tasya eka vastu tvena tatra tādṛśa ākārā na eva sambhavanti iti api ca yādi ākārā yāthātathyena abhyupagamyante tadā yathā vividhānām rekhā ādīnām vistāraḥ tathā jñāna ākārāṇām api ākāravat  pṛthaktvam prasajyeta siddhānta vaividhya sthāpana artham aneka jñānānām utpādam avagacchataḥ  vijñānasya viṣayeṣu yathā prasāraḥ tathā ābhāsaḥ  asambhāva eva eka jñānena abhinna svabhāva tvāt  ākārāṇām api eka svabhāvatā prasaṅgaḥ yadi ākārāḥ bhinnāḥ tadā artha sadṛśjñānena teṣām grahaṇam na upapadyate bhinna artha tvāt tad grahaṇa artham satyām api anyāni ākāra kalpanāyām ākārāṇām anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ anyān i akāraṇām kadācid api unubhava abhāvāt yadi te alīkāḥ tadā tattva anyatva vicāraḥ  aupi asambhavī tadā anayā dṛṣṭayā tad vaśena anya artha vyavasthānam sarvathā yuktam asamyak tvāt  grāhya akāraḥ  api hi prajñā āptiḥ eva syāt  api ca yadi jñāna sādṛśayam sarva ātmanā bhavati tadā artha anusāriṇaḥ  api jñānasya ajñāna svabhāva tvam syāt  para citta abhijñasya yoginaḥ  api sarā gattva ādi prasaṅgaḥ sa rāga ādīnām para citta ādīnām parigrahaṇāt  eka deśena api na sādṛśyam yujyate ekasmin sāvayavatva prasaṅgāt  yadi viparyaye hi upacārat  kartuḥ eka deśa eva tadā sarvatra vastu sādṛśya sambhā vanayā sarvajñātṛ tvam syāt  sādṛśyam api prajñaptiḥ eva strān na tu parama artham atas  sādṛśyena jñāna itara svabhāva grahaṇam na sarvathā yujyate asambhavāt  tad sādṛśyate api na tad pratyakṣa tvena grahaṇam yujyate viṣayasya hetu tve tad anubhava kāle sāmīpya abhāvāt sāmipye api na eva tad grahaṇam ātma stha sādṛśya grahaṇa pravaṇa tvāt jñānasya aparasya artha stha ākārasya tadānīm anavabhāsāt avabhāse api tad viruddha tvam tulya parīkṣaṇīyam yadi sa eva anubhavaḥ tad artha ākāra anubhava tvena gṛhyata iti ced  kalpanā mātram eva etad  na eva tāvat mātreṇa vastunaḥ tādṛśaḥ svabhāv san atiprasaṅgāt  aagniḥ māṇavakaḥ bāhmaṇa vaṭuḥ iti kṛte api upacāre na eva tamin dāha pāka ādiḥ prayujyate ākāreṇa anya artha vyavasthāne api anumānam eva etad na eva hi tad pratyakṣam pratyetavyā artha antarāḥ sāmīpye api na jñāna ākāra vyāptā bhavanti artha antara abhāve api svapna ādiṣu tathā ākāra sambhavāt  atyanta parokṣa tvāt artha antarāṇām te artha antarāḥ tadīya jñāna ākāravantaḥ santi iti na eva sidhyati hetu tvam tāvat na kevalam sa ākāra kāryasya utpādanam nāma svakīya vijñānānām cakṣuḥ ādi dvārā bhrānta tvāt  śabda ādi jñāna antaram cakṣuḥ vijñāna utpādena śabda ādi ābhāsi cakṣuḥ vijñāna utpāda sambhavāt ca atas tāvat kālikā avabhāsi jñāanena artha antara grahaṇam na eva yujyate na api anābhāsibhiḥ teṣu bheda abhāvāt tadā yadi sāmīpyāt  vijñānena artha antara grahaṇam bhavati iti kalpyate tadā sarvāṇi api vijñānāni sarva samīpa viṣaya kāṇi syuḥ sarveṣu tad sattāyā bheda abhāvāt phalataḥ sarvaiḥ sarva darśanam syāt  śrotra ādi jñānāni api rupādi viṣaya kāṇi syuḥ sāmīpye bheda abhāvāt tadānīm tatas ca aidam nīlam pītam idam iti vibhāgaḥ  na eva syāt  kasyacanā api vibhāga viśesya anabhyupagamāt yadi abhyupagamyata iti tadā tad sādṛśyam abhyupagatam syāt  kalpanā svarūpa mātre jñāna abhinna ātmake sādṛśya atirikta tayā na kaścana api bhedaḥ  bhavituḥ mahati tad doṣāṇām abhihita tvāt  sāmīpya vaśāt jñānasya yadi na artha antarāt anubhavaḥ tadā katham iti praśne tad utpattyā eva iti vaktavyam syāt  tathāvidham abhidhānam na eva yuktam jñāna kāle viṣayasya abhāvāt  abhāva grahaṇa ayogāt sama kālika kāryaṇa bhāva āsyāyujyamāna tvāt ca kasya api evaṃvidha abhyupagama abhāvāt iti cakṣuḥ indriya ādīnām api tad hetu tvāt  grāhyatva prasaṅgaḥ tulya eka sāmagrī pratibaddhau deśa kālau  eva vijñānena gṛhyete na anyat  yadi evam parikalpyeta tadā api cakṣuḥ ādi grāhyatva prasaṅgaḥ duṣparihāraḥ viṣayatva abhāvāt eva indriyam na gṛhyata iti ced na etāvatā tad aviṣāya tvam viṣaya lakṣaṇasya satvāt  grāhya tvam api na viṣaya svabhāva itarat  atas  aviṣaya tvāt na asti tad viṣaya iti katham iva vaktum śakyate tad evam nirākāreṇa tāvat jñānena na artha antara grahaṇam yujyate na api tad anyena sa ākāreṇa jñānena vyavasthāyāḥ  eva abhāvāt yadi evam tarhi śrotra vijñānena api rupādi grahaṇam syāt  artha antarāṇām parokṣa tve na eva anya ākāraḥ  api sidhyati yasmāt artha antara grāhaka ākāra antaraḥ  api na asti tasmāt  kārya kāraṇa ātmakaḥ  api na ākāra antaraḥ sidhyati atas  paramārtha taḥ  na pratyakṣataḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhiḥ ata eva paramārthataḥ tad vivikta tad ākāra pratyakṣeṇa dveyena ca kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya vyavasāyaḥ  vidhīyate iti yad uktam tad api asiddham sa ākāra buddhayā artha antara pariccheda abhāvāt kārya kāraṇa bhāva niśrcāyaka pramāṇa abhāve sati jñāna dvaya abhāva kathane na asti kim api bādhakam anayā tāvat  yuktyā sarveṣām dharmāṇām citta mātra tā kāya pramukha tvāt  tad pratyakṣe artha antara ayoge api tad jñānam sva saṃvedana pratyakṣa gamyam eva tad api ca kārya kāraṇa bhūtam eva itiḥ kārya kārana bhā vaḥ tu pratyakṣa siddha iti ced na eva tad  yuktimat  yathā tathatā tathā anubhava abhāvāt  yathā ca anubhavaḥ tathā tathā tāyā abhāvāt  evam yadi vijñānasya grāhya grāhaka ākāra rahita tve api tasya vastu sattvam abhyupagamyate tadā tatra tathā anubhūteḥ abhāvaḥ sarvasya grāhya grāhaka ākāra jñānasya eva sarvadā anubhūteḥ yadi evam na syāt tadā sarvasya eva tathatā adarśanam syāt iti tad jñānam api yathā anubhūyate na tathā sthitam bhavati ekasmin sva rūpa dvaya virodhāt yadi bhrānta tvāt  tad tathā jñānam iti ced  kā nāma bhrāntiḥ yadi jñānam tadā na eva sā pratyakṣam abhrānta lakṣaṇa tvāt  pratyakṣasya tad tu svayam svatas  bhrāntam iti dvaya ātmake ca tad svabhāva avabhāsāda dvaya svabhāva hāni prasaṅgaḥ dvaya advayayoḥ paraspara virodhāt  artha antarasya bhrānta tve api paryanta sva saṃvedya tvāt na tena advaya jñānam yadi pratyakṣam kalpanā svabhāvam tadā na tad  sva lakṣaṇa viṣayakam kalpanāyāḥ samānya lakṣaṇa viṣaya tvāt api ca yaḥ kalpanā svabhāva ucyate tena svatas tad ātmanaḥ  abhivyaktiḥ ucyate grāhya grāhaka ākāraḥ  api svata eva abhivyajyate atas  kalpanā svabhāva eva eṣaḥ yadi sa grāhya grāhaka ākāraḥ mithyā tadā tad abhinnaḥ kalpanā svabhāvaḥ  api tathā eva mithyā tathā tve katham sa pratyakṣa pramāṇena bhāva svabhāvaḥ prasidhyet  yadi viśeṣaḥ  viśeṣyaḥ mithyā tadā kalpanā svabhāvasya sāmānyasya vastu tā asambhavinī anya vyavacchedena sāmānyam viśeṣeṣu vyavahriyate tad evam tattva jñānasya yathāvat anubhava abhāvāt na eva tasya sva saṃvedana pratyakṣa tvam yuktam sva saṃvedana pratyakṣa tve api na hi tena jñānena kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhiḥ ekātmyena kārya kāraṇa ātmakasya dvaya svabhāvasya virodhāt  apekṣā viśeṣeṇa tayoḥ svabhāvaḥ parikalpyeta tathā api artha antara tvāt apekṣāyāḥ sva saṃvedana pratyakṣa abhāve sā na eva sidhyati phalataḥ tad apekṣayā vyavasthitasya tad svabhāvasya api pratyakṣa tvam na yukti yuktam kārya ātmakasya kāraṇa ātmakasya ca svabhāvasya artha antara bhūtam jñānam api bhinnam bhinnam atas  hi ekasmin jñāne na ubhayoḥ anubhavaḥ bhinna kāla tvāt yadi ekasmin jñāne na anubhavaḥ tadā na kena api sambandha grahaṇam eka jñāna avabhāse api aidam kāraṇam kāryam ca idam iti pratyakṣe na śakyam ubhayoḥ sattā sambandha grahaṇam nirvikalpaka tvāt tasya sambandha grahaṇa abhāve na eva tāvat  kārya kāraṇa bhāva grahaṇ anyathā hi ati prasaṅgaḥ syāt  tad pṛṣṭha bhāvinā niścaya ākarṣiṇā jñānena api paramārthataḥ tad  dvayam na eva yujyate tena tad anubhavasya abhāvāt anya anubhavasya anyena niścayaḥ  api na eva śakyate kartum atiprasaṅgāt eva eka santāne eka anubhavasya prajñaptiḥ api na eva yuktimatī eka santāne prajñaptasya vastūnaḥ  hi asattvāt  bhinna santāne api paraspara anubhavasya tāvat asattvam niścāyaka jñāna kāle tāvat  kāryam kāraṇam ca api atītam atas  sva saṃvedana pratyakṣeṇa api na kārya kāraṇa abhāvaḥ prasidhyati iti yadi pratyakṣeṇa kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ  na anubhūyate katham tadā smṛti svabhāvaḥ  api utpadyeta iti ced na svapna ādiṣu artha anubhava abhāve api smṛti sambhavāt  na ca paramārthataḥ tad svabhāve artha antara anubhavaḥ sidhyati yathā uktam prāk  ittham pratyakṣeṇa tāvat na tasya kārya kāra na bhāvasya siddhiḥ na anumānena api yathā ukta nayena pratyakṣeṇa anubhūyamānasya kasyacid  dharmasya abhāvāt  atas  kaḥ tāvat  tad sava bhāva tvenam sādhyeta hetavaḥ  api sarve svabhāva asiddhā āśraya asiddhāḥ ca dṛṣṭānta dharmī api asiddhaḥ sarva viruddha tvāt tulya parīkṣaṇīya tvāt ca api ca kārya hetunā api sa vastu tvena sādhayitum na śakyate anyaḥ  anya āśraya doṣa prasakteḥ tathā hi kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhau kārya hetoḥ siddhiḥ kārya hetoḥ ca siddhauḥ karya kāraṇa bhāva siddhiḥ iti su spaṣṭam anyaḥ anya āśraya doṣaḥ dharmiṇaḥ  asiddhau ca kutas  svabhāva hetoḥ api pravṛttiḥ dharmiṇaḥ siddhau  api paramārthataḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhaye na asti eva kutra api hetovyārptiḥ sarvatra viruddha tvāt  tulya parīkṣaṇīya tvāt ca yadi kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhaye aasmin sati idam bhavatī ati ucyate tadā api etad  bhrāntam eva tad hetu kāle ca aśeṣa jagataḥ  vidyamāna tvāt  aasmin satī ati tasya kāraṇa tā na eva sarvathā sambhāvyate santatau  eva anya vyatireka sambhavāt tasyām eva kārya sattvasya hetu tvam na kṣaṇika tve yadi evam ucyate tathā api parama artha kārya kāraṇa bhāva sādhanasya eva atra avasthita tvāt na eva tad  yujyate kṣaṇikatva vyatirekeṇa paramārthataḥ santateḥ asiddha tvāt kasya api kārya kṣaṇasya sattvam kasya api karaṇa kṣaṇa sattvāt  yadi kalpyate tadā tad sama kālam sarva sattva antarga śeṣa vidyamāna kṣaṇānām api sattvam syāt  yathā tad sva hetu kṣaṇā vidyamānāḥ yadi dṛśyante na vidyamānā yadi na dṛśyante tathā eva tad hetu kṣāsam ākālam sarva sattva antargata āśeṣa kṣaṇā vidyamānā yadi dṛśyante na vidyamānā yadi na dṛśyante evam sati teṣām katham na hetu tvam api ca ayat asti tad  sat iti uktau tad śabdena yadi anyaḥ  hetu bhūtaḥ  dharmī iti evam gṛhyate tadā saḥ  api paramārthataḥ pratyakṣe na eva sidhyati yathā uktam prāk  na anumānena api dharminaḥ sattva siddhiḥ sambhāvyate sarveṣām api sattva sādhakānām hetūnām doṣatrayān atikrānta tvāt yadi dharmī tāvat asiddhaḥ tadā sataḥ  dharmasya hetu tvam na eva sambhavi na api ca asataḥ  dharmasya yaktam viruddha tvāt  ubhaya dharmaḥ tu tāvat  bhrānta eva asapakṣe api sattvāt  na etebhyaḥ  bhinnāḥ sādhana ākārāḥ yadi dharmī tāvat asiddhaḥ tadā parasya api sattvam na eva sidhyati tad apekṣita tvāt kārya siddhiḥ api tathā evasambhavinī na atra svabhāva hetunā kārya kāra na bhāva siddhiḥ na api anupalabdheḥ pratiṣedha sādhaka tvāt tāsām sarvāsām kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhiḥ tāvat  pratyakṣataḥ anupalabdha iti yad uktam tatra api unupalabdhi śabdaḥ tāvat  tad itarasya upalabdha ātmaka pratyakṣasya abhiprāyeṇa prajujyate na anumānam abhipretya yathā tad apramāṇam tathā ukta tvāt  api ca yā khalu upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ sā samupalabdhiphalā īdṛśa ūna anvayena yā karya kāraṇa bhāva siddhiḥ tatra api paramārthataḥ sandehaḥ kim tattvataḥ sat iti atas  sat  atavā adṛśyānām piśāca ādīnām samīpa varti tvāt  athavā dūredeśa sthitasya vastu antarasya samīpa vartinaḥ  balāt evaṃvidhaḥ samdehaḥ upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhyā deśa antarāt tad āgamanasya pūrvatas  vā tad sattvasya niṣedhaḥ kriyate na anya phalasya iti yadi tad  sat tadā tad sattvam yādṛcchikam syāt  dūra deśa stha candradīnām api cakṣuḥ vijñāna hetutva abhyupagamāt ye ca anye tad samartha hetavaḥ teṣām nivṛttau tad phalasya api nivṛttau vyatirekena yā tad siddhiḥ uktā sā api paramārtha taḥ  na eva sandeha vigatā piśāca ādīnām dūra deśa sthitānām api anyeṣām sattve api tad asattva sandehāt yadi tad asattvam tatra api yādṛt chika tvam sambhavati yathā mātṛ vivāha saṃskāravati deśe janma ādānam yatra ca na asti mātṛ vivāhaḥ tatra asat  tad samartha kāraṇa antarāṇi santi iti evam viśeṣa abhāvāt na syāt  sandeha iti ced  na teṣām sāma arthya viśesya asiddha tvāt avasara prāpta tvāt ca tattva siddheḥ iti kārya kāraṇayoḥ sandehe sati tad naiyatya artham yadi api tad kāraṇam samartham tathā api prajñā kṣetre viśeṣataḥ tad asiddhi vacanāni katham vidvadbhiḥ nirākriyantām anvaya vyatirekau vyatīricya vastuni tad siddhi niścāyaka hetūnām abhāvāt tatra anavasthā doṣaḥ syāt  yadi tad  sat tadā tad sattvam sādhayitum śakyate kintu sahakāri vastūnām pṛthak svabhāva iva anyebhyaḥ tad utpatti āśaṅkā katham nivarteta na api adarśana mātreṇa tad abhāva niścayaḥ  yujyate atiprasaṅgāt  na arvagdarśinām parebhya utpatti niścayasya spaṣṭam darśanam bhavati iti yadi parebhyaḥ  api tad utpattiḥ tadā na bhavet  hetu bhedāt  bheda iti ced  na tathā sati svabhāva vailakṣaṇya ādi sahakāri pratyayebhyaḥ  api anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ yadi pṛthak  tad viśeṣeṣu eva te sahakāri pratyayā upayujyante na tu kārya mātre iti ced  na paramārtha taḥ  viśeṣāṇām apṛthaktvāt  yadi tad aṃśena api kāryāṇi utpādyāni iti ced  na na ekasmin aṃśa bhedaḥ sambhavati iti yadi viśeṣasya pṛthak viśeṣe upacaryamāṇa tvāt  sa tattva anya tvābhyām cintayitum na yujyata iti vyāharantaḥ  na eva viśeṣān vyāharanti prājñaptikasya kadācid api hetauvayujyamāna tvāt  samūha mātreṇa eva tāvat utpattiḥ vibhaktiḥ ca api vidhīyate na tu ekaikena iti ced  tad api na eva yujyate na ca kāyam vyatiricya samūhaḥ  bhavati atas  ekaikaḥ samūha eva hetu tvena abhyupagamyate phalataḥ paramārthataḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhau na asti kim api pramāṇam kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya sāṃvṛtika tvāt  ata ācāryaiḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ  yathā prasiddhi siddha iti uktaḥ atas  sa na eva asti parama arthena iti abhyupeyam iti evam paramārtha taḥ  anitya svabhāvam sādhayitum na asti kim api pramāṇam para parikalpita śabdānām apramāṇa tvāt  pramāṇasya ca etad pramāṇa dvaya saṃgṛhita tvāt nitya svabhāvam api tāvat  paramārthataḥ sādhayitum na asti pramāṇam pratyakṣeṇa evam tāvat tad asiddha tvāt pūrvavat teṣām sa ākāra nirākāra jñānabhyām api grahaṇasya anupapanna tvat ātma ādi nitya vastūni api yathā sva siddhanteṣu vijñapyante tathā pratyakṣa jñāne na eva avabhāsante pratyakṣa jñāna viṣaya tve sat mātra tvena teṣām sattvam tathā sati sarvadā sattva prasaṅgaḥ na ca atra para apekṣā yujyate anādheya atiśaya tvāt  apekṣāyā ayogāt  ahetukānām ca viṣayatva anupapanna tvat tad vijñānane vijñeya svabhāva tvāt  viṣayatva upacāre api tad vijñānasya tad vnnityatva prasaṅgaḥ tasya vijñānasya vijñeya svabhāva anusaraṇāt saḥ vijñeyaḥ api tad  vijñānam anusarati anyathā tena jñeya svabhāva anusaraṇam api na kṛtam syāt  tad vijñeyasya tad apekṣita tvāt na anumānena api tad  sidhyati kena api hetunā saha tasya asambaddha tvāt atas  kārya hetuḥ tāvat asambhavī tatas  kramayā aupadyābhyām kasya api phalasya anutpādāt  apratyakṣa arthasya kim api sahakāri kāṇa tvena na parigṛhyate kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tāvat anvaya vi atirekābhyām spaṣṭam avagamyate ata ātma ādīnām sukha ādi phalena saha kutra api anvayaḥ  na sidhyati avikala kāraṇa tvena na tatas  kādācitka sukha utpatiḥ iti vyatirekaḥ  api tāvān na asti eva nitya tvāt avyatireka eva na api svabhāva hetoḥ tad sattva siddhiḥ sambhavati ādhāra dharmiṇaḥ  asiddha tvāt  tad sattā sādhaka hetoḥ pūrvavat doṣa trayān atikrānta tvāt ca ye tāvat  rupādayaḥ prasiddha dharmiṇaḥ te api paramārtha taḥ  asiddhā eva kādācitka tvāt teṣām vyavahāreṇa api nityasya apekṣā durupapāda eva anupalabdhyā api tāvat na eva tad sattva siddhiḥ pratiṣedha siddhau samartha tvāt  pratiṣedha mātram sā sādhayati iti api ca svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ api tāvat na eva sambhavinī abhāva vyavahāra sādhana paratvāt tasyāḥ indriyaiḥ agrāhya arthena saha viruddhayoḥ vyāpi vyāpaka yoḥ kārya kāraṇayoḥ ca asiddha tvāt  viruddha upalabdhiḥ api tāvat na eva sambhavinī pramāṇa dvayam atiricya na asti pramāṇa antaram iti anyatra prasādhita tvāt  phalataḥ vastu svabhāva parīkṣaṇa artham na asti kim api sādhakam pramāṇam iti atas  prekṣāvadbhiḥ paramārthataḥ sattvena sa na eva vyavaharttavyaḥ tatra tāvat ayam payogaḥ yasya parama arthaḥ sādhane nasti kim api pramāṇam kalpanā nirmita tvāt tasya tathā eva samyaktāyā grahaṇam na eva karttavyam yathāśyāmatva ādi guṇa viśiṣṭasya vandhyā putrasya iti upari uktayoḥ ubhayoḥ samyak svabhāvayoḥ prasiddhayartham na asti kim api pramāṇam vyāpaka anupalabdheḥ tāvat  pratiṣedha mātra phala tvāt prekṣāvatām sat vyavahārasya ca pramāṇa vyāpta tvāt  na asti hetoḥ asiddha tvam iti yad uktam tad  pūrvam vistareṇa vicāritam vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva anupapatteḥ kalpanā yoga prasaṅga nivṛtteḥ tu bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt na asti anaikāntika tvam api sa pakṣe sattvāt na asti hetoḥ viruddha tvam api sat asat vyavahārayoḥ pramāṇa vyāptatva abhyupagata tve bhāva siddhiḥ eva nūnam syāt  tādṛśasya khalu vyāpya vyāpaka bhāvasya kutra api anvayam vihāya vyatireka mātrena siddheḥ asambhavāt  vyatireka niścayaḥ  api na eva anvayaḥ cayam vinā sambhavati yad  sat  tad  katham asat iti tad nivṛttyā vyatirekī bhavitum śaknoti sambandha abhāvāt atas  niyatam eva pramāṇa abhivyakta anvayaḥ sadbhāva vyavahāraḥ ca svīkarttavyaḥ yadi sa svīkriyate tadā kvacid tad eva sat iti sat avyavahāra pramāṇam yad  yad  sattā anuvidhāne prasiddham tad eva asmākam vastuni prasiddham iti ced  tad na eva yujyate evam sat vyavahāra pramāṇa vyāptam api pramāṇa mātreṇa parama artha tayā naiyatyena sat viṣayi tvena na eva setsyati vyāpaka saṃnidhānena vyāpya viśeṣa niścayasya karttum aśakyatvāt  anyatra api sambhavāt ca anyathā vṛkṣeṇa api śiṃśapā ādi viśeṣā niścayeṇa jñāsyanta iti kim atena asti pratikūlam evam tāvat  vṛkṣaḥ tu aśeṣa viśeṣa sādhāraṇa tvāt na tena devala ādi viśeṣā nirṇetum śakyāḥ pramāṇam hi na eva tāvat  bhāva atikrānte aparasmin  api sambhavati ittham abhāva pravṛtta tvāt  pramāṇa hāniḥ eva syāt  sarva pramāṇāni bhāva abhivyañjakāni tad vyāpta pramāṇa bala bhāvi vyavahāra pravartakāni api pramāṇa avajñāta vastu mātre pravṛtta tvāt  vṛkṣa ādivat  kutas  sādhāraṇāni iti ced  na etad  yujyate saṃvṛtika jagat artha viṣayīṇi api pramāṇani bhavanti iti etad  bahudhā pūrvam carcitam anyathā sarva pramāṇāni parama artha eka viṣayīṇi bhaveyuḥ tatas ca sarve tattva darśinaḥ syuḥ tattva darśinām kṛte ārya mārga bhāvanāyāḥ ca api nairarthakyam vaktṛṇām api tattva viṣeye kaścana vivādaḥ  na syāt  sarveṣām tattva darśi tvāt teṣu saṃśaya abhāvāt  pramāṇa lakṣaṇa śāstrāṇām praṇayanam api nirarthakam syāt  moha nivartana phalatva ateṣām tattva jñāna artham eva taiḥ sarveṣām moha avakāśaḥ  dūrīkriyata iti lakṣaṇa kāraiḥ lakṣaṇeṣu paraspara virodhaḥ  bhinna siddhānta praveśaḥ  vā na kariṣyate tattvasya eka svabhāva tvāt atas  vyavahāra pramāṇam yad na eva parama artha viṣayi tad api vyavahāra pramāṇam sambhavati eva na eva hi sarva pramāṇāni paramārtha tvena vyāptāni aparama artha viṣayi tve api iṣṭa artha prāpaka tvena svapna ādivat  vyavahāra pramāṇam vyavasthāpyate tad viṣayeṣu aparama arthā iti saṃjñā pradāne api na asti vivādaḥ deha dhāriṇaḥ  ye vastu svabhāvasya yathāvat  parijñānena saṃsārakārātaḥ  mumukṣavaḥ teṣām avidyā viṣayebhyaḥ  vinivṛtta vabhāvā te ca viṣayāḥ samyak jñāna gocarā jāyante abhīṣṭa artha kriyā sādha kartha prāpti mātreṇa puruṣā na eva muktāḥ syuḥ sarvasya mukti prasaṅgāt  atas  avisaṃvādi jñānam pramāṇam iti yad uktam tad  pramāṇa sādhāraṇa lakṣaṇam sat vyavahāra vyāptam api tad na samyak artha viṣayi tvena sidhyati atas  katham tasmin samyak  vastu aviparīta tayā setsyati asmin bādhaka pramāṇa abhāva rupaḥ vyavahāraḥ  api sidhyati ye tāvat  paramārthataḥ sva para ubhayā hetukataḥ anutpannāḥ teṣām samyaktayā niḥsvabhāva tvāt  kha puṣpavat  yāni tāvat  svatas  vā paratas  vā aviparītayā sat vastūni tāni sarvāṇi api tathā eva atra na asti pramāṇa asiddha tvam api yatas  ye tāvat  sāṃkhya ādayaḥ te hetum satkāryam vyavasthāpayanti svata eva vastūni jāyanta iti bruvāṇā na eva yukti saṅga tāḥ na hi sat  vā asad vā vastu svatas  sva hetau niṣpadyate iti evam vastuḥ yadi ātmānam utpādayati iti niyatam eva tatra ekatarasya asiddha tvam na hi atra asiddhaḥ tāvat utpadyate tadānīm tasya asiddha tvāt eva phalataḥ kaḥ  hi nāma kasya utpādakaḥ syāt  vandhyā putra ādayaḥ khalva siddha svabhāvā na ātma svabhāvam utpādayitum kṣamāḥ svabhāvata siddhaḥ  api na eva utpādakaḥ tad ātmanā siddhaḥ  api viśeṣa abhāvāt kaḥ tāvat  kasya utpādakaḥ syāt  yaḥ tāvat  siddhaḥ sa na eva asiddha svabhāva yuktaḥ atiprasaṅgāt  upakārya upakāraka tvam tāvat utpādya utpādaka svabhāva eva vastuni yujyate yadi sa svabhāvena siddhaḥ tadā tasmin aṇu mātram api upakārya svabhāvasya abhāvāt  katham sa utpādyaḥ syāt  aviśeṣaṇīya tve api yadi utpādya tvam ahetuka tāyām upakalpyate tadā sat jñānam api tathā eva kim na parikalpyate abhinna tvāt ādhyātmika āyatana ādīni tathā eva na parikalpayitavyāni ata eva vidvadbhiḥ  abhyātmika āyatanāni na svata utpannāni sattvāt  sat jñānavat  iti asmin prasaṅge prāṅga artham aviditvā kecana prayoge asmin dṛṣṭānta asiddhim kecid ca viruddha hetu tvam nirupayanti tatra teṣām ajñānasya eva doṣaḥ iti am pareṣu paraspara virodham pratipādayiṣayā pareṣu siddhāni sat jñāna ādīni tāvat udāhriyante svatas tāvat  saṃsiddha vastuni kaḥ  api asvīkṛti prasaṅgaḥ  na eva āpāditas  sat jñānam api pareṣu na asiddham atas  dṛṣṭānta asiddhiḥ hetoḥ viruddha tvam api na staḥ nitya eka paryāya svabhāvāyāḥ sva santateḥ siddhayartham tathāvidha hetu dṛṣṭānta asiddheḥ aparatas ca paraspara apratibaddha abhidhānam tāvat abhidhāna abhilāṣa mātram eva na tu svasantateḥ vastu dharma tāyāḥ prasādhanam yadi sa siddhaḥ syāt tadā tad virodha abhidhānam ucitam tatra hetu dṛṣṭāntayoḥ aprasiddha tvāt tad abhidhānam tāvat apratibaddham eva pariniṣpanna bhāva ātmaka tve api yadi tad upakāraḥ svīkriyate tadā tad bhinnaḥ sa upakāraḥ  na svata utpadyate artha antara bhūtasya upakārasya utpanna tvāt  yadi abhinnaḥ tadā upakārasya api tathā eva siddha tvāt  sa katham iva setsyati atas  asmin  api hetu abhidhānam āvaśyakam api ca yadi kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ  ayam vṛkṣa drumavat  paryāyatayā ucyate tadā na tathā loka prasiddhiḥ iti atas  avaśyam eva asya pravṛtteḥ bhinnam kāraṇam iti su alpam api hetū parśanam āvaśyakam yadi kārya kāraṇa eka tvam abhyupagamyate tadā tad upadarśanam asambhavam yadi hetu abhivyaktau vipariṇāme vā sati phalam bhavati iti nirdiśyate tadā evam ayam pṛthagvyasthitaḥ sat hetuḥ eva na evam cintanam yujyate yatas  hi sa yadi abhivyakteḥ vipariṇāmasya vā avabhāsaḥ  niścayena tad bhinnaḥ tadā kevalāt anyasmāt utpattiḥ eva abhyupagatā syāt  yadi na asti bhinnaḥ tadā kārya kāraṇa viplava doṣaḥ prasaktaḥ syāt  ekasmin yugapad  vyakta avyakta ādi viruddha dharma yogaḥ katham iva yujyeta atas  paraspara viruddha tvāt  bheda abheda pakṣaḥ  api na eva samīcīnaḥ paraspara parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa dharmasya itara pratiṣedhaka tvāt  anyatra asiddha tvāt ca anubhaya pakṣa kalpanam api na eva yuktīmat  api ca yadi abhīṣṭe tad hetau abhīṣṭam vastu ātmanaḥ purvasvabhāvam aparityajya abhivyakta ādi avasthām prāpnoti tadā avasthā vikṛti prasaṅgaḥ phalataḥ eka pratīti apekṣa ghaṭa ādīnām avabhāsaḥ  anavabhāsaḥ ca syātām vārdhakye api balya avasthā ādayaḥ spaṣṭam pratibhāseran yadi parityajya iti pakṣaḥ tadā niraṃśa svabhāva tvāt kaścid api anvaya svabhāvaḥ  na syāt  paścāt  vyakta avasthāyām api dravya antarasya utpādāt na eva svata utpādaḥ na api kācid abhivyaktiḥ pariṇāmaḥ  vā syāt iti api ca vyaktam api anābhāsitam saditara lakṣaṇa tvāt  itarābhyām abhivyakti pariṇāmābhyām prabhāvita tvāt  parikalpitam eva na ca tad anyarupeṇa viparivartanīyam viruddha tvāt  ekam eva vastu tattva pariccheda kāle tad itara vyāvṛttyā paricchidyate anyat api itara vyāvṛttyā paricchidyate etad aviparīta tvena paricchede sati na tad  pariccheda yogyam syāt  yasya pariccheda kāle yaḥ  vicchedyaḥ  na bhavati tad abhāvaḥ tena saha paraspara parihāra sthita lakṣaṇaḥ  bhavati ye paraspara parihāra sthita lakṣaṇāḥ te ekasmin dharmiṇi na eva yuktarupāḥ yathā ekasmiḥ citte mūrtta mūrttatva viśeṣaṇāni tattva anyatvayoḥ tad sadṛśayoḥ vā katham ekasmin yogaḥ sambhavet  yadi viruddha dharmāṇām api eka tvam tadā sarveṣām eka dravya tvam prasajyeta atas ca bandhana muktyoḥ jāti maraṇayoḥ ca yaugapadyam syāt  yadi evam na asti tadā nāma mātram khalu eka tvam na asti atra kaścana vivādaḥ atas  yaḥ  hi vastu bhedaḥ prāk avasthā
